## RISK & OPPORTUNITY REGISTER ‚Äî clause 6.1 Risks & Opportunities (the FIRST register family; R18/R49; migration 0058‚Äì0059)

> The largest remaining core-ISO gap + the **FIRST "register" family** (sets the register-as-Document pattern Context 4.1 / Interested Parties 4.2 reuse). SPEC-FIRST (a register-as-Document architectural fork + a new-vs-existing-keys call = owner's). Builds on the now-complete process-scope authz arc (below): risk rows carry `process_id`, **own-id-only per R48**.

- **S-risk-4b** (the Risk & Opportunity register SPA ‚Äî the LAST slice; **with it the clause-6.1 family is COMPLETE end-to-end**) ‚Äî **the web surface the register has lacked: a register page + a hand-rolled 5√ó5-matrix SVG + a detail drawer with the risk‚ÜíCAPA spawn seam + a Home PLAN high-risk line + the `/risks` route, all row-surface-only per the ratified F-1 (the register-steward lifecycle UI stays deferred).** **What shipped (FE-only, NO migration [head stays `0059`], NO new permission key [rides `register.read`/`register.manage`/`capa.create`, catalog 102]; contract = the additive `CapaSource` `"risk"` value documented in 0059):** a new `features/risk/` dir mirroring `features/objectives/` ‚Äî (1) **`RisksRegisterPage`** = a gated **New** (`register.manage` @ the row's PROCESS via a first-readable-process probe ‚Äñ SYSTEM, **keyed on the key, never process-count**, AND the head editable), a read-only **banner** when the register is Effective, a **client-side scorecard rollup** from the live `useRisks()` rows (the WORKING view ‚Äî distinct BY DESIGN from `GET /risks/summary`'s governing read, which Home/MR/doc-13 consume; spec ¬ß3.3), the register-triage toolbar (search ¬∑ band + type filters ¬∑ sort ¬∑ keyboard ¬∑ URL-state), the `?risk=` drawer wiring; (2) **`RiskMatrix`** = a hand-rolled 5√ó5 SVG heatmap (D4 ‚Äî the `ObjectiveTrendChart`/`BandPreview` idiom), Likelihood√óSeverity, cells tinted by a v1-mirrored `bandForCell` (`matrix.ts` + a golden test pinning the backend `default_criteria` thresholds), each cell carrying its **rating** (the greyscale-safe non-colour channel) + risk count + a `<title>`, the selected cell ringed, a `role="img"` summary, a tone+glyph+range legend; (3) **`RiskDetailDrawer`** (`?risk=`, the CapaDrawer/InitiativeDrawer idiom) = score/treatment + the **risk‚ÜíCAPA spawn seam** (risks only; the one-click `POST /risks/{id}/capa`, 201 new / 200 replay, gated `capa.create` @ the row's process, **NOT** on head editability ‚Äî operational [S-risk-3]; a linked row shows the `/capa?capa=` link) + the gated **Edit** (`register.manage` + head editable); `NewRiskModal`/`EditRiskModal` (the `requireProcess` idiom; a partial PATCH sending only changed fields with null-clear); (4) **Home PLAN card** + `useHomeAsOf` = a high-risk `StatLine` from `useRiskSummary` (the GOVERNING read; `allForbidden` folds it; an honest "no published register yet" line pre-release); (5) **`/risks` route** + a **LeftRail PLAN entry**. Band/status carried by `StatusBadge` **tone + glyph + label, never colour alone** (DP-5 / WCAG 2.2 AA); the FE renders the server-graded `band`/`band_tone`/`band_rank` verbatim (no re-grade). **‚öÝ Codex was THE edge-finder AGAIN over 2 rounds (8 findings: 6 fixed + 1 declined + 1 declined-re-raise) a CLEAN diff-critic + web-test-trap-reviewer (both passed all categories) missed:** round-1 (5 fixed + 1 declined) ‚Äî the LeftRail entry gated on SYSTEM `register.read` HID the link from a PROCESS-scoped reader of a filter-not-403 page ‚Üí **ungate it (the CAPA precedent)**; a risk reclassified Risk‚ÜíOpportunity HID the linked-CAPA traceability link ‚Üí **show the link for ANY latched row, type-gate only the spawn**; the band column sorted on the global desc default ‚Üí Low-before-Critical ‚Üí **negate `band_rank`** so desc is danger-first; the drawer's `sys.can ‚Äñ proc.can` would show actions for a row in a process-DENY carved out of a SYSTEM grant ‚Üí **for a process-owned row use the effective PROCESS probe ALONE** (it folds matching SYSTEM grants + scoped DENYs; deny-wins); the read-only note said "Effective‚Ä¶start a revision" for InReview/Approved too ‚Üí **neutral copy**. round-2 (1 fixed + 1 declined-re-raise) ‚Äî the **P1**: the read-only banner instructed "Start a revision" but the SPA exposes NO risk-lifecycle POST (the F-1 steward-UI deferral) ‚Üí a released register can't be reopened for editing IN-APP ‚Üí **owner-ratified merge-as-is + corrected the banner to not instruct an unavailable action** (the in-app register-steward console is the named **S-risk-5** follow-up; reopening rides the API / a SYSTEM override in v1); the `?risk=` sync effect didn't follow the param's REMOVAL (back/forward left the drawer open) ‚Üí **key the effect on the risk param alone + sync to null** (a filter-param change must not close a local open ‚Äî +a regression test). **DECLINED (both rounds, same rationale): "probe ALL readable processes, not just the first"** ‚Äî the ratified S-capa-raise-process O(1) first-readable-process trade-off; the required picker + the server's PROCESS-scoped POST enforce is the boundary; a `useQueries` fan-out was owner-rejected (an auditor reads all org processes ‚Üí N `/me/permissions`); a future backend `can_create` signal is the clean fix if it bites. **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) a filter-not-403 page's nav entry must NOT gate on SYSTEM `can(key)` ‚Äî it hides the link from PROCESS-scoped readers (ungate, the CAPA precedent); (2) a `sys.can ‚Äñ proc.can` affordance gate bypasses deny-wins ‚Äî for a row with a known process use the EFFECTIVE PROCESS probe alone (it already folds SYSTEM grants); (3) a `?param=`-seeded drawer must sync to the param's REMOVAL (key the effect on the param, not the whole search-params, so other filters don't close a local open); (4) preserve a traceability link (the spawned CAPA) independent of a reclassifiable type gate; (5) don't write banner/empty copy that instructs an action the UI doesn't expose (here the deferred steward lifecycle). **Named residuals (not faked):** **S-risk-5** = the in-app register-steward lifecycle console (start-revision / publish / release + approval-task routing; F-1 deferral; the backend endpoints already exist); the first-readable-process probe false-negative (the ratified O(1) trade-off); a per-risk clause picker in the New/Edit modals (`clause_id` accepted by the backend, not surfaced in v1); the matrix criteria-from-server (a future `scoring_method`). **Test delta: web 1093‚Üí1120 (+27)** ‚Äî `matrix.test.ts` (3, the threshold golden mirror) ¬∑ `RiskMatrix.test.tsx` (2) ¬∑ `RisksRegisterPage.test.tsx` (11: render/scorecard/matrix, the read-only banner, gated New incl. the PROCESS-only first-readable-process probe, band danger-first sort, band/type filters, the `?risk=` deep-link + row-open, the filter-doesn't-close-a-local-drawer P3 guard, empty) ¬∑ `RiskDetailDrawer.test.tsx` (7: score/treatment, the spawn seam [unlinked‚Üíspawn‚Üílink, linked, reclassified-linked-keeps-link, opportunity-no-section, no-`capa.create`-hidden], the head-editable Edit gate) ¬∑ `EditRiskModal.test.tsx` (2: dirty gating, partial-PATCH changed-only + null-clear) ¬∑ PlanCard +2 / HomePage +1 (the risk line + `allForbidden`); **api unchanged.** Full `/check-web` green (eslint + strict tsc + build + 1120 vitest, 203 files). **diff-critic CLEAN + web-test-trap-reviewer CLEAN (both first pass); Codex 2 rounds (6 fixed, 2 declined-with-rationale, all 9 threads resolved).** **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + Codex threads resolved + owner's explicit "merge as-is" go. - **S-risk-4a** (the deferred high-risk read endpoint ‚Äî the doc-13/Home seam; the FIRST half of the FE slice, split BE-then-FE) ‚Äî **`GET /risks/summary` projects the register's GOVERNING (current Effective) frozen snapshot via the pure `summarize_register` (the S-risk-2 helper) ‚Üí `{published, total, by_band, high_risk, by_type, effectiveness}` ‚Äî the CONTROLLED read-of-record (never the live working satellite), for the doc-13 dashboard / Home PLAN tile (S-risk-4b).** **What shipped (NO migration [head stays `0059`], NO new permission key [rides the seeded `register.read`, catalog 102]; contract = the `/risks/summary` path + a `RiskRegisterSummary` schema):** (1) **`api/risk.py::risk_summary_endpoint`** ‚Äî `governing = await governing_register(session, org_id)`; returns `{"published": governing is not None, **summarize_register(governing or {"rows": []})}`. `high_risk` = the danger-tone (High ‚à™ Critical) count; `published:false` + all-zeros pre-first-release (the empty `{"rows": []}` never touches criteria ‚Äî `summarize_register` reads them only inside the per-row loop, so the all-zero shape is unit-proven). Gated **`register.read` @ SYSTEM** (the bare `require("register.read")`, org-level enforce, **403-on-deny ‚Äî NOT a per-row filter**), identical to the S-risk-2 MR consumer; mounted BEFORE `/risks/{risk_id}` (the S-pack-2 str-convertor shadow guard). (2) **openapi** ‚Äî `getRiskSummary` + `RiskRegisterSummary` (`additionalProperties:false`, the `published` wrapper + the `summarize_register` keys). **Three owner forks ratified (AskUserQuestion √ó3, all recommended options):** (F-1) **S-risk-4b scope = row surface only** (view/create/edit/treat + matrix + drawer + Home card + this endpoint), surfacing head state read-only ‚Äî the steward publish/release UI stays the named register-steward-role/UI deferral; (F-2) **a dedicated `GET /risks/summary`** (over the governing snapshot) rather than folding `high_risk` into `/risks/register`; (F-3) **split** S-risk-4 into 4a (this endpoint, tested first) ‚Üí 4b (the SPA). **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) the high-risk read is the GOVERNING read-of-record (consistent with the MR input-(e)), gated **org-level `register.read`** ‚Äî the per-process-deny-vs-org-aggregate gap is the SAME already-named, pre-existing cross-cutting deferral (every sourced summary is org-wide; not a RISK regression), NOT re-opened here; (2) `/risks/summary` must mount before `/risks/{risk_id}` ‚Äî and a no-grant **403 test alone can't catch a shadow** (a shadowed route's `get_risk_endpoint` require would ALSO 403), so the real guard is a route-RESOLUTION unit test asserting the endpoint NAME; (3) the **`published:false` branch is NOT deterministically reachable on the per-org-singleton shared integration DB** (once any test releases, `governing` is never `None` again) ‚Üí covered at the UNIT level (`test_risk_summary.py::test_empty_published_register_is_all_zeros`) + an integration `published == has_governing` invariant; (4) **importing a fixture from a sibling test module needs an `__all__` re-export** (or `# noqa: F401`) ‚Äî a test fn's parameter named `subj` SHADOWS the imported `subj`, so ruff F401 sees the import as unused and its autofix STRIPS it (breaking the fixture wiring); the `__all__` is load-bearing, not decorative. **Named residuals (not faked):** **S-risk-4b** (the SPA ‚Äî register page / 5√ó5-matrix SVG / `RiskDetailDrawer` + the risk‚ÜíCAPA spawn seam / Home PLAN card / `/risks` route + LeftRail entry); the family-completion `docs(s-risk-4)` back-prop (doc 13/15/16/18). **Test delta: +3 api unit** (`test_risk_routes.py` ‚Äî `/risks/summary` resolves to `risk_summary_endpoint` not the `{risk_id}` shadow; `/risks/register` + a real UUID also pinned) **+3 api integration** (`test_risk_summary_endpoint.py`: the strong positive + **read-of-record invariance** [publish‚Üírelease a critical treated row ‚Üí `published:true` + governing counts; then start-revision + re-score low on the live satellite ‚Üí the summary is UNCHANGED while `GET /risks` shows low]; the no-grant **403**; the deterministic `published == has_governing` invariant); **web unchanged.** ruff/format/mypy-strict clean (modulo the Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline); redocly clean; CI 11/11 green (all 4 shards). **diff-critic CLEAN; a 2-lens adversarial Workflow (authz/read-of-record ¬∑ test-determinism) returned 0 confirmed defects; Codex CLEAN (no findings, no open threads).** Also lands the **S-risk-4 FE spec + plan** (`docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-20-s-risk-4-*`). **Merge gate:** green CI + Codex clean + owner's explicit go. - **S-risk-3** (the CAPA-spawn seam ‚Äî closes the named S-risk-1b/-2 deferral) ‚Äî **one-click, idempotent "treat this risk ‚Üí spawn a CAPA": `POST /risks/{risk_id}/capa` latches `risk_opportunity.linked_capa_id` under a `FOR UPDATE` lock on the RISK row held across check-then-spawn, and creates a `source=risk` CAPA inheriting the risk's process + a band-derived severity.** **What shipped (migration `0059` = TWO additive `ALTER TYPE ‚Ä¶ ADD VALUE`s only [`capa_source` += `risk`, `event_type` += `RISK_SPAWNED_CAPA`; no new column/table ‚Äî `linked_capa_id` + its RESTRICT‚Üí`capa.id` FK already exist from 0058], NO new permission key [rides `capa.create`/`register.read`/`capa.read`, catalog 102], contract = the new endpoint + the `CapaSource` enum value):** (1) **The owner's design fork (AskUserQuestion) ‚Äî `linked_capa_id` is OPERATIONAL metadata, NOT frozen version content:** REMOVED from `lifecycle._frozen_row`, so the spawn works at ANY register head state (no editable gate, no head lock, decoupled from the publish freeze) and no governing read-of-record depends on it (the MR 9.3.2(e) summary reads treatment/effectiveness/rating/type/band, never the CAPA link) ‚Äî the objectives operational-rollup posture; the one-time byte-shape change is greenfield-safe (a single re-freeze on the next publish). (2) **`services/risk/service.py::spawn_capa_for_risk`** ‚Äî `get_risk(for_update=True)` (the existing `populate_existing` overrides the route's pre-lock identity-mapped read, the S-drift-1 trap) held across the latch check; `linked_capa_id` set ‚Üí return `(existing, created=False)`; else `build_capa(source=CapaSource.risk, process_id=row.process_id, raised_block={risk back-pointer})` + set the latch + emit `RISK_SPAWNED_CAPA` (object_type=document, keyed on the register head) + commit. Severity auto-derives from the governing-graded band via `_BAND_TO_CAPA_SEVERITY` (Critical‚ÜíCritical, High‚ÜíMajor, Medium/Low‚ÜíMinor ‚Äî only the highest risks route the CAPA's two-tier Critical approval). **R16's idempotency guard is the parent-row lock, NOT a UNIQUE** (two spawns would otherwise mint two distinct CAPA ids that never collide). Lives in `services/risk/` (owns the latch + lock + audit), importing `build_capa` from `..capa.service` ‚Äî verified cycle-safe (`services/capa`/`services/dcr` don't import `services/risk`). (3) **`api/risk.py`** ‚Äî `POST /risks/{risk_id}/capa` (mounted after `/risks/register*`; 201 new / 200 replay, returning `_capa_full` ‚Äî the complaint‚ÜíCAPA shape). **‚öÝ Codex was THE authz edge-finder AGAIN over 2 rounds (5 genuine fixes + 1 declined) a CLEAN diff-critic + migration-reviewer + a 3-lens adversarial Workflow [0 findings] ALL missed:** round-1 (3): **the replay returned a CROSS-PROCESS CAPA** ‚Äî after a risk is reassigned, the latched CAPA keeps its original process, so a caller owning only the risk's NEW process passed the `capa.create` gate but received a CAPA bound to a process they couldn't access ‚Üí re-auth on the **existing CAPA's own process**; **`risk` was usable on direct `POST /capas`** (`raise_capa` only rejected `review_output`) ‚Üí reject `risk` too (spawn-only, sets nothing/no audit); **no `register.read` before spawning** (the title/Raised block surface the risk description + the call mutates the row) ‚Üí enforce `register.read` on the locked risk. round-2 (2 fixed + 1 declined): **the replay RETURNS the CAPA's details (a read)** so the round-1 `capa.create` re-check was the wrong key ‚Üí gate the replay on **`capa.read`** over the CAPA's own process (the GET /capas/{id} authority; supersedes the round-1 re-check, also closes the cross-process disclosure); **an `opportunity` row could spawn a `source=risk` corrective CAPA** ‚Üí reject `type != risk` (422; opportunities ‚Üí improvement initiatives). **Declined (greenfield-moot):** "block Effective spawns for OLD-code-frozen registers that serialized `linked_capa_id`" ‚Äî single-org/pre-release (D1), no register was ever published under the old `_frozen_row`, and the new code's signed version never carries the field ‚Üí no live-vs-signed divergence; an Effective-block would CONTRADICT the ratified operational decision (replied-with-rationale + thread resolved). **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) the parent-row `FOR UPDATE` lock (not a UNIQUE) is the latch idempotency guard ‚Äî prove it with a 2-session concurrent-POST race test (single CAPA, {201,200}); (2) a spawn/treat endpoint that RETURNS an existing object's details must gate on the READ key of that object (capa.read), not just the create key, AND re-auth over the OBJECT's own process when the parent (risk) is reassignable; (3) an additive enum value breaks the golden enum-VALUE pin (`test_capa_fsm.py::test_capa_family_enum_values`) ‚Äî append the Python member LAST + bump the pin (the api-unit job's sole CI fail, invisible to the Windows targeted-run); (4) ruff strips just-added imports ‚Üí BODY-FIRST (hit repeatedly, incl. the unit-test imports added before the test body); (5) the per-org-singleton RSK head ‚Äî the spawn-while-Effective proof uses the `restore_register_head` teardown. **Named residuals (not faked):** the **FE (S-risk-4)** + the doc-13/Home high-risk endpoint; an optional caller-supplied severity override (auto-derived from band today); `subject.risk_rating` workflow routing (no resolver, pre-existing). **Test delta: +1 api unit** (`test_risk_register_content.py::test_frozen_row_excludes_linked_capa_id` pins the operational decision; the `test_capa_fsm` CapaSource pin UPDATED + the `test_risk_summary` frozen-row fixture trimmed) **+8 api integration** (`test_risk_capa.py`: idempotent spawn [source/severity/process/latch + RISK_SPAWNED_CAPA audit], the 2-session race [serializes to one CAPA], authz escalation [P1 owner ‚Üí 201 P1 / 403 P2+org-level], cross-process replay denial, replay-requires-`capa.read`, opportunity rejection, direct-raise risk-source rejection; `test_risk_lifecycle.py`: the spawn-while-Effective operational proof [PATCH 409s, spawn 201s]); **web unchanged.** ruff/format/mypy-strict clean (modulo the Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline); migration round-trip up‚Üîdown‚Üî`alembic check` CLEAN on PG16 (both enum values present); redocly clean; CI 11/11 green (all 4 shards). **diff-critic CLEAN; migration-reviewer CLEAN; 3-lens adversarial Workflow 0 findings; Codex 2 rounds (5 fixed, 1 declined-with-rationale, all 6 threads resolved).** **Merge gate:** green CI + Codex threads resolved + owner's explicit go (the `üí° Codex Review` body emoji flips üëÄ‚Üíüëç on approval). PR [#231](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/231), squash `668d8d3`.
- **S-risk-2** (read consumers ‚Äî the Management Review 9.3.2(e) input) ‚Äî **the FIRST downstream consumer of the register family: the MR "actions to address risks and opportunities" input now compiles the register's CONTROLLED read-of-record ‚Äî the GOVERNING (current Effective) frozen snapshot, never the live working satellite (which during UnderRevision carries the steward's unpublished edits).** **What shipped (BE-only, NO migration [head stays `0058`], NO new permission key [rides the seeded `register.read`, catalog 102], NO new endpoint, NO openapi change [the MR `source_ref` is an untyped generic object; the `input_type` enum already lists `RISK_OPPORTUNITY_ACTIONS`]):** (1) **Pure `domain/risk/summary.py`** ‚Äî `summarize_register(register)` projects a governing `{rows, criteria}` snapshot ‚Üí `{total, by_band, high_risk, by_type, effectiveness}` (mirrors `summarize_scorecard`). Each frozen row's band grades against the snapshot's **frozen per-method criteria** via `resolve_criteria(register, method)` ‚Äî never live code (R49 L2 derive-and-freeze) ‚Äî so a code-level band edit can't re-grade a published summary; `high_risk` = the danger-tone (Critical+High) count (the doc-13 high-risk set, spec ¬ß4); `effectiveness` is over **treated** rows (`treated`/`recorded`/`pending`, `recorded+pending==treated` ‚Äî the clause-9.3.2(e) "effectiveness of actions taken" metric); every leaf is a JSON primitive (survives `rfc8785.dumps` at the WORM minutes freeze). (2) **`services/mgmt_review/compile.py`** ‚Äî drops `RISK_OPPORTUNITY_ACTIONS` from `_SOURCELESS_GAPS`; adds a `_build_row` branch gated on the **owner's** `register.read` (the non-auditing `_owner_holds`, fail-closed to a no-access gap row) reading `governing_register(session, org_id)` (the prior-Effective frozen snapshot, parsing the `lifecycle._frozen_row` DICTS, never the live ORM satellite); a `None` governing (pre-first-release, no Effective version) ‚Üí a `no published register` gap row (the `PRIOR_ACTIONS`-until-a-release shape). The summary is captured AS-OF compile and **frozen into the WORM MR minutes** at submit ‚Äî so it must be the point-in-time governing view, not the mutable satellite. **Owner decisions (AskUserQuestion √ó3, all owner-confirmed recommendations):** read-of-record = the GOVERNING frozen snapshot (spec ¬ß3); the summary = bands + high-risk + effectiveness-over-treated; the doc-13/Home high-risk **endpoint deferred to S-risk-4** (the pure `summarize_register` helper is the reusable seam, ready). **‚öÝ Codex P2 (the authz edge-finder, 1 round, owner-decided):** the MR summary gates on the owner's SYSTEM `register.read` and counts ALL governing rows, whereas the live `GET /risks` per-row filters by `_risk_scope(row.process_id)` ‚Äî so a SYSTEM-allow **+** PROCESS-deny owner would see a denied process's rows in the MR aggregate. **Verified pre-existing + systemic, NOT introduced:** every sourced MR input gates on the owner's SYSTEM grant and summarizes the **org-wide** set (the F3 design); the identical property already exists for `NONCONFORMITIES_CAPA` (`GET /capas` per-row filters via `_readable_capas`, yet the MR uses `list_capas(org_id)`); and the triggering grant (SYSTEM allow + PROCESS deny on a `*.read` key) is **not minted by any seeded v1 role** (`_matches_scope`: a PROCESS deny doesn't match a SYSTEM resource). Owner's call: **keep the org-wide summary** for consistency (per-row filtering RISK alone would diverge from the 5 siblings) + record a **named cross-cutting follow-up** (should MR sourced summaries honor per-process denies across ALL inputs) rather than a RISK-only divergence; reply-with-rationale + thread resolved. **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) a controlled consumer reads the GOVERNING frozen snapshot (`governing_register`'s DICTS), never the live satellite ‚Äî the live satellite carries unpublished UnderRevision edits, and the MR minutes WORM-freeze the summary; (2) the summary helper must keep every leaf a JSON primitive (the `rfc8785.dumps` minutes freeze); (3) **ruff strips just-added imports ‚Üí body-first** (hit twice this slice: the `compile.py` `summarize_register`/`governing_register` imports AND the `test_risk_lifecycle` `_MR_KEYS`/`_create_review` import were both stripped by the format hook when added before the body used them ‚Äî re-add AFTER the body lands); (4) the shared per-org-singleton RSK head ‚Äî the new MR read-of-record integration test publishes a register, so it normalizes-at-start + uses the `restore_register_head` teardown (non-polluting), and the existing fully-granted MR compile test deliberately WITHHOLDS `register.read` so `RISK_OPPORTUNITY_ACTIONS` gap-rows deterministically regardless of sibling publishes (governing persists once any test releases). **Named residuals (not faked):** the cross-cutting "MR sourced summaries honor per-process denies" decision (Codex P2, owner-deferred); the doc-13/Home high-risk **endpoint** (S-risk-4, the helper is ready); `subject.risk_rating` workflow routing (no resolver, pre-existing); **S-risk-3** (CAPA spawn); **S-risk-4** (FE register/matrix/Home). **Test delta: +6 api unit** (`test_risk_summary.py` ‚Äî band counts + high-risk, effectiveness-over-treated incl. whitespace treatment, by_type, empty register, **the L2 proof** [a custom frozen criteria beats a live-code band re-grade], the missing-criteria default fallback) **+2 api integration test fns** (`test_risk_lifecycle.py`: `test_mr_input_e_reads_governing_register` drives a critical/treated/effective risk to Effective, compiles an MR [available + summary], then re-scores the row low on the LIVE satellite under a revision and proves a fresh MR **still reads the same governing high-risk count** while `GET /risks` shows the live low band ‚Äî the read-of-record proof; `test_mr_input_e_gap_row_without_register_read` the fail-closed no-access gap row) **+1 api integration test updated** (`test_mgmt_review.py` moved `RISK_OPPORTUNITY_ACTIONS` into the sourced set + asserts the no-access gap reason); **web unchanged.** ruff/format/mypy-strict clean (modulo the Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline); CI 11/11 green (all 4 shards). **diff-critic CLEAN; a 3-lens adversarial Workflow (read-of-record ¬∑ test-pollution ¬∑ authz) returned 0 confirmed defects; - **S-risk-1b** (the controlled-document publish/freeze/release lifecycle ‚Äî closes the named S-risk-1 deferral) ‚Äî **the RSK register head becomes a true controlled Effective document: risk rows are version CONTENT, edited through FSM revisions, FROZEN (rows + per-method scoring criteria) into immutable versions at publish; the live band grades against the GOVERNING version's frozen criteria, never live code (R49 L2; the objectives derive-and-freeze precedent verbatim).** **What shipped (NO migration [head stays `0058`], NO new permission key [catalog 102]; contract = 4 new `/risks/register/*` endpoints + `RiskRegisterStatus`/`RiskRegisterPublish` schemas):** (1) **Pure `domain/risk/register_content.py`** ‚Äî `build_register({rows,criteria})` / `criteria_for_methods` / `resolve_criteria(governing, scoring_method)` / `register_needs_freeze` (mirrors `domain/objectives/commitment.py`; rows sorted by id for a reproducible WORM body; criteria a per-method map keyed by `scoring_method.value`). (2) **The content-aware WORM freeze (`services/vault/service.py`)** ‚Äî `_snapshot(risk_register=‚Ä¶)` (additive; ‚àâ `SNAPSHOT_FIELDS` ‚Üí invisible to the DCR metadata diff) + `checkin_risk_register` (the `checkin_objective_commitment` verbatim: `rfc8785.dumps` JCS ‚Üí staging-PUT `application/json` ‚Üí `finalize_worm` ‚Üí `metadata_snapshot.risk_register`; **FLUSH not commit** [publish owns the txn], `application/json` non-renderable R26, `rendition_blob_sha256` left NULL [never the mirror's controlled-copy pointer], blob-iff-bytes held). (3) **`services/risk/lifecycle.py`** ‚Äî `start_register_revision` (T7 wrapper over the vault `start_revision`) + `publish_register` (the `submit_objective_for_review` shape: head FOR-UPDATE+populate_existing ‚Üí `register_needs_freeze` ‚Üí `checkin_risk_register` ‚Üí drop the start-revision WorkingDraft [O-4] ‚Üí `submit_review` ‚Üí `instantiate_approval` ‚Üí audit ‚Üí commit ‚Üí release the edit lock); `queries.governing_register` resolves the head's Effective version's frozen `risk_register` (PRIOR Effective while UnderRevision ‚Äî R43). (4) **`api/risk.py`** ‚Äî `POST /risks/register/{start-revision,publish,release}` + `GET /risks/register` status; the `_risk` serializer grades the band via `resolve_criteria(governing, ‚Ä¶)`; the static `/risks/register*` routes mount BEFORE `/risks/{risk_id}` (S-pack-2). **Two owner decisions (AskUserQuestion):** (D-2b) **`register.manage` @ SYSTEM gates start-revision/publish** ‚Äî the QMS Owner (holds it @ SYSTEM) stewards the register, a bound Process-Owner's PROCESS grant can't publish the org head; release on **`document.release` @ SYSTEM + SoD-2** (the OBJ release posture; SYSTEM override in v1). The OBJ surface-key precedent over the spec ¬ß2's loose "document.* SYSTEM override". (D-3b) **fold the managed-doc reservation in.** **Investigated, no config needed:** `instantiate_approval` is keyed by `WorkflowSubjectType.DOCUMENT` (the `document_approval` def) ‚Äî **doc-type-agnostic** ‚Üí RSK rides the SAME lightweight Approver/QMS-Owner stage OBJ/MR ride; an empty pool ‚Üí `NEEDS_ATTENTION`. **The D-3b reservation, completed under Codex pressure ‚Äî the RSK head is now reserved from EVERY content/lifecycle mutation:** generic metadata-PATCH / distribution / document-link (both branches + the link **target** + delete other-end), clause-mapping map/unmap (RSK-only), obsoletion at the **`lifecycle.obsolete` CHOKEPOINT** (covers the generic `/obsolete` route AND a RETIRE DCR that calls `obsolete()` directly), and **DCR targeting** at `_resolve_target` (RSK-only ‚Äî closes a REVISE-DCR adopting the publish-Approved version + releasing it past the `/risks/register/release` SoD-2). The generic `/documents/{id}/release` is intentionally left open (authz-equivalent: same `document.release`+SoD-2+cutover, not a bypass). **‚öÝ THE structural lesson ‚Äî the RSK head is a per-org SINGLETON shared across the one-org integration DB**, so a lifecycle test that drives it to Effective would 409 every OTHER test's risk-create (and break `test_risk_process_scope`); there is NO runtime multi-org bootstrap ‚Üí the head-advancing test NORMALIZES the shared head to editable at the start + a **`restore_register_head` teardown fixture** returns it to UnderRevision even if the body fails mid-lifecycle (a `MissingGreenlet`-500 after `release()` had already committed the head Effective was the cascade CI shard-4 caught). **‚öÝ Codex was THE edge-finder again over 3 rounds a CLEAN diff-critic √ó2 + green CI MISSED ‚Äî 6 genuine fixes; the re-posts are STALE duplicates (the fixes present + CI-proven by the held-lock/reservation tests) ‚Üí trim-don't-chase + ask the owner, don't loop:** round-1 (1 P1 + 3 P2): **the P1 version-integrity TOCTOU** ‚Äî a concurrent `POST/PATCH /risks` row write could land AFTER publish freezes the version (row writers didn't hold publish's head lock), leaving live rows out of the SIGNED version ‚Üí `add_risk_row`/`update_risk_row` now lock the head **FOR UPDATE** (consistent row‚Üíhead order; publish locks only the head ‚Üí deadlock-free; the S-records-W discipline), proven by a 2-session held-lock-blocks test; + the link-target / clause-mapping reservations. round-2 (1 new): the RETIRE-DCR obsolete bypass ‚Üí the chokepoint. round-3 (1 new): **the empty-register publish race** ‚Äî the first `POST /risks` commits the 0-row head in `resolve_or_create_head` BEFORE taking the head FOR UPDATE to insert, so a publish that locks the head in that window freezes an EMPTY version + 409s (loses) the first risk ‚Üí `publish_register` rejects a zero-row register under the lock (closes the race + a sensible business rule). Plus the **release endpoint `MissingGreenlet`** (read status off `release()`'s `_cutover`-refreshed doc, NOT `expire_all`+re-read ‚Äî the sync `_register_status` lazy-loaded otherwise). **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) the per-org-singleton head makes lifecycle tests pollute siblings ‚Üí normalize-at-start + restore-on-teardown; (2) row writes must lock the head FOR UPDATE to serialize against the publish freeze (the version must contain EXACTLY the signed rows); (3) reserve the managed head at the SERVICE chokepoint when a path can reach it both via an endpoint AND a DCR (`lifecycle.obsolete`); (4) read post-release status off `release()`'s returned doc, never `expire_all`+re-read (sync-serializer `MissingGreenlet`); (5) **ruff strips just-added imports ‚Üí body-first** (hit repeatedly: the api/risk + dcr/service + test imports + `contextlib`); (6) Codex re-posts fixed findings as stale duplicates anchored to the same hunk ‚Äî verify the fix is present + CI-proven, resolve the thread, don't re-fix. **Named residuals (not faked):** the **FE** (`S-risk-4`); ## v1.x INCLUDE_SUBPROCESSES RECONCILE ‚Äî PROCESS-grant descendant inclusion is v1.x-deferred (R48); the whole process-scope authz arc is now COMPLETE (docs-only, no migration, head stays 0057)

- **S-include-subprocesses** (reconcile `include_subprocesses` to v1 own-id-only + a binding R48 entry) ‚Äî **the LAST named gap in the process-scope authz arc** (S-owner-assignment-1 [#209] ‚Üí `GET /processes` row-filter [#213] ‚Üí records R/W/C [#216/#217/#218] ‚Üí CAPA-raise [#220] ‚Üí **here**). docs/07 ¬ß5.1/¬ß5.3/¬ß9.1 + docs/15 ¬ß9.2 promised a `PROCESS` grant "optionally includes descendants (`include_subprocesses` flag, default true)", but the v1 PDP (`domain/authz/pdp.py` `_matches_scope`, PROCESS branch) matches PURELY on own-id intersection (`bool(scoped & resource.process_ids)`) and NEVER walks `process.parent_id` ‚Äî the flag is unimplemented anywhere; owner-assignment mints an EXPLICIT `process_ids` set, and `_document_scope`/the records resolver/search/the `GET /processes`/`/map` row-filter all match on own-id/own-link sets. **SPEC-FIRST (a binding authz-model fork ‚Üí owner's call, not a silent pick):** a 4-agent analysis Workflow (impl-surface map / adversarial 4-lens refute panel / doc-reconcile sweep / cost-alternatives) weighed IMPLEMENT vs RECONCILE; the refute panel returned `reopens_nonconverging_surface` (CRITICAL/unsafe) and the owner chose **RECONCILE-defer**. **What shipped (DOCS-ONLY, NO migration [head stays `0057`], NO new key, NO behavior change):** marked descendant inclusion **v1.x-deferred (v1 = own-id-only)** at the 4 forward-promise locations (07 ¬ß5.1 table PROCESS-row selector cell, ¬ß5.3 Processes inheritance bullet, ¬ß9.1 Diego persona bound-scope cell, 15 ¬ß9.2 scope-inheritance bullet) + a new **R48** decisions-register entry + bumped the register's OWN self-range `R1‚ÄìR47 ‚Üí R1‚ÄìR48` (the intro line + the Part-3 heading). The factual `process.parent_id` self-FK schema (docs/14, the ERD `parent/subprocess` edge) is **UNCHANGED** ‚Äî a process CAN nest; only its authz-grant inheritance is deferred. **‚öÝ WHY defer, not implement (the refute panel's CRITICAL finding):** expanding a PROCESS grant's `process_ids` to descendants at the SINGLE `gather_grants` grant-resolution chokepoint would **silently DEFEAT every per-target write re-auth guard** (`_enforce_target_process_record`, `_enforce_target_process`, the per-process `capa.create` gate) ‚Äî each re-enforces against a single LITERAL target process id that the expanded grant would now intersect, re-opening exactly the non-converging records/CAPA **write-escalation** surface S-records-W deliberately trimmed to broad-only; a faithful `default true` flip would ALSO silently widen every existing bound Process-Owner grant at once (no grant carries the flag today). **‚öÝ The better future design (if v1.x ever implements it):** a materialized **ltree ancestry column** on `process` (mirror how FOLDER achieves ZERO-walk subtree inheritance via the `folder_path` string, R6 / `pdp.py` FOLDER branch) ‚Äî its own slice (migration + backfill + reparent-rewrite + a resource-side path on EVERY `ResourceContext` builder) + its own register decision, **NOT** an on-the-fly grant-side expansion. **Verification:** the reconcile matches the proven code ‚Äî the existing `test_process_owner_list_hides_unreadable_parent_id` (`tests/integration/test_process_scope.py`) already encodes own-id-only behavior (a bound child-owner does NOT reach a resource via the parent); diff-critic CLEAN (verified PDP own-id-only, all surfaces own-id/own-link, the cited test, R48 numbering/format/truthful no-migration claim, the 4-location consistency, markdown intact). **‚öÝ Codex P3 (the one finding): an R48 add leaves the register's own self-range labels stale at `R1‚ÄìR47`** (intro + Part-3 heading) ‚Üí bumped both. **‚öÝ A push/merge RACE dropped the P3 range-fix commit from the squash** ‚Äî I pushed the fix (`7d3f401`) while the owner squash-merged the LAGGING PR head (`6e520db`); GitHub squashed the *displayed* head, so the range bump landed on the branch ref but NOT in the merged squash ‚Üí **re-applied via this finish-slice follow-up** (the lesson: after a late push, VERIFY the PR head SHA before relying on a merge ‚Äî a squash captures the registered head, not necessarily the branch tip). **Named residuals (NOT regressions; carried from the arc, none re-opened):** the v1.x descendant-inclusion itself (now bound as R48 + the ltree-ancestry future design); `init-upload` PROCESS-staging (S-records-W); Process-Owner CAPA/finding/document-evidence trimmed broad-only (S-records-W); the 2 round-6 correction-vs-link TOCTOUs (S-records-W); the CAPA-raise multi-role first-process-probe false-negative (S-capa-raise-process). **No test delta (docs-only; web/api counts unchanged).** PR [#222](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/222) squash `8ba40a8` (the reconcile) + this finish-slice docs follow-up (re-applies the lost `R1‚ÄìR48` range bump + the slice narrative).

## v1.x CAPA-RAISE PROCESS-SCOPE ‚Äî a bound Process-Owner reaches + raises a CAPA from the board (closes the named owner-assignment CAPA-raise deferral; no migration, head stays 0057)

- **S-capa-raise-process** (wire the PROCESS-scoped CAPA raise from the board + scope the board's reads per-process) ‚Äî **closes the long-deferred CAPA-Raise process-scope gap (Codex P1 on #102, named "UNBLOCKED but unwired" by S-owner-assignment-1), now exercisable because the owner-assignment binding [#209] mints a real PROCESS-scoped `capa.create` and the `GET /processes` row-filter [#213] populates the picker source.** **Scope GREW from FE-only ‚Üí BE+FE mid-review** (owner-approved) when Codex showed the FE alone couldn't reach its target persona. **What shipped (BE+FE, NO migration [head stays `0057`], NO new permission key ‚Äî rides `capa.create`/`capa.read`, catalog stays 102; contract = description text only):** **(FE)** (1) **`RaiseCapaModal`** gained an optional Process picker (`useProcesses()` from `objectives/hooks`, the `RaiseInitiativeModal` idiom; conditionally rendered when ‚â•1 process is readable) that submits `process_id` in the `CapaRaiseBody` ‚Äî a process-less raise stays byte-identical to the SYSTEM/ad-hoc CAPA; (2) a `requireProcess` prop makes the picker **required** (label "Process" + placeholder "Pick the owning process"; submit gated on a pick) for a PROCESS-only creator, since a process-less raise authorizes at SYSTEM ‚Üí 403; (3) the modal is now **conditionally mounted** (`{raiseOpen && <RaiseCapaModal ‚Ä¶/>}`, the `RaiseInitiativeModal` precedent) so close unmounts + discards the draft (a picked-then-cancelled process can't bleed into the next raise); (4) **`CapaBoardPage`** Raise button shows when the caller holds `capa.create` at **SYSTEM OR their first readable process** (`usePermissions()` SYSTEM probe `||` a `usePermissions({level:"PROCESS",id:firstProcessId})` probe; `usePermissions(undefined)` dedupes to the SYSTEM query when there are no readable processes), and passes `requireProcess={!systemCanCreate}`. **(BE ‚Äî the Codex P1 fix)** the board's own reads were SYSTEM-gated, so a *pure* bound Process-Owner 403'd `GET /capas` (`useCapas().forbidden` ‚Üí the no-access panel) and never saw the button ‚Üí applied the **S-process-scope-2 read-filter pattern** (a safe DECOUPLED read ‚Äî a CAPA's `process_id` is set by an already-re-authorized `POST /capas`): (5) `GET /capas` moved from `require("capa.read")` (SYSTEM enforce) to `get_current_user` + a new **`_readable_capas`** per-row filter (`gather_grants("capa.read")` once ‚Üí keep rows where `authorize(grants, "capa.read", _process_scope(row[0].process_id), ctx).allow`; **filter-not-403**, SYSTEM grants match every row byte-identical, `source_ip` threaded; a process-less ad-hoc CAPA needs a SYSTEM grant); (6) `GET /capas/{id}` + `/approval` moved to **`_capa_read_scoped = require("capa.read", async_scope_resolver=_capa_scope)`** (PROCESS-enforce; a SYSTEM Top-Management approver still matches; a bound owner reads their own process's CAPA; else 403). **Load-bearing decisions:** (a) **the button gate keys on `capa.create`, NEVER on "has readable processes"** ‚Äî an Internal Auditor holds SYSTEM `process.read` (a non-empty process list) + SYSTEM `capa.read` (board access) but no `capa.create` at any scope, so gating on process-count would leak the button to auditors (and regress today's behaviour); the per-process `capa.create` probe is the only correct discriminator. (b) **The button gate is O(1)** ‚Äî the owner chose `SYSTEM ‚Äñ first-readable-process probe` over a `useQueries` fan-out across ALL readable processes, specifically to avoid firing N `/me/permissions` calls for every broad-`process.read` caller (an auditor ‚Üí all org processes) on each board load; the owner-assignment binding mints `process.read` + `capa.create` over the SAME bound set, so for a single-role bound owner every readable process is a createable one (first is representative). (c) **filter-not-403 on `GET /capas`** (doc 18 ¬ß5.2, matching records/search/processes) ‚Äî a no-grant caller now gets `200`+empty (an empty board) instead of the no-access panel; the FE's defensive 403 handling is retained but effectively dead for `/capas`. **‚öÝ THE structural lesson ‚Äî the FE-only premise was incomplete: a feature cannot reach its target persona if the board's own LIST read is SYSTEM-gated.** The deferral note + the brief both fixated on the `POST /capas` write (already process-scoped) + the button, and MISSED that `GET /capas` (the board's render gate) was the real chokepoint ‚Äî Codex P1 caught it; the fix is the same read-filter S-process-scope-2 applied to `/processes`. **‚öÝ Other traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **the ruff PostToolUse hook strips just-added imports ‚Üí body-first** (hit again: `RequestContext`/`authorize`/`gather_grants` were stripped because the body using them came in a later edit). (2) **Mantine's `required` label appends an asterisk to the accessible name** (`getByLabelText("Process")` exact FAILS for a required field ‚Üí "Process *") ‚Äî query the required picker by its requireProcess-only PLACEHOLDER ("Pick the owning process"), a genuine discriminator, not the tautological `/^Process/` (which matches both labels) or an exact "(optional)" negative (always null for a required field ‚Äî the web-test-trap MAJOR was exactly this false-PASS). (3) **the board's "Ôºã Raise CAPA" open button AND the modal's "Raise CAPA" submit both match `/Raise CAPA/`** while the modal is open ‚Üí target the modal submit by EXACT `{name:"Raise CAPA"}`; and the board's Severity FILTER (`aria-label="Severity"`) clashes with the modal's Severity while open ‚Üí scope or avoid. (4) **a backend read-port that flips a list to filter-not-403 must update any PRE-EXISTING test asserting the old 403** (the diff-critic CRITICAL: `test_capa.py::test_capa_read_requires_grant` still asserted `GET /capas`‚Üí403; renamed ‚Üí `test_capa_list_filters_not_403_ncr_still_enforces`, 200+empty while `/ncrs` stays SYSTEM-403). **Named deferrals (not faked):** (i) **the multi-role first-process-probe false-negative** ‚Äî a caller who is BOTH an auditor (SYSTEM `process.read` ‚Üí all processes) AND a bound owner of a *non-first* process may have the button hidden (a SAFE false-negative ‚Äî never a crash/over-grant; server-403 is the boundary); the O(1) probe is the owner-approved trade-off, with a future backend `can_raise` signal the fix if it ever becomes real (Codex re-raised this as a fresh P2, declined-with-rationale). (ii) **NCR raise NOT widened** ‚Äî `ncr.create` is in the catalog but bound to NO role (SYSTEM-override-only in v1), so no Process-Owner can hold it at any scope ‚Üí the NCR raise gap is not exercisable by a bound owner (owner-confirmed; the picker would be dead). **Test delta: +5 api integration** (`test_capa_process_scope.py`, CI-only on Windows: list-narrows-to-owned [P1/P2/ad-hoc] ¬∑ detail+approval-enforce-process-scope [owned 200 / unowned 403] ¬∑ a SYSTEM `capa.read` holder reads a PROCESS-scoped CAPA [the Top-Mgmt path] ¬∑ no-grant-list-is-200-empty-not-403 ¬∑ a bound owner raises ONLY in an owned process [own 201, process-less 403, unowned-P2 403]) **+ the `test_capa.py` 403‚Üí200-empty rename/fix; +7 web** (`CapaBoardPage.test.tsx`: button shows for a PROCESS-only `capa.create` holder ¬∑ hidden for a read-only auditor ¬∑ the board threads `requireProcess` [placeholder discriminator] ¬∑ reopen discards the draft; `RaiseCapaModal.test.tsx`: submits the chosen `process_id` ¬∑ omits the picker when no processes ¬∑ `requireProcess` gates submit until a pick); **web 1086‚Üí1093** (fixtures pinned via `satisfies MePermissions`/`CapaRaiseBody`). ruff + ruff-format + mypy-strict clean (modulo the Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline); redocly clean; CI 11/11 green (all 4 integration shards). **diff-critic CRITICAL** (the stale `GET /capas`‚Üí403 assertion) **‚Üí fixed**; **web-test-trap-reviewer MAJOR** (the board required-picker test was a false-PASS ‚Äî tautological label queries) **‚Üí fixed** (placeholder discriminator + the modal's real submit-gate), plus 2 MINORs (modal-test tautology, persistent-modal reset ‚Üí conditional mount). **Codex** P1 (board read-filter) + P2 (required picker) FIXED, the fresh multi-role P2 declined-with-rationale; all 3 threads resolved. **Merge gate:** green CI + 0 unresolved threads + reviewers' findings fixed + owner's explicit go. PR [#220](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/220), squash `6e645f8`.

## v1.x RECORDS PROCESS-SCOPE ‚Äî Process-Owner record read + authoring + the clause-map grant (the named S-process-scope-1 follow-up; 0057)

> The deferred "records process-scope read" follow-up S-process-scope-1 named after its records read enrichment did NOT converge under Codex and was reverted. Specced first, then shipped in sequenced slices: **spec ‚Üí R (read) ‚Üí W (write-enable) ‚Üí C (clauseMap.read grant)**. The structural insight (from the S-process-scope-1 revert): a READ surface is only safe to scope by process bindings if EVERY write path that CREATES those bindings re-authorizes the target ‚Äî so the read DECOUPLES from the write (R ships safely with the write gates process-blind), and write-enable (W) is its own sequenced slice with per-target re-auth. The whole records WRITE re-auth is the non-converging surface (Codex took 3‚Äì4 rounds each on R + W); **trim-don't-chase** is what converged it.

- **S-records-C** (Process Owner gains `clauseMap.read` @ SYSTEM ‚Äî the create-in-process wizard's clause step) ‚Äî **the LAST functional piece of the arc.** A bound Process-Owner (the seeded "Process Owner" role assigned with a PROCESS `bound_scope`, as owner-assignment mints) got **403** on `GET /clauses` (gated `clauseMap.read`, SYSTEM-scoped) ‚Üí the wizard's clause step was empty. **What shipped (migration `0057`, NO new permission key ‚Äî `clauseMap.read` already exists [`0004`]; catalog stays 102; R47 = an R38-ADDITIVE role GRANT, not a key):** (1) **migration 0057** grants the Process Owner role a SYSTEM-scoped `clauseMap.read` `role_grant`, inserted for EVERY org's Process Owner role (by role NAME ‚Äî not the `DEFAULT` org `0004` targets ‚Äî so it reaches a renamed install like `AHT`; idempotent `on_conflict_do_nothing` on `(org_id,role_id,permission_id)`; data-only ‚Üí `alembic check` unaffected). (2) **THE coupled resolver fix** in `services/authz/repository._grant_from_role`: the grant alone is INSUFFICIENT ‚Äî a bound owner's `role_assignment` carries a PROCESS `bound_scope`, and the resolver did `raw = bound_scope or scope_template` (bound_scope REPLACES every grant's scope), so the new SYSTEM `clauseMap.read` got CLAMPED to the bound PROCESS ‚Üí unsatisfiable against the SYSTEM clause-map resource (`pdp._matches_scope` PROCESS = `bool(scoped & resource.process_ids)`, and a SYSTEM resource has empty `process_ids`). Fix: an **EXPLICIT `level=="SYSTEM"` template is never clamped by a bound_scope** (a SYSTEM-finest grant has no `:assignment_process` placeholder to concretize); every parameterized (PROCESS/FOLDER/‚Ä¶) template still defers to the bound_scope. **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **`finest_scope` is documentary, but the bound_scope CLAMP is the real blocker** ‚Äî unlike S-process-scope-2 (where threading `process_ids` was the whole fix), here the SYSTEM grant exists but the bound_scope replace-semantics ate it; the resolver fix is the load-bearing half, not the migration. (2) **blast radius verified = exactly this case** ‚Äî every pre-existing bound assignment uses `bound_scope={"level":"SYSTEM"}` (a SYSTEM bound + any template = SYSTEM either way ‚Üí unchanged), and the only PROCESS-bound role today (owner-assignment Process Owner) had NO SYSTEM grant before this slice; no existing SYSTEM grant is widened. (3) **exempt only an EXPLICIT SYSTEM template, not `_scope_from_dict`'s SYSTEM default** ‚Äî a NULL/level-less template defers to the bound_scope (the conservative, non-widening direction); pre-empts the reviewers' NULL-template note. (4) the ruff hook strips just-added imports (body-first; hit twice here). **Test delta: +1 api unit** (`test_authz_resolver.py`, 5 cases ‚Äî SYSTEM-not-clamped, PROCESS-still-concretized, SYSTEM-bound-unchanged, no-bound-stays-SYSTEM, level-less-defers; runs LOCALLY) **+1 api integration** (`test_clauses.py::test_bound_process_owner_reads_clauses` ‚Äî a bound owner reads `/clauses` ‚Üí 200; discriminates BOTH the migration grant AND the resolver fix) **+ a Process-Owner grant assertion in `test_authz`** (catalog stays 102, the grant is SYSTEM-scoped); **web unchanged.** ruff + format + mypy-strict clean; migration round-trip up‚Üîdown‚Üî`alembic check` CLEAN on PG16 (grant verified `Process Owner/clauseMap.read/SYSTEM`, catalog 102). **migration-reviewer + diff-critic both CLEAN** (the NULL-template note pre-empted via the explicit-level exemption); **Codex CLEAN** ("Didn't find any major issues"). **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + 0 unresolved threads + reviewers + Codex clean + owner's plan approval (pre-authorized the merge path). PR [#218](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/218), squash `71ecfcf`.

- **S-records-W** (Process-Owner record AUTHORING ‚Äî write-enable + per-target re-auth) ‚Äî **enables a bound Process-Owner to AUTHOR records bound to their process, the write half R decoupled from.** **What shipped (NO migration [head stays `0056`], NO new key; contract = gate-note text):** `_record_read_scope` renamed `_record_process_scope`, now resolving BOTH the `_read` AND the per-record `_create_scoped` (write-enable) gates; a new **`_enforce_target_process_record`** (the `documents._enforce_target_process` analogue ‚Äî re-enforce `record.create` over a scope whose `process_ids` is JUST the target, so a SYSTEM/ARTIFACT/FOLDER holder still passes but a PROCESS holder must own the SPECIFIC target). Re-auth points: **capture** = a per-process loop over the source doc's processes (own ALL; mirrors `documents.create`); **evidence-link add/remove** = re-auth a PROCESS target the caller owns, while EVERY other target type (CLAUSE/DOCUMENT/FINDING/CAPA_STAGE) re-auths over an EMPTY set ‚Üí broad/SYSTEM holders only (the TRIM ‚Äî satisfies the spec's R3-2 capa_stage gap by DENY, not by scoping); **correction** = re-auth the UNION of the successor's new-source processes AND the original's FULL effective binding, per-process. `_dispose` stays process-blind. **‚öÝ THE non-convergence (this surface) ‚Äî diff-critic CRITICAL + 3 substantive Codex rounds, trim-don't-chase converged it:** the diff-critic caught the **capture untightened** (the base intersection-match passes if ANY source process is owned ‚Üí a P1-owner could mint a P1+P2 record under a shared doc) ‚Üí the per-process loop. Codex then surfaced a NEW correction/evidence-link edge each round: **round-4 P1** ‚Äî the correction re-auth used `source_processes OR effective(original)`, which SHORT-CIRCUITED on an owned source process and skipped an unowned EXISTING binding (a P1-owner could supersede a record co-bound to P2; `capture_correction` does NOT carry the original's EvidenceForLinks ‚Üí a P1-only successor P2 owners lose) ‚Üí **replaced the `or` with a UNION** (own every process the original is currently bound to + any new source); **round-5 P2** ‚Äî a TOCTOU: the correction read the binding BEFORE `capture_correction`'s FOR UPDATE lock, and `link_evidence` inserted without locking the Record ‚Üí **lock the Record row FOR UPDATE in correction_endpoint (held through the supersede, `populate_existing`), link_evidence, AND unlink_evidence** so all three binding-relevant writers serialize on the one row; **round-6** (2 deeper P2 TOCTOUs ‚Äî re-auth-under-lock for `link_evidence`, lock the unbounded `correction_of` ancestor chain ‚Äî + the CAPA-stage residual re-raised) were **TRIMMED as bounded named residuals** (single-org, deep interleavings; the deterministic escalation + same-record TOCTOU are already closed; fixes are unbounded/invasive on a non-converging surface). **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **a READ surface is only safe to scope by process bindings if EVERY binding-MINTING write re-authorizes the target** ‚Äî capture (per-process), evidence-link (PROCESS-target), correction (union of the original's full binding); the `_enforce_target_process_record` discipline for EVERY target type. (2) **the records WRITE re-auth does NOT converge ‚Äî trim, don't chase**: when a surface keeps generating edges round after round, TRIM the over-grant to broad-only/deny (evidence-link non-PROCESS targets) and the FOR UPDATE lock is the STRUCTURAL terminal fix, not another logic patch that invites the next round. (3) the final-state of a correction-vs-link race can't DISTINGUISH the bypass from the legal correction-wins case ‚Üí prove the lock with a deterministic 2-session held-lock-blocks test, not an `asyncio.gather` final-state assertion. (4) `populate_existing` on the correction's locking load is LOAD-BEARING (the handler reads `original.source_document_id` off the locked object). (5) the ruff hook strips just-added imports (body-first, recurring). **Named residual: `POST /records:init-upload` stays SYSTEM-gated** (process-less byte staging ‚Üí a Process-Owner authors FORM records + PROCESS links against an already-staged blob, but staging a NEW evidence blob is a bounded follow-up); plus the trimmed Process-Owner CAPA/FINDING/DOCUMENT evidence (broad-only) + the 2 round-6 TOCTOUs. **Test delta: +8 api integration** (`test_records_process_scope.py`: capture-in-owned-process, evidence-link target re-auth add/remove, artifact-holder-not-over-blocked, cannot-introduce-unowned-source, cannot-capture-under-shared-doc, cannot-link-non-process-target, correction-reauths-inherited-binding, correction-cannot-supersede-co-bound [round-4], binding-writes-serialize-on-record-lock [round-5]); **web unchanged.** ruff + format + mypy-strict clean; **diff-critic √ó3 (CRITICAL on capture ‚Üí CLEAN on the union + lock fixes); Codex 3 substantive rounds (4/5/6).** **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + 0 unresolved threads (all rounds replied + resolved, round-6 trimmed with rationale) + owner's explicit per-round go. PR [#217](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/217), squash `6dcb976`.

- **S-records-R** (records process-scope READ via a DECOUPLED read-only resolver) ‚Äî **a bound Process-Owner's PROCESS-scoped `record.read` authorizes records bound to their owned processes, WITHOUT enabling them to mint a binding (the writes stay process-blind; authoring is W).** The decoupling is the spec's central result: a read-only resolver ships safely with NO write re-auth because no NARROW holder can mint a binding (every binding-minting write 403s them at the process-blind base gate). **What shipped (NO migration [head stays `0056`], NO new key ‚Äî rides `record.read`, `finest_scope` documentary; no contract change):** (1) `services/records/repository.py` = the ONE source of truth ‚Äî **`record_process_ids`** (leg A `EvidenceForLink(PROCESS)` targets ‚à™ leg B source-doc `ProcessLink`s), **`record_process_ids_effective`** (+ the R3-1 `correction_of` walk ‚Äî ITERATIVE, visited-set, no hop cap), and a batched **`record_process_ids_for`** for the list; (2) a new **`_record_read_scope`** resolver (full context + the process binding) for the `_read` gate ONLY ‚Äî `_create_scoped`/`_dispose` stay on the process-BLIND `_record_scope` (the decoupling); the `GET /records` list row-filter enriched (batched binding + per-row R3-1 fallback); (3) `packs/service.classify_candidates` refactored onto `records_repo.record_process_ids_effective` (the pack classifier + `/records` now agree from one source; the duplicate left `packs/repository`). **3 Codex rounds:** CX-3 hop-cap ‚Üí **visited set** (cycle-safe, no cap that drops a long legitimate correction chain) + a 2-hop test; the pack-candidate query must ALSO walk corrections (so the pack `record.read` exposure matches the records gate); the candidate "owned" predicate must equal a non-empty own union EXACTLY. **‚öÝ Traps:** the decoupling (read resolver separate, writes process-blind) is WHY R is safe without W's re-auth ‚Äî never fold the write gates onto the process-aware resolver without W's `_enforce_target_process_record`. **Test delta: +6 api integration** (`test_records_process_scope.py`: reads-owned/403s-unowned, list-filters, source-less-invisible, R3-1 single + 2-hop correction-chain visibility, + the read/write decoupling invariant ‚Äî reads 200 but a per-record write 403s); **web unchanged.** ruff + mypy-strict clean; **diff-critic CLEAN (prompted the decoupling-invariant coverage add); Codex 3 rounds.** **Merge gate:** green CI + 0 unresolved threads + Codex clean + owner's go. PR [#216](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/216), squash `1fc8f24`.

- **S-records-spec** (the authz model + sequenced slice plan for "records process-scope read") ‚Äî **the deferred follow-up, SPECCED + adversarially validated BEFORE code** (the surface that did not converge in S-process-scope-1). `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-19-records-process-scope-authz-design.md`: the model + a **4-lens refutation panel** (read-only-safe, 0 holes). **Central result:** enriching a DECOUPLED read-only resolver (read + list only, write gates process-blind) is escalation-free with NO write re-auth ‚Äî a Process-Owner reads their records but mints nothing (every binding-minting write 403s them at the base gate; capture inherits only the source-doc's already-re-authorized links; the minter enumeration is complete). The write re-auth (the B-work) is needed ONLY to ENABLE Process-Owner authoring, which alone opens the `capa_stage` target class. **Ratified plan: Slice R (read) + Slice W (write-enable, sequenced) + Slice C (`clauseMap.read` ‚Üí Process-Owner bundle, R38).** Four bounded caveats named as accepted residuals (capture doc-spans-processes visibility, sibling SYSTEM-gated read surfaces, the `correction_of` hop cap, AZ-INV-8 monotonicity). Docs-only. PR [#215](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/215), squash `4e929a9`.

## v1.x OWNER-ASSIGNMENT ‚Äî PROCESS-scoped RBAC binding: substitutes the long-deferred `:assignment_process` placeholder (0056)

- **S-process-scope-2** (per-process read-filter on `GET /processes` + `/map`) ‚Äî **"Slice A" of the named S-process-scope-1 "records process-scope read" follow-up: the smallest, lowest-risk, highest-unblock piece, split out from the deeper records work.** A bound Process-Owner's `process.read` is PROCESS-scoped, but the process-landscape reads were gated `require("process.read")` at **default SYSTEM scope** ‚Üí a bound owner got a hard **403**, so the create-in-process wizard PICKER (shipped #211) was empty for them. **What shipped (BE-only, NO migration [head stays `0056`], NO new permission key [rides `process.read`, catalog stays 102]; contract = description text only ‚Äî no shape change):** (1) **`GET /processes` + `GET /processes/map`** moved from `Depends(_read)` (SYSTEM enforce) to `Depends(get_current_user)` + a new `_readable_processes()` **row-filter** (`gather_grants("process.read")` once ‚Üí per-row `authorize` over `ResourceContext(process_ids={str(p.id)})`; the `GET /records` + `/search` precedent). `/map` also **drops any edge whose endpoint is hidden** (no dangling edge to an unreadable process). (2) **`GET /processes/{id}`** moved `_read` ‚Üí the existing `_read_scoped` (enforce `process.read` at the process's PROCESS scope; still **403-on-deny**, single-resource). (3) the now-unused `_read` (SYSTEM) removed. **THE load-bearing correction (vs the brief, which assumed a migration/finest_scope change):** **no migration and no new key are needed** ‚Äî the seeded *Process Owner* bundle ALREADY grants `record.read`/`process.read` at PROCESS scope (`0004_seed_authz.py:205,322`), and **`finest_scope` is documentary catalog metadata, NEVER enforced at runtime** (`pdp.py:81-83` matches a PROCESS grant purely on `bool(scoped & resource.process_ids)`); the only blocker was the empty `resource.process_ids` on the read gate. **Decisions/behavior:** a SYSTEM grant matches every row (`_matches_scope` returns True for SYSTEM regardless of `process_ids`) ‚Üí QMS Owner / Internal Auditor / a `demo` SYSTEM override see the org-wide landscape **byte-identical**; the **one observable change (owner-approved): a no-grant caller on the LIST/MAP now gets `200` + empty instead of `403`** ‚Äî the documented list-surface **filter-not-403** doctrine (doc 18 ¬ß5.2 / doc 15 ¬ß9.3), matching records/search (the list/map GETs no longer document a `403`). `GET /clauses` was explicitly **OUT** (a per-process clause filter is ill-defined ‚Äî clauses are framework-anchored reference data; `clauseMap.read` isn't even in the Process-Owner bundle) ‚Üí a separate owner decision. **Understand phase** ran a 6-reader ‚Üí synthesis Workflow that produced the A/B1/B2/B3 split (B1 write-path re-auth BEFORE B2 read scoping is the structural insight from the S-process-scope-1 records revert) and surfaced the no-migration correction. **Codex round 1 ‚Äî 3 P2, triaged 2-fixed/1-declined (a clean diff-critic passed):** **CX-1** (thread `source_ip`) **FIXED** ‚Äî `_readable_processes` now threads `request.client.host` so an `ip_allow` grant evaluates exactly as the replaced `require()` enforce did (v1-deferred but kept faithful; the S-leadership-cx1 precedent); **CX-2** (a row-filtered child row leaks its hidden parent's id via `parent_id`) **FIXED** ‚Äî `_process(p, visible_ids)` nulls `parent_id` on the list/map when the parent isn't visible (the edge-filter rationale; detail/authoring keep it); **CX-3** (honour `include_subprocesses`) **DECLINED** ‚Äî `include_subprocesses` (docs/07 ¬ß5.3, "default true") is documented but **UNIMPLEMENTED anywhere in the v1 PDP** (the PROCESS match is a pure own-id intersection, no resolver walks `parent_id`, owner-assignment mints explicit `process_ids`, `_document_scope`/records/search all use own-id/own-link sets) ‚Üí a cross-cutting authz-model change that must land consistently across documents/records/processes, named as its own follow-up. **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **for a process landscape read, `finest_scope` is a red herring ‚Äî it is documentary, not a runtime gate**; the grant already existed, so the fix was purely threading `process_ids` into the resource context. (2) **a row-filter must sanitize EVERY pointer to a hidden row, not just the rows themselves** ‚Äî the `/map` edge filter AND the `parent_id` null (CX-2) are the same "no dangling pointer / no hidden-id leak" rule. (3) **the ruff PostToolUse hook strips just-added imports ‚Üí body-first** (recurring; hit again here). (4) **Slice A converged in ONE Codex round** (the predicted LOW risk) precisely because it's a pure READ with no write-path-minted visibility channel ‚Äî the opposite of the records read (B2) that didn't converge; the A/B split exists so the safe read ships first. **Deferred (named, not faked) ‚Äî the rest of "records process-scope read":** **B1** (records evidence-link POST/DELETE + correction RE-AUTHORIZE the target/effective-source process ‚Äî the `_enforce_target_process` analogue, the safety floor) ‚Üí **B2** (scope records read by a single shared loader == `packs::record_process_ids`, only after B1) ‚Üí **B3** (the pre-existing `capa_stage` evidence-link authz gap, orthogonal); plus the `GET /clauses` fix (add `clauseMap.read` SYSTEM to the bundle vs route the wizard's clause step elsewhere ‚Äî an owner call) and the NEW **subprocess/descendant-inclusion** authz follow-up surfaced by CX-3. **Test delta: +2 api integration** (`test_process_scope.py`: a bound owner of P1-not-P2 narrows on list/map with the P1‚ÜíP2 edge dropped + a SYSTEM-author full-landscape baseline; + a SYSTEM-holder `404`-not-`403` detail assertion); **web unchanged** (the FE `useProcesses()` already degrades-on-403 and renders whatever it gets ‚Üí the picker now populates for a bound owner with no FE change). ruff + ruff-format + mypy-strict clean (modulo the Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline); redocly clean; CI 11/11 green (all 4 integration shards). **diff-critic CLEAN** (SYSTEM-byte-identical, the /map dangling-edge filter, no write-path over-grant channel, the 403-before-404 detail order, the dropped enforce-audit matching records/search, the tests' genuineness all verified ‚Äî it also prompted the SYSTEM-404 coverage add). **Merge gate:** green CI + 0 unresolved threads (3 Codex P2 ‚Äî 2 fixed, 1 declined-with-rationale ‚Äî all replied + resolved) + Codex üëç re-approve + owner's explicit go.
