- **S-process-scope-1** (enrich the secondary auth surfaces with `process_ids` + the `document.create` link-on-create write-path) ‚Äî **the named S-owner-assignment-1 follow-up "enrich every auth surface with `process_ids`", shipped for the surfaces that CONVERGED.** S-owner-assignment-1 migrated `_document_scope` (document detail/list/edit), but the workflow approval-history reads, the search row-filter, and `document.create` all built their own `ResourceContext` WITHOUT `process_ids`, so a bound Process-Owner's PROCESS-scoped grant mis-denied them. **What shipped (BE+FE, NO migration [head stays `0056`], NO new permission key [catalog stays 102, R38 not engaged]; contract = ONE additive `DocumentCreate.process_ids`):** (1) a shared `vault_repo.process_ids_for_doc(s)` loader ‚Äî `_document_scope_by_id` + the `GET /documents` list batch refactored onto it (parity-preserving, deletes the two duplicated inline ProcessLink queries); (2) **workflow** ‚Äî `GET /workflow-instances/{id}` + `GET /documents/{id}/approval` carry the subject doc's `process_ids` (both gate `document.read`); (3) **search** ‚Äî `_readable_hits` + `/search/suggest` batch-load `process_ids` per candidate hit; (4) **`document.create` write-path** ‚Äî `DocumentCreate.process_ids` (optional, `maxItems:50`) links the new doc AT creation: `create_document(processes=...)` creates the doc + `ProcessLink` rows + `PROCESS_LINKED` audit (with `identifier=doc.identifier` ‚Üí `to_audit_event` maps `scope_ref=identifier`, byte-compatible with the standalone link endpoint's per-document trail) in ONE txn/commit (atomic ‚Äî a failed link can't strand a doc its process-scoped creator could no longer read); authorize `document.create` over the declared processes THEN re-`enforce` `document.manage_metadata` PER declared process (mirrors `_enforce_target_process`, so an owner of P1 can't smuggle a link to an unowned P2 ‚Äî the S-owner-assignment-1 escalation class), empty `process_ids` ‚áí byte-identical to the pre-slice create; plus a processes `MultiSelect` on the New-Document wizard. **Load-bearing decisions:** the enrichment is **strictly monotonic / AZ-INV-8-safe** ‚Äî the PDP matches a PROCESS grant iff `selector.process_ids ‚à© resource.process_ids ‚âÝ ‚àÖ`, so adding `process_ids` only newly *matches* a grant already targeting that exact process, never widens SYSTEM/ARTIFACT/FOLDER/DOC_CLASS (re-derived per surface). `_decision_scope` (the workflow approve/review DECIDE gate) was deliberately EXCLUDED ‚Äî the seeded "Process Owner" role holds no `document.approve`/`review`, so enriching it is a dead no-op (named, not missed). **‚öÝ THE big lesson ‚Äî the records read enrichment did NOT converge and was TRIMMED OUT mid-slice:** records read (a record inherits its source-doc + `EvidenceForLink(PROCESS)` scope, matching the packs `record.read` gate) was built + reviewed, but Codex surfaced a NEW evidence-link/correction over-grant edge every round ‚Äî **CX-1** (evidence-link POST doesn't re-auth the PROCESS target ‚Üí an owner of P1 makes a record readable to P2's owners), **CX-4** (correction doesn't re-scope its source), **R2-1** (the re-auth must PRESERVE the record scope, replacing only `process_ids`, else ARTIFACT/FOLDER holders over-blocked), **R2-2** (the evidence-link DELETE also needs target re-auth), **R2-3** (`capture_correction` FORCES a source-backed original's OWN source ‚Äî the body's is ignored ‚Äî so re-auth the EFFECTIVE source), **R3-1** (a source-less evidence-linked record's correction loses its process binding ‚Üí invisible to its creator), **R3-2** (a PRE-EXISTING `capa_stage` evidence-link authz gap the partial re-auth highlights). After 3 substantive rounds with no convergence, the owner's call was to **revert the records read enrichment** (restore `api/records.py`, `services/records/repository.py`, `services/packs/repository.py` to `main`) and ship only the converged surfaces. **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **adding `process_ids` to a READ surface is monotonic and safe, but adding it to a surface whose process bindings are created by UN-RE-AUTHORIZED write paths (records evidence-link / correction) opens an over-grant** ‚Äî the read enrichment is only as sound as the write-path target re-authorization (the `_enforce_target_process` discipline) for EVERY target type, AND the correction-chain scope; that whole sub-project is deferred. (2) the `document.create` chicken-and-egg (a new doc has no ProcessLink) is the reason create needs `process_ids` in the BODY + atomic link-on-create ‚Äî it can't be a pure resolver enrichment like the reads. (3) the ruff PostToolUse hook strips just-added imports (body-first, recurring). (4) **Codex authz non-convergence again** ‚Äî the shipped surfaces (workflow/search/create) had ZERO findings across 4 rounds; 100% of findings were on records (reverted) or the deferred FE; triage per round, and when a surface keeps generating edges, TRIM it rather than chase. **Deferred (named, not faked) ‚Äî ONE focused follow-up, "records process-scope read":** the records read enrichment bundled with its write-path target re-auth (evidence-link POST/DELETE + correction effective-source + EVERY non-process evidence-link target incl. the pre-existing `capa_stage` gap), the correction-chain scope, the pre-existing packs `record.read` exposure, AND **per-process read filtering on `GET /processes` + `GET /clauses`** (both SYSTEM-gated today ‚Üí the create-in-process wizard works for SYSTEM/Author authors but the picker + clause step are empty for a bound Process-Owner; the `document.create` backend is correct regardless). Codex **CX-3** (require `document.create` per declared process) was **DECLINED** ‚Äî the end-state (a doc linked to P1+P2) is reachable with the same perms via `create([P1])` + the standalone `link(P2)` (which gates only `manage_metadata`-for-P2), so per-process create would be stricter than the documented decomposed flow. **Test delta: +8 api integration** (`test_process_scope.py`, CI-only on Windows: create-in-owned-process + multi-process dedup + can't-create-unlinked + the P1+P2 escalation-403 + unknown-process-422 + create-holder-without-manage_metadata + the workflow approval/instance 403‚Üí200 flip on a linked doc with the unlinked-stays-403 boundary + search-sees-only-linked-effective) **+2 web** (`NewDocumentWizard.test.tsx`: the picker sends `process_ids`; the omitted-when-empty byte-identical body); **web 1084‚Üí1086**, no api unit added. ruff + mypy-strict clean (modulo the Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline); redocly clean; full web `1086/1086`. **diff-critic (√ó2) + web-test-trap-reviewer + a 3-lens review Workflow (missed-surface / authz-edges / create-parity) all CLEAN on the shipped surfaces**; the records findings were 100% Codex (the documented authz-non-convergence pattern). **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + 0 unresolved threads (12 total ‚Äî records moot/reverted, CX-3 declined, FE deferred ‚Äî all replied + resolved) + owner's explicit go. PR [#211](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/211), squash `42f8de6`.

- **S-owner-assignment-1** (real process-owner binding + the repo-wide `_document_scope`‚Üí`process_ids` migration) ‚Äî **closes the owner-assignment gap that every prior PROCESS-scoped slice rode around via SYSTEM overrides.** The whole PROCESS-scoped ABAC engine was already built (`ScopeLevel.PROCESS`, the PDP `_matches_scope` process_ids intersection, `role_assignment.bound_scope` as the concretization seam, the seeded "Process Owner" permission-role), but nothing turned "Diego owns Purchasing" into a concrete `process_id`: every seeded Process-Owner grant carried the literal placeholder `selector.process_id = ":assignment_process"` (migrations 0004/0036/0040/0043/0044/0052) that matches no real process, so PROCESS-finest-scope authority was satisfied only by SYSTEM overrides. **What shipped (BE+FE, migration `0056`, NO new permission key ‚Äî rides the seeded-but-unenforced `process.assign_owner`; catalog stays 102, R38 not engaged):** (1) the ERD-deferred **`org_role_assignment`** RACI carrier (`org_role_id`‚Üí`org_role`, `user_id`‚Üí`app_user`, `process_id` NULLABLE‚Üí`process`, `UNIQUE(org_role_id,user_id,process_id)`) + its ORM (registered in `db/models/__init__.py`) + two additive `event_type` values `PROCESS_OWNER_ASSIGNED`/`_REVOKED` (autocommit_block ADD VALUE; NO new `audit_object_type` ‚Äî events key on the existing `process` value); (2) **`services/owner_assignment.py`** ‚Äî `assign_process_owner`/`revoke_process_owner` in ONE txn: resolve-or-create the single generic "Process Owner" org_role, upsert the org_role_assignment RACI row, and **mint/extend a SINGLE PROCESS-scoped Process-Owner `role_assignment.bound_scope`** carrying a GROWING `process_ids` set (the PDP reads `selector.process_id OR process_ids`, so one row authorizes many owned processes ‚Äî `role_assignment` has no uniqueness backstop, so one growing row beats N rows), **system-attributed** (the `process.assign_owner` content-tier gate is the sole authority; NOT re-gated through SYSTEM-tier `permission.grant`), serialized on the parent `app_user` row FOR UPDATE, audited both halves, then `invalidate_user_permissions`; (3) `POST`/`DELETE /processes/{id}/owner` + `GET /processes/{id}/owners` (+ openapi); (4) the **repo-wide `_document_scope` migration** ‚Äî `_document_scope_by_id` now folds the doc's `ProcessLink` ids into `ResourceContext.process_ids` (deleting the single-use `_document_scope_with_processes`, repointing `_distribute`), and the `GET /documents` list read-filter batch-loads process links per row (no N+1), so a bound Process-Owner's `document.*` grant authorizes across EVERY document gate, not just `distribute`; (5) a minimal **`admin/ProcessesAdmin.tsx`** tab (assign/revoke owners; coarse SYSTEM `process.assign_owner` probe gates the write affordances, server 403 is the true boundary). **THE central design device ‚Äî the `managed_by:"owner_assignment"` bound_scope marker** (the PDP `_scope_from_dict` ignores it ‚Äî reads level/selector/predicates only): owner-assignment-minted grants confer the scoped PERMISSION set but are EXCLUDED from every ROLE-MEMBERSHIP consumer. **‚öÝ THE load-bearing lesson ‚Äî "mint a Process-Owner `role_assignment`" leaks role MEMBERSHIP everywhere, and Codex (3 substantive rounds, 6‚Üí6‚Üí3 findings) is the only finder of it** (clean diff-critic/migration-reviewer/web-test-trap passed the core code each round): the marker exclusion had to be applied to (a) **workflow candidate resolution** `wf_repo.users_with_roles` ‚Äî the **P1**: migration 0043's DCR-MAJOR-approval stage NAMES "Process Owner" as a candidate role and `users_with_roles` joins on `Role.name` (scope-blind), so an owner of process A would otherwise become a candidate for every "Process Owner"-gated stage org-wide (a DCR for process B); (b) **ack audience** `resolve_audience` ‚Äî same flood onto every process owner for a role-targeted distribution; (c) the **generic role surface** `authz.py` ‚Äî `list_user_roles` HIDES marked rows + `revoke_user_role` 409s them (a bare delete would orphan the org_role_assignment RACI row), and the marker is **un-forgeable** (`assign_user_role` strips a caller-supplied `managed_by`). **‚öÝ The `_document_scope` widening ALSO introduced a process-link ESCALATION** ‚Äî `document.manage_metadata` now matches via ANY linked process, so an owner of A on a doc linked to A+B could mutate links to B ‚Üí the link/unlink endpoints re-`enforce` `document.manage_metadata` against the TARGET process scope (`_enforce_target_process`: SYSTEM/ARTIFACT/FOLDER holders still pass, a PROCESS owner must own the target). **‚öÝ Other traps:** an idempotent re-assign must SKIP the phantom `PROCESS_OWNER_ASSIGNED`/`ROLE_ASSIGN` audit rows (track whether the binding or the process_ids actually changed); a narrowing revoke emits `ROLE_REVOKE` (not `ROLE_ASSIGN` ‚Äî revoke always reduces access); `GET /owners` is process-scoped read (a PROCESS owner can read their own process's owners ‚Äî **the FIRST CI failure was a TEST bug**: it's `process.read`-gated and the tests granted only `assign_owner` ‚Üí 403, then the next test iterated the 403 error body ‚Üí `TypeError`); the optional `org_role_id` body field was REMOVED (every binding keys to ONE generic org_role ‚Üí at most one org_role_assignment per (user,process) ‚Üí revoke can't over-delete an unrelated RACI binding); `bound_scope` is JSONB ‚Üí reassign a fresh dict, never in-place (S-ing-4); FK names match the Base naming convention (alembic-check phantom-DROP) + the ORM registered in `__init__.py`; the ruff hook strips just-added imports (body-first). **Deferred (named, not faked) ‚Äî ONE coherent follow-up, "enrich every auth surface with `process_ids`":** the slice migrated `_document_scope` (document detail/list/edit/approve work), but `document.create` (POST /documents authorizes from folder/doc_class), workflow approval-history reads (`/workflow-instances/{id}`, `/documents/{id}/approval`), the `search` row-filter, and `record.read`/list scopes all build their OWN ResourceContext without process_ids ‚Äî so the minted Process-Owner grant is **read/edit/approve-effective on EXISTING process-linked documents** but create + those secondary reads need the same enrichment (each a sibling resolver). Plus the FE per-process assign-owner probe (deliberate coarse-SYSTEM gate; additive if process-scoped `assign_owner` delegation lands); the **CAPA Raise process-scope deferral is now UNBLOCKED** (the binding exists) but the Raise process-picker is still unwired. **Test delta: +11 api integration** (CI-only on Windows: the 403‚Üí200 doc-read flip on a process-linked doc ¬∑ the union + idempotent no-op ¬∑ revoke-narrows-then-drops ¬∑ admin SYSTEM + PROCESS grants survive ¬∑ workflow-candidacy exclusion ¬∑ managed-revoke 409 ¬∑ target-process link authority ¬∑ forged-marker strip) **+4 web** (`ProcessesAdmin.test.tsx`: roster + read-only drawer, assign, remove, calm 403); **web 1080‚Üí1084.** No api unit added. ruff + mypy-strict clean (modulo the Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline); migration round-trip up‚Üîdown‚Üî`alembic check` CLEAN on PG16; redocly clean. **diff-critic 1 MINOR** (owner-revoke could clobber a separately-granted admin Process-Owner row ‚Üí the `managed_by` marker; fixed + tested); **migration-reviewer + web-test-trap-reviewer CLEAN; Codex 3 substantive rounds ‚Üí round 4 CLEAN üëç** (the design class genuinely doesn't converge ‚Äî each round surfaced a new role-membership/scope-widening interaction; triage per round: fix the introduced issue, defer bounded-safe). **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + 0 unresolved threads (15 total, all replied + resolved) + Codex clean + owner's explicit go. PR [#209](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/209), squash `48c7e71`.

## v1.x OBJECTIVE GRADING FREEZE ‚Äî per-reading frozen direction/threshold (closes the S-obj-charts "freeze the grading inputs" deferral) (0055)

- **S-obj-freeze** (freeze the FULL per-reading KPI grading basis) ‚Äî **closes the named S-obj-charts v1.x deferral: the per-reading RAG verdict was only PARTIALLY frozen, so a commitment revision that flipped `direction` (HIGHER‚ÜîLOWER) or moved the `at_risk_threshold` retroactively re-graded historical readings (a past green could read red).** Only `kpi_measurement.target_at_capture` was frozen; `direction`/`at_risk_threshold` were read LIVE from the governing commitment at serialize time. **What shipped (BACKEND-ONLY, additive, migration `0055`):** two new `kpi_measurement` columns ‚Äî `direction_at_capture` (REUSE the `objective_direction` enum, `create_type=False`) + `at_risk_threshold_at_capture` (Numeric) ‚Äî both **NULLABLE**; `record_measurement` snapshots them from the SAME governing-else-working resolution as `target_at_capture` (and seals them into the WORM `KPI_READING` record's `form_field_values` too); `api/objectives.py::_measurement` grades off the frozen columns (the two measurement endpoints SHED their now-dead `resolve_commitment` blocks ‚Äî a net simplification). **The frozen basis stays INTERNAL** ‚Äî the `Measurement` response is byte-identical (only the `rag` description in `openapi.yaml` updated to the frozen-basis semantics), so **no web/MSW change** (contracts + web CI jobs are no-ops). `compute_scorecard` (the live-objective grade) is intentionally UNCHANGED ‚Äî a different semantic from a frozen historical reading. **Capture-time backfill (the load-bearing part ‚Äî 4 Codex rounds hardened it):** each existing reading freezes the commitment that was the CURRENT effective version at its `created_at`, EXACTLY what `record_measurement` froze (it reads `current_effective_version_id`, which only moves at `_cutover`). The version-selection (1) considers ONLY versions that actually went Effective (`version_state='Effective' OR effective_to IS NOT NULL` ‚Äî never a still-`Approved` scheduled revision), and (2) bounds each version's governing window by the PRIOR version's `effective_to` (the real cutover via the `superseded_by_version_id` chain), NOT its own (possibly scheduled) `effective_from`. A reading with no applicable governing version (pre-first-release) or under a fold-less/non-object snapshot falls back to the working row for BOTH columns (mirroring the runtime `governing = raw if isinstance(raw, dict) else None` guard). The backfill UPDATE runs as the migration OWNER role, unaffected by `kpi_measurement`'s app-role `REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE` (WORM intact ‚Äî no app path updates the columns post-insert). **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **the historical backfill is the hard part, not the column add** ‚Äî reconstructing "what commitment governed at capture" is genuinely subtle and the migration round-trip / `alembic check` are VALUE-BLIND (empty fresh DB), so the **diff-critic + migration-reviewer were CLEAN on the application code but Codex was the edge-finder on the backfill over 4 rounds**: capture-time-vs-current ‚Üí scheduled-vs-actual-cutover ‚Üí not-yet-cutover-Approved-version ‚Üí nullable-row-aborts-SET-NOT-NULL. Validate the backfill CASE/version-selection with **synthetic VALUES-based SQL** (no FK scaffolding) on a throwaway PG16 ‚Äî pin the gap cases (a reading between a scheduled `effective_from` and the late `release_due` cutover must freeze the PRIOR basis). (2) **the migration-reviewer (not Codex) caught the FIRST real bug a clean diff-critic missed** ‚Äî the threshold CASE was gated on a different predicate than the direction CASE (a `COALESCE` vs a `CASE`-with-fold-guard), so a fold-less governing version would NULL the threshold where the live grader uses the working row ‚Üí gate BOTH columns on the IDENTICAL `jsonb_typeof(... ->'objective_commitment')='object'` predicate. (3) **`direction_at_capture` is NULLABLE, not NOT NULL** ‚Äî `objective_id` is schema-nullable + the serializer handles an objective-less reading, so a `SET NOT NULL` would abort on an ad-hoc/imported objective-less row (Codex); the serializer narrows the now-Optional direction (None‚Üí"unmeasured", unreachable for the objective-scoped endpoints). (4) **the discriminating test must FLIP the verdict** ‚Äî the existing target-freeze test coincidentally stays amber under both old/new behaviour; the new direction-flip + threshold-move integration tests are designed so frozen‚âÝlive (else they don't prove the freeze). (5) the **revision-id `varchar(32)` limit** ‚Äî `0055_objective_freeze_grading_inputs` (36 chars) overflowed `alembic_version.version_num` at runtime (CI/round-trip would have caught it, but locally first) ‚Üí renamed to `0055_objective_grading_freeze` (29). (6) the **ruff auto-fix hook strips a just-added import** (the recurring trap ‚Äî re-add `objective_direction_enum` AFTER the column references it). **Deferred (named, not faked):** exposing the frozen `direction_at_capture`/`at_risk_threshold_at_capture` in the `Measurement` response (audit-transparency tooltip "graded under higher-is-better, amber<95" ‚Äî owner kept them INTERNAL this slice; a trivial additive add); the other S-obj-charts deferrals (register sparklines, time-proportional x-axis, per-process objective reads) are untouched. **Test delta: +2 api unit** (`test_objective_measurement_rag.py` unit: `test_rag_reads_frozen_direction_not_live` + `test_rag_reads_frozen_threshold_not_live` ‚Äî same value/target, opposite frozen basis ‚Üí opposite verdict; full unit **810 passed**) **+2 api integration** (CI-only on Windows: a direction-flip and a threshold-move revision where frozen‚âÝlive ‚Üí the old reading's `rag` is unchanged) + the `test_objective_revision.py` mid-revision capture test EXTENDED to assert direction/threshold snapshot the GOVERNING (not in-edit) values via a direct DB read; **web unchanged** (backend-only). ruff + mypy-strict clean; migration round-trip up‚Üîdown‚Üî`alembic check` clean on PG16 + the backfill logic proven across 8 synthetic cases. **diff-critic CLEAN; migration-reviewer** found 1 MAJOR (the threshold/direction asymmetry, fixed + re-confirmed CLEAN); **Codex 4 rounds** (capture-time backfill / seal-record / contract-sync ‚Üí prior-`effective_to` window ‚Üí `version_state` filter + nullable ‚Üí final **clean: "no major issues, Delightful"**); all 7 inline threads resolved. **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + 0 unresolved threads + Codex clean + owner's explicit go. PR [#197](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/197), squash `b83bae4`.

## v1.x LEADERSHIP ROUTING ‚Äî document-backed Top-Management release authorization (POL/OBJ/MR)

- **S-leadership-dcr-test** (lock in the DCR-implement leadership preflight ‚Äî closes the named S-leadership-1 deferral) ‚Äî **closes S-leadership-1's named-not-faked deferral verbatim: "a dedicated DCR-implement-of-a-leadership-artifact integration test."** **Backend TEST-ONLY ‚Äî no migration (head stays `0055`, next free `0056`), no production code / contract / permission change.** **The guard:** `services/dcr/service.py::implement_dcr` preflights the Top-Management release gate SYNCHRONOUSLY (`services/vault/leadership_authorization.assert_release_authorized`, BEFORE `session.commit()`) for a REVISE/CREATE go-live ‚Äî because the real cutover runs LATER in the async `release_due` Beat sweep, which **swallows** the gate's 409 (`vault/lifecycle.release_due` catches `(ProblemException, IllegalTransition)` and skips). Without the preflight a leadership-gated DCR implement would commit the DCR as Implemented while the version stayed Approved (a stuck false-success ‚Äî the S-leadership-1 round-2 Codex P2). That path had ZERO DCR integration coverage (no `grep` hit for leadership / `assert_release_authorized` / `leadership_authorization_required` under `tests/integration`). **What shipped:** ONE integration test `test_revise_implement_blocked_until_leadership_authorized` (appended to `tests/integration/test_dcr_implement.py`) on a NON-singleton **OBJ**-typed REVISE DCR, both arms in one narrative: (1) flag on ‚Üí implement ‚Üí **409 `leadership_authorization_required`** AND `GET /dcrs/{id}` still `Approved` (the flip rolled back ‚Äî no false Implemented); (2) authorize the Approved version (`POST ‚Ä¶/request-leadership-authorization` + a Top-Management `verify`) ‚Üí the **SAME** implement ‚Üí 200 Implemented ‚Üí `release_due()` sweep ‚Üí version Effective ‚Üí `close` ‚Üí Closed (proves the preflight blocks, rolls back, AND does not over-block). **Care points / decisions:** the gate keys on `document_type.code ‚àà {POL,OBJ,MR}` + the flag + a version `verify` sig, so a PLAIN OBJ-typed vault document (`s5.drive_to_approved(type_id("OBJ"))` + the existing REVISE `_drive_dcr_to_approved`, **NO `quality_objective` row**) exercises it ‚Äî REVISE never trips the CREATE-only `create_target_managed_subtype`/`create_target_not_new` guards, and the generic sweep cutover has no managed-subtype coupling; **OBJ is `is_singleton=False`** so pushing it Effective is shared-org-safe (POL would be singleton ‚Üí 409-only, no happy path ‚Äî the owner's chosen "both arms on OBJ" over "blocked-only on POL"). The org flag is flipped ON in a `try`/reset OFF in `finally`, every assertion is run-scoped to this test's own ids, and `release_due()` is checked with membership (`in`), never an absolute global count (the global-sweep pattern of the existing `test_revise_implement_then_sweep_then_close`). Reuses the leadership helpers (`_set_leadership_flag`/`_assign_top_mgmt`/`_request`/`_my_pending_task`) cross-imported from `test_leadership_authorization` (aliased `_request as _request_leadership`, `_my_pending_task as _my_leadership_task` to dodge the `test_capa._my_pending_task` clash); identity wiring is consistent (same `keycloak_subject` ‚Üí same `AppUser` across `_auth`/`_ensure_user`/`_assign_top_mgmt`). **‚öÝ Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) the **ruff auto-fix hook STRIPPED the just-added imports as unused** (they're unused until a body references them) ‚Üí append the test body FIRST, THEN re-add the imports (the recurring "ruff strips a just-added import" trap). (2) **CI scopes mypy to `src` only** (`ci.yml` api job: `uv run mypy src`), NOT `tests/` ‚Äî so integration tests are NOT type-checked (this is why the pre-existing `no-any-return`/`attr-defined` "errors" in `test_vault`/`s5_helpers`/`test_capa`/`test_leadership_authorization` sit on green `main`); `ruff check .` DOES lint the whole repo (incl. tests). So a TEST-ONLY slice's local gate = ruff lint + format-check; mypy is irrelevant; the integration shards in CI are authoritative (the `-m integration` suite can't run on the owner's Windows box). (3) the discriminator: the **SAME** implement call is asserted 409 then 200 around the authorize step (same `_latest_approved_version` resolved both sides), so the verify-sig is genuinely load-bearing ‚Äî not a coincidental pass. **Test delta: +1 api integration** (`test_dcr_implement.py`, +103 lines); **web unchanged** (backend-only). ruff + format clean; **diff-critic CLEAN** (verified the 409 code is raised in exactly one place ‚Äî `leadership_authorization.py:187`; no earlier authz/SoD-2/FSM gate pre-empts it; the positive arm depends on the sig; flag-reset/run-scoping/`release_due`-membership all sound); **Codex CLEAN** ("Didn't find any major issues"); all 4 integration shards green. **Merge gate:** green CI (11/11) + 0 review threads + Codex clean + owner's explicit go. PR [#201](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/201), squash `8d9dd08`.

- **S-leadership-cx1** (close the S-leadership-fe deferral **CX-1** ‚Äî the server-computed per-document "request leadership authorization" capability) ‚Äî **a small, FE-enabling follow-up that fixes a real visibility gap; backend probe + 1 contract field + FE gate rewire. Chose A ‚Äî the gate already reads that exact payload for all three surfaces, so it's **1 serializer, 0 parent changes, no drift** across three independently-computed `capabilities.release` booleans; B would touch 3 cap serializers + 3 openapi schemas + thread a prop from 3 parents. **OpenAPI:** `can_request` added to `LeadershipAuthorizationStatus` `properties` **and** `required` (it has `additionalProperties:false`). **‚öÝ Codex P2 (the edge-finder again ‚Äî a CLEAN diff-critic + web-test-trap-reviewer BOTH missed it):** the probe built `RequestContext` with **`source_ip=None`**, but the PDP rejects an **`ip_allow`-narrowed** `document.approve` grant when `source_ip` is None (`pdp.py:134`), while the real POST gate goes through the PEP's `evaluate()`, which sets `source_ip=request.client.host` (`pep.py:94`) ‚Üí under an `ip_allow` grant the status returns `can_request:false` and the FE HIDES a button the server would allow ‚Äî **the inverse false-PASS (over-strict probe) CX-1 itself exists to prevent.** Fixed (commit `8fedd64`) by threading `source_ip` into the probe exactly as `pep.py::evaluate` builds it, so an `ip_allow` grant evaluates identically in probe and gate. **‚öÝ Note for a future session:** `ip_allow` is a **v1-deferred** predicate (its `guest_grant` carrier is v1.x; no grant carries it today ‚Äî docs/06), and the **sibling capability probes** (`release`/`edit`/‚Ä¶ in `_document_capabilities`, `_objective_capabilities`, `_mr_capabilities`) **share the same pre-existing `source_ip` gap** ‚Üí a separate, codebase-wide follow-up (thread `source_ip` through every capability probe, or leave it while `ip_allow` stays deferred); CX-1's probe now mirrors its endpoint exactly. - **S-leadership-1** (route the clause-5/6/9 leadership artifacts' release sign-off to a Top-Management pool) ‚Äî **the document-backed sibling of S-improvement-4, closing the named-enhancement gap the welded single-stage `document_approval` can't express (doc 10 ¬ß2.5, decisions-register R45).** **Why:** the Quality Policy (POL ¬ß5.2), Quality Objectives (OBJ ¬ß6.2) and Management Review (MR ¬ß9.3) are all `kind=DOCUMENT` and rode the welded single-stage path ‚Äî their approver pool is whoever holds `document.approve` (Approver/QMS-Owner); there was NO Top-Management gate on these leadership acts, and the welded `decide()` cannot conditionally route. **What shipped (BACKEND-ONLY, opt-in, additive ‚Äî the welded `document_approval`/`decide()`/`instantiate_approval` path is byte-identical, pinned by `test_approval.py`):** an org config flag `system_config.leadership_release_requires_top_management_authorization` (default **OFF**) that, when on, blocks **RELEASE** of a leadership-type doc until a "Top Management" member signs `meaning=verify` on the Approved `document_version`. The gate is enforced at the **shared `vault/lifecycle._cutover` chokepoint** (covers the direct `POST /documents/{id}/release`, the `/objectives/{id}/release` + `/management-reviews/{id}/release` wrappers, AND the DCR-implement go-live ‚Äî one insertion, no side-door) via a shared `services/vault/leadership_authorization.assert_release_authorized`. The sign-off routes through the generic multi-stage engine: `POST /documents/{id}/request-leadership-authorization` (gate `document.approve` at the doc scope; 409 `not_a_leadership_artifact` / `document_not_approved` / `authorization_in_progress` / `already_authorized`) opens a seeded `leadership_release_authorization` instance (a single Top-Management `PARALLEL`/`ANY` stage, `signature={meaning:verify}`) under a NEW `WorkflowSubjectType.LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZATION`; the decision rides the existing `POST /tasks/{id}/decision` (a new dispatch branch ‚Üí `decide_leadership_authorization`, which allow-lists `{verify,reject}` AFTER the keyless candidate-pool auth gate and forces `REJECTED`+skips siblings on a decisive decline). The COMPLETING `verify` mints a SINGLE `signature_event(meaning=verify, signed_object_type=document_version, signed_object_id=<version>)` bound to the EXISTING version row (NO own-table stage-event ‚Üí **no two-INSERT seam**, unlike CAPA/initiative) + a first-class `EventType.LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZED` audit (object_type=`version`); the document FSM is **untouched** (release is the separate act the cutover gates). Plus a `GET /documents/{id}/leadership-authorization` status read (`{is_leadership_artifact, required, version_id, authorized, instance}`). **Authority = Top-Management candidate-pool membership (NO new permission key ‚Äî R38; the self-scoped-task doctrine); the REQUEST reuses `document.approve`.** **Migration 0054** (head `0053‚Üí0054`): the two enum `ADD VALUE`s (`workflow_subject_type`‚Üí`LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZATION`, `event_type`‚Üí`LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZED`) in an `autocommit_block` so the new subject-type commits before the seed uses it (the 0053 ordering rule); `signed_object_type=document_version` + the `verify` meaning are **REUSED** (no enum adds there ‚Äî R2 closed-but-additive); an `ALTER TABLE system_config ADD COLUMN ‚Ä¶ boolean NOT NULL DEFAULT false` (mirrored in the ORM); and a seed-only `leadership_release_authorization` workflow_definition + its `leadership_authorization` stage **reusing the 0038 "Top Management" role** (NOT reseeded). Round-trips up‚Üîdown‚Üî`alembic check` clean; NOT-EXISTS-guarded downgrade. **OpenAPI:** the two new document endpoints + 4 schemas (`LeadershipAuthorizationRequest`/`Task`/`Cycle`/`Status`), `LEADERSHIP_AUTHORIZATION` added to `WorkflowInstance.subject_type`, the config flag on `OrgConfig`/`OrgConfigUpdate`. **The Codex saga (5 findings / 2 rounds ‚Äî a CLEAN diff-critic + migration-reviewer + all local gates missed every one; the edge-finder again):** **round 1 (3√óP2 + 1√óP3):** (a) the single-active guard only blocks NON-terminal instances ‚Üí a 2nd request after a COMPLETED authorization (pre-release) mints a DUPLICATE `verify` sig ‚Üí the `scalar_one_or_none()` replay re-derivation 500s ‚Üí fixed by guarding the request with `has_release_authorization` (409 `already_authorized`; **version-scoped**, so a NEW Approved version still re-requests); (b) the new `WorkflowSubjectType` must be added to the openapi `WorkflowInstance.subject_type` enum (`GET /workflow-instances/{id}` + `GET /tasks/{id}` serialize it ‚Üí a generated client would reject the response); (c) the decision result used `version_id` but `DecisionResult` is `additionalProperties:false` and defines `document_version_id` ‚Üí renamed the result key (COMPLETE + replay) + the tests; (d/P3) a decisive reject left `stage_state=PENDING` while forcing `current_state=REJECTED` ‚Üí set `stage_state=FAILED`. **round 2 (1√óP2):** the **DCR-implement go-live** of a leadership artifact runs the cutover only later in the async `release_due` sweep, which CATCHES the gate's `ProblemException` and skips ‚Üí `implement_dcr` would commit the DCR as Implemented while the version stays Approved (false success, stuck) ‚Üí extracted the gate to the shared `assert_release_authorized` (the cutover delegates) and **preflight it synchronously in `implement_dcr`** before scheduling `effective_from`/committing. ‚öÝ **Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **the ANY-quorum + outcome-allow-list pair from S-improvement-4 carry verbatim** ‚Äî allow-list `{verify,reject}` AFTER the keyless candidate-pool gate (else a generic positive mints a spurious verify; a pre-auth 422 leaks the task), and an ANY decline is NOT decisive in the engine ‚Üí force `REJECTED`+skip siblings in the caller. (2) **the release-gate read of the hot shared `system_config` row lives in the SERIALIZABLE `_cutover`** ‚Äî acceptable (the integration suite is sequential per pytest-split shard; a genuinely concurrent `/admin/config` write would 40001 a release, which is retryable), but a v1.x option is to read the flag pre-cutover. ## v1.x RENDER HARDENING ‚Äî pre-render linked-resource detection + gotenberg 8.34 (no migration)

- **S-render-1** (detect externally-linked Office resources before render ‚Üí R26 source-only, then adopt gotenberg 8.34) ‚Äî **closes a WORM/mirror integrity hazard the 8.34 bump introduces.** **Why:** gotenberg 8.34 changed LibreOffice conversion so external/local **linked** resources (`http(s)://`, `file://`, UNC `\\host\share`, drive/POSIX-absolute, and external-mode *relative* targets) still convert (HTTP 200) but are **no longer rendered into the PDF**. The worker (`GotenbergRenderSink`) caches any successful convert as the mirror's CONTROLLED COPY, so a doc referencing a linked logo/include/picture would silently cache an **INCOMPLETE** controlled copy ‚Äî a violation of "the controlled copy is a faithful rendition of the controlled source." So before any convert, the worker runs a structural scan; a linked source is marked **non-renderable (R26, doc 04 ¬ß11.4)** ‚Üí the mirror keeps source bytes + `no_controlled_rendition` instead of a lossy PDF. The gotenberg 8.34 adoption (declined earlier as Dependabot #157, pending exactly this guard) ships in the SAME PR. **100% BACKEND-ONLY** ‚Äî **no migration** (head stays `0052`), **no new permission key / endpoint / OpenAPI contract** (gate = `/check-api` + `/check-migrations` n/a). **What shipped:** a NEW pure-stdlib module `services/vault/linked_resources.py::scan_linked_resources(mime, source_bytes) -> LinkScan(has_external_links, reason)` (mirrors the `domain/ingestion/minhash.py` house rules: **pure / no-I/O / stdlib-only** [`zipfile`/`re`/`xml.etree`] / **bounded** [8 MB member cap, 4 MiB RTF/OLE prefix, 512-member + 64 MB zip budgets] / **ReDoS-safe** [no nested quantifiers, anchored bounded classes] / **XXE-closed** [refuses any `<!DOCTYPE` before the default non-fetching expat parser ‚Äî no defusedxml, D4] / **fail-open** [any parse error ‚Üí `LinkScan(False)`, defer to the normal render path]). Routing: RTF + legacy-OLE by mime; **OOXML/ODF by CONTAINER CONTENT** (a top-level `content.xml` ‚Üí ODF scan; `[Content_Types].xml`/any `*.rels` ‚Üí OOXML scan ‚Äî NOT a fixed mime allowlist, so every `.dotx/.xltx/.potx/.ppsx`/`.ott/.ots/.otp/.odg` variant the render path converts is inspected). **Hyperlinks are EXCLUDED** (OOXML `Type=.../hyperlink`, ODF `text:a`/`draw:a`, RTF `HYPERLINK` command) ‚Äî 8.34 renders a clickable annotation fine, and flagging them would source-only nearly every real document. **Doctrine direction:** a false-positive is SAFE (‚Üí R26 source-only, source always retained); a false-negative is the hazard (an incomplete cached copy). **Wiring (threading unchanged across all rounds):** scan runs in `GotenbergRenderSink.render` AFTER `_is_non_renderable`, BEFORE `_convert`; `RenderResult.reason` (new field) ‚Üí `_resolve_rendition`'s 5-tuple ‚Üí `mirror._metadata` writes `no_controlled_rendition_reason` into `metadata.json` for the auditor. The api process holds the no-op `LoggingRenderSink`, so this is worker/CLI-only (the S-dcr-3b rendering-is-worker-only invariant). **The 6-round Codex saga (the load-bearing story):** an inherently-imperfect heuristic over UNTRUSTED Office formats kept surfacing safe-direction edges ‚Äî Codex findings ran **7‚Üí6‚Üí3‚Üí6‚Üí3‚Üí5 across rounds 1‚Äì6** (severity decaying P1‚ÜíP2), and round-6 was 4/5 RE-RAISES of already-decided dispositions. The fixes that landed: hyperlinks excluded (r1); 7 false-negatives closed [INCLUDEPICTURE/INCLUDETEXT match anywhere, LINK only in field-context, case-insensitive, External-mode relative targets, variant mimes] (r2); **parse-and-concatenate split `<w:instrText>` runs** [Word splits `INCLUDE`+`PICTURE` across adjacent runs ‚Üí a raw-text regex misses it] + ODF embedded-subdocument dir-prefix membership [`./Object 1` stored as `Object 1/content.xml`] + footnote/endnote/comment story parts (r3); **route ODF by top-level `content.xml` first** + scan `.rels` before the budget break + **bounded RTF control words** between `\fldinst` and the command [`\fldinst \lang1033\rtlch INCLUDEPICTURE`] (r4); **independent per-category member budgets** [rels vs field-code parts each get `_MAX_ZIP_MEMBERS` ‚Äî fixes the symmetric starvation the r4 rels-first sort introduced] (r5); **scan BOTH ODF+OOXML when both zip fingerprints present** [OR-ed, short-circuit ‚Äî a crafted OOXML with a dummy `content.xml` no longer bypasses its `.rels` scan; supersedes the r4 either/or routing] (r6). ‚öÝ **Traps a future session MUST carry:** (1) **Codex caught ~17 real scanner edge-cases across 6 rounds that CLEAN diff-critic passes missed** ‚Äî on a heuristic over untrusted/adversarial input, the diff-critic is necessary but NOT sufficient; the adversarial PR reviewer is the real edge-finder. (2) **It does not converge** ‚Äî past ~round 4 Codex re-raises the same documented residuals (incl. the owner's own fail-open tradeoffs framed as findings); the discipline is to TRIAGE (fix genuinely-new high-value, respond/defer the rest) and ASK THE OWNER for the merge decision rather than loop. (3) **the auto-formatter strips a just-added unused import** ‚Äî `import pytest` added BEFORE its first `@pytest.mark.parametrize` use was removed by the PostToolUse ruff hook; add the usage first or re-add after (the recurring S-statusbadge-2 trap). (4) **rels-first ordering is a half-fix** ‚Äî preferring the most-reliable signal under a SHARED budget starves the other category; the right shape is INDEPENDENT per-category budgets. **Owner decisions:** (a) **KEEP FAIL-OPEN** for a VALID zip whose part is uninspectable (DOCTYPE-bearing or oversized member) or a truncated RTF/legacy prefix ‚Äî explicitly chosen over fail-closed (D1 trusted authors; source always retained ‚Üí worst case is an incomplete COPY for an uncommon shape, never lost content; a fail-closed switch stays an easy follow-up). (b) **fix-high-value / defer-rest** triage for rounds 4‚Äì6. **Deferred (named-not-faked) ‚Üí v1.x hardening:** RTF/legacy >4 MiB streaming/chunked scan with overlap (a marker after a huge embedded-hex picture is missed); a ZIP entry-enumeration cap (stdlib `ZipFile` parses the whole central directory on open regardless, so capping `namelist()` can't reduce the dominant cost without a custom incremental reader ‚Äî D4); a legacy-OLE **drive-path** (`C:\‚Ä¶`) marker (a raw-byte marker would false-positive on the ubiquitous embedded template/author paths every `.doc` carries ‚Üí needs structural CFB/OLE2 moniker parsing). **By-design (not a bug):** cached-rendition recheck ‚Äî a cached `rendition_blob_sha256` was produced by the pre-8.34 gotenberg (complete copy), and the single-host Compose deploy (D4) restarts the image + scanner together (no rollout window), so a cache hit correctly returns a complete copy; only a cache MISS runs 8.34 + the scan. **Test delta: +55 api unit** (new `test_linked_resources.py` = **53**: OOXML/ODF/RTF/legacy-OLE + variant mimes + corrupt/fail-open/bounded + every round's regression; **+2** `test_render.py` short-circuit/clean-convert) **+ 1 integration** (`test_render.py` linked-Office ‚Üí `no_controlled_rendition`); **web unchanged** (backend-only). Full unit `800 passed / 18 skipped` (Windows; 17 POSIX skips + 1 release-ceremony). **diff-critic CLEAN** on rounds 3 & 4 (round-5/6 self-verified + Codex-reviewed). **Merge gate:** all Codex threads resolved + 0 unresolved + green CI (11/11) + owner's explicit go. PR [#180](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/180), squash `97f4192`. (Rides atop the merged Phase-2 design-critique work + the fully-drained Dependabot queue; gotenberg 8.34 was declined as Dependabot #157 pending this slice.)

- **S-design-p4** (the design-critique **P2/P3 polish tail** ‚Äî the named follow-up S-design-p3 left open: the compact inline-state primitive + the Skeleton-list loader for the deferred idiom families, plus the residual Drift "Failing" glyph + the as-of-clock consistency gap) ‚Äî **100% FRONT-END-ONLY** ‚Äî no migration (head stays `0055`), no key/endpoint/contract; gate = `/check-web`. **Three new `lib/states.tsx` primitives (siblings of the four page-level ones from S-design-p3):** **`InlineState({kind, children, onRetry?})`** ‚Äî the compact in-tab / in-drawer / in-card `<Text size="sm">` idiom (`loading`‚Üí`role="status"` dimmed live region, `forbidden`/`empty`‚Üídimmed, `error`‚Üíred + an OPTIONAL inline "Try again" mirroring `ErrorState.onRetry`); **`SkeletonList({rows, height, gap?, label?, role?})`** ‚Äî N stacked `<Skeleton>` rows for table loaders, ALWAYS a named `role="status"` region (an `aria-label` on a roleless container is an axe `aria-prohibited-attr` violation ‚Äî hanging it off `role="status"` FIXES the prior nameless `LibraryPage`/`IngestionRunsPage` loaders); - **S-statusbadge-2** (StatusBadge Phase 2, critique **#1** ‚Äî the remaining badges) ‚Äî completes the canonical-status migration: the ~12 remaining per-feature badge components now ride the ONE `<StatusBadge tone label kind>` system (Phase 1 = `lib/StatusBadge.tsx`/`lib/status.ts`/`theme/mantine.ts`, #142). **100% FRONT-END-ONLY** ‚Äî no migration/key/endpoint/contract (head stays `0051`); gate = `/check-web` only. the orchestrator MUST reconcile to ONE convention (faithful-to-old-hue is the tiebreaker absent an owner design-call), and the diff-critic caught a SECOND (MR `Closed` gray‚Üísuccess) needing an owner call. (2) **StatusBadge couples the visible label + the aria-label from ONE `label` prop** ‚Äî a two-channel split (visible band name vs aria "Ambiguous") can't be preserved; keep the primary value in the label + put the secondary signal in a sibling caption, else you ship a contradictory glyph+label pill (`‚úì Ambiguous`) ‚Äî the `ConfidenceCell` lesson (ambiguity now rides only the `‚öñ ambiguous` caption). (3) **the spec target table can MISLOCATE a badge** ‚Äî migrate where it actually lives (compliance "Overdue" ‚Üí `CompliancePage`; MR `close_state` ‚Üí `ManagementReviewsRegisterPage`). - **S-optimize-1** (`/impeccable optimize`, critique **#5** ‚Äî power-user triage) ‚Äî the surfaces Mara/Ken live in most can now be triaged **in place**. **BACKEND (migration-free, additive contract) + FE across all six high-traffic surfaces.** Head stays `0051`, catalog 100; no new key/enum/endpoint/migration. **Backend:** `GET /tasks` LIST gains `subject_type`/`subject_id`/**`subject_identifier`**/**`subject_title`** via ONE query ‚Äî `Task‚ÜíWorkflowInstance` (inner; `instance_id` NOT-NULL) + `LEFT JOIN documented_information` + `LEFT JOIN dcr`, `func.coalesce(di.identifier, dcr.identifier)`/`coalesce(di.title, dcr.reason_text)` (NO N+1; `subject_id` is a polymorphic UUID across DISJOINT id-spaces so ‚â§1 LEFT JOIN matches ‚Äî CAPA/MGMT_REVIEW/OBJ are shared-PK subtypes of `documented_information`, PERIODIC_REVIEW/DOC_ACK act on a DI, only DCR lives in its own table). (2) `useDebouncedSearch` **clobbered an EXTERNAL `?q` change** (back/forward, a same-route link) ‚Äî because **react-router's `setSearchParams` is NOT referentially stable** (it changes on every location change), a write effect keyed on it re-fired on the external change with the stale local value. ‚öÝ Two insufficient fixes were caught by the new regression test before the right one: a naive `setQ(urlQ)` sync (a same-commit clobber survives), then a `debounced === q` guard (the unstable-setter re-fire survives) ‚Üí the landing fix **refs both `urlQ` + `setUrlQ` and keys the write effect on `debounced` ONLY**. Also folded in: the Audits **"Started" column sorts by `started_at`** (what it displays), not `created_at`. +2 web regression tests (943‚Üí945).

## v1.x DCR UI track ‚Äî clause ¬ß10‚Üí¬ß7.5 change control ‚Äî surfaces the built-but-UI-less DCR domain in the SPA (read spine first)

- **S-dcr-target-typeahead (A3)** server-driven debounced DCR raise target picker ‚Äî **CLOSES the last-named DCR ui-2a residual** (the target-picker large-list typeahead that S-dcr-ui-2a/S-doc-filters both explicitly deferred: the raise REVISE/RETIRE target `Select` in `DcrRaiseFields` fetched `useDocuments({current_state:"Effective"},{limit:200})` + filtered CLIENT-SIDE by label, so a target beyond the 200-row cap was unreachable for any org with >200 Effective controlled docs). **BACKEND + FE, migration-free, no permission key** (head stays `0055`, next `0056`; rides `document.read`); gates `/check-api` + `/check-contracts` + `/check-web`. **Owner design fork (asked in-plan, A vs B vs a discovered C):** **A ‚Äî add a top-level `q` to `GET /documents` (substring ILIKE)** ‚Äî chosen over **B** (the FTS `GET /search`: heavier `snippet`/`rank`/`clause_refs` shape + `websearch_to_tsquery` semantics, awkward for picking an exact doc by an identifier fragment) and **C** (reuse the existing `GET /search/suggest` typeahead ‚Äî already Effective-only + documents-only + `document.read`-filtered + `{id,identifier,title}`-shaped, BUT its `_SUGGEST_SQL` is a **prefix** match `'<term>%'`, so reusing it would REGRESS finding `SOP-PUR-014` by typing `PUR`, and broadening it to substring would alter the shared ‚åòK `CommandPalette`). ‚öÝ **#138 was NOT a typeahead precedent** (it added the boolean `has_effective_version`/`managed_subtype` *filters*; `ImplementCreateDcrModal` is still client-`searchable`) ‚Üí there was **no existing server-typeahead picker to mirror**; the only debounced-server-query precedent is `CommandPalette` + `useSuggest`. **Backend:** `list_documents` gains an optional **top-level `q`** (a sibling of `limit`/`offset`, **NOT** part of the `filter[‚Ä¶][‚Ä¶]` eq/has/gte/lte grammar ‚Üí `_FILTER_ALLOW` untouched, no `unknown_filter` risk) ‚Üí a case-insensitive **substring** `or_(identifier.ilike, title.ilike)` with pattern `%term%`, wildcards neutralised by a new **`_ilike_escape`** (backslash-first, mirrors `services/search/indexer.py`) + `escape="\\"`, **appended to the `filters` list so it ANDs** with the bracketed grammar + the `org_id`/`kind=DOCUMENT` scope. A blank/whitespace `q` adds **no condition** ‚Üí byte-identical for the Library + every other `useDocuments` caller. ‚öÝ **the `document.read` per-row authz filter is unchanged and REMAINS the security boundary** ‚Äî `q` only narrows the candidate window (UX narrowing, never a visibility change); the backend `_resolve_target` stays the submit-time correctness guard (a REVISE/RETIRE target must be a controlled Document, not a Record). **FE (`DcrRaiseFields`, the single shared component ‚Üí one change covers Raise + BOTH SpawnDcrModal seams [CAPA + MR-output]):** a 200ms `useDebouncedValue(search)` drives `useDocuments({current_state:"Effective", q: debounced.trim()||undefined},{limit:20})`; **react-query keys by `q`, so a slow earlier response can't clobber a newer one ‚Äî the hand-rolled stale-guard the `CommandPalette` needs is a non-issue by construction**; Mantine's client filter is disabled (`filter={({options})=>options}`, server already narrowed) and the redundant `kind==="DOCUMENT"` client filter is dropped (server excludes Records); a `Loader` `rightSection` while fetching + an `isError`-aware `nothingFoundMessage` (calm degrade, never crash). The **picked option is unioned into the data** so its label survives a later narrower search (the Codex stale-row edge), **gated on `selected.value === value.target_document_id`** so a stale pick goes inert the instant the parent nulls the target on a CREATE switch (no orphan can leak ‚Äî derived, no effect). The `CREATE‚ü∫no-target` biconditional (`isDcrFieldsValid`) + the RETIRE-clears-date logic are untouched. ‚öÝ **The reset story took a mutation-testing pass:** an initial `useEffect` to clear the search on the CREATE switch was a **genuine NO-OP** ‚Äî Mantine **remounts** the inner `Select` on the CREATE‚ÜíREVISE round-trip (and fires `onSearchChange("")` on the fresh mount), so the search already resets; it couldn't be discriminatingly tested ‚Üí **removed it**, and the only real lingering-state path (a stale *committed* pick after a CREATE clear) is closed by the `selected.value === target` union gate instead. ‚öÝ **Web test traps carried:** (1) the **debounce timing trap** ‚Äî `SOP-PUR-014` is present in BOTH the `q=""` and `q="PUR"` pages, so `findByRole(PUR)` is a FALSE gate (it matches the pre-narrow list); the real narrowing SIGNAL is `QMS`-gone **AND** `PUR`-present asserted in ONE `waitFor` (retries through the `q=""` both-present state + the in-flight loader blank); (2) the **ruff PostToolUse hook strips a just-added unused import** (the `_ilike_escape` test import) ‚Äî append the body FIRST, re-add the import AFTER (the recurring trap); (3) MSW fixtures `satisfies DocumentSummary`/`DocumentsPage` pinned to the real `_document` serializer + the real `{limit,offset,returned,has_more}` page envelope (the old fixture's `total` was fictional); (4) both the union test AND the orphan-guard test are **mutation-verified** (each fails when its mechanism is removed). **Reviews:** diff-critic = CLEAN; **web-test-trap-reviewer 2 rounds ‚Äî both findings the no-op reset effect + the uncovered `selected.value===target` union guard were resolved with mutation-verified discriminating tests** (the round-2 catch: deleting the guard clause kept the suite green ‚Üí added a "stale pick not re-offered after a CREATE clear" test that fails without it); **Codex CLEAN ("Didn't find any major issues. Swish!")** on the final commit. **Deferred (named, not faked):** true paging / infinite-scroll in the picker (a debounced typeahead + a 20-row page is sufficient ‚Äî a target is found by typing, not scrolling; the `document.read` row-filter + the `_resolve_target` guard keep it safe regardless); **diacritics-insensitive search** (ILIKE is ASCII-case-only ‚Äî `unaccent`/a trigram index is a v1.x refinement, the same note S-doc-filters carried); the **CREATE-implement picker** (`ImplementCreateDcrModal`) left on its #138 server-narrowed client-`searchable` form (its never-released-Approved candidate set is small + already server-narrowed ‚Äî the owner scoped this slice to the raise picker only). **Test deltas: +2 api unit** (`test_documents_filters.py` ‚Äî `_ilike_escape` leaves plain text untouched + neutralises `% _ \`, order-correct) **+2 api integration** (`test_documents_list.py` ‚Äî run-scoped via `owner_user_id`+salted titles: substring narrowing over identifier AND title / case-insensitive / identifier-vs-title isolation / non-match‚Üíempty; `%`-escaping doesn't broaden + `q` ANDs with `filter[current_state][eq]`; **CI-authoritative on this Windows box**); **web 1045‚Üí1050 (+5:** DcrRaiseFields 2‚Üí6 [debounced narrowing, re-show-clean-after-CREATE, union persistence, orphan-guard], useDocuments 6‚Üí7 [top-level `q` emission / omitted-when-blank]). **Verified:** `/check-web` (eslint + strict tsc + build + 1050 vitest, full run via `--pool=forks --singleFork`) ¬∑ `/check-api` fast (ruff + format + mypy-strict; only the known Windows `O_NOFOLLOW` baseline) ¬∑ `/check-contracts` (redocly valid; `q` documented as a top-level optional string) ‚Äî all green; **CI all 11 checks green incl. all 4 integration shards.** PR [#203](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/203), squash `ed4af1d`. **The DCR-UI track now has NO open named residuals.**

- **S-doc-filters** server-side CREATE-picker candidate filters on `GET /documents` ‚Äî **closes the CREATE-picker half of the long-named picker-pagination v1.x deferral** (the ui-2a/ui-4 first-page-only gap). + FE picker filters (`current_effective_version_id === null` + exclude OBJ/MR document-types via `useDocumentTypes`, FRM and other plain controlled docs stay valid) so invalid candidates never appear. the client-side filters could hide a valid page-2 candidate) ‚Äî the same v1.x limitation as the S-dcr-ui-2a target picker; **the server-side guard makes it safe** (validity is *enforced* regardless of the picker; `get_dcr_endpoint` returned `resulting_document_id`=the new doc for CREATE, `== target` for REVISE); ‚öÝ **the in-drawer modal/deep-link could NOT be driven via Chrome MCP** ‚Äî the documented `/dcrs` drawer-open limitation (ref/coordinate/JS `.click()` all no-op; subagent-driven TDD (4 tasks, per-task spec+quality review); **Codex 2 rounds, all 5 threads replied + resolved**; ‚öÝ **one CI flake of mine** (the F1-guard integration test gave the approver the `Approver` role instead of `grant_lifecycle`, so `drive_to_effective`'s release 403'd ‚Äî the releaser needs `document.release`; - **S-dcr-impact-annotation + the `CapaApprovalContext` a11y follow-up** ‚Äî two small follow-ups closing two named residuals of the (now-complete) DCR-UI track; both **100% FRONT-END-ONLY** (no migration, no permission key, no new endpoint, no contract change; gate = `/check-web` only ‚Äî head stays `0051`).
  - **#132 ‚Äî inline annotation of the 7 DCR impact dimensions.** The SPA could *view* a DCR's impact dimensions (the ui-1 read-only `DcrImpactTable`) but not *annotate* them; this wires the requester annotation through the already-built **`PUT /dcrs/{id}/impact`** (S-dcr-3b/-5 ‚Äî the service `annotate_impact` is a **partial merge**: it sets `requester_annotation` only on the dimensions present in the body dict, leaves `auto_populated` untouched, emits `DCR_UPDATED`, has **no FSM-state gate** ‚Äî it only requires the impact rows to exist; unknown dimension ‚Üí 422 `unknown_dimension`, an un-assessed dimension ‚Üí 409 `impact_not_assessed`, both unreachable from the UI which only edits existing rows). **Owner F-decisions (2026-06-14, after verifying the backend):** F1 ‚Äî the Annotation column is editable when **`impact.length > 0 && <capability> && state ‚àâ {Closed,Cancelled,Rejected}`** (matches the backend's permissiveness ‚Äî a requester/approver can refine annotations right up through approval, where they inform the decision; only the three terminals hide it, where an edit is pointless); F2 ‚Äî **inline-editable cells + one batch Save** (the Annotation cells become `Textarea`s; a single "Save annotations" button PUTs only the changed dimensions), not a modal. **The slice:** `lib/api.ts` `api.send`/`apiSend` method union widened `+"PUT"` (additive ‚Äî existing callers byte-unaffected); `useAnnotateImpact(id)` (`PUT ‚Ä¶ {annotations}`, **`onSuccess` writes the PUT response into the `["dcr-impact",id]` cache via `setQueryData(resp.data)`** + invalidates `["dcr",id]` ‚Äî non-optimistic, the server returns the refreshed rows); `DcrImpactTable` gains an editable path; `DcrDrawer` passes `editable={(impact?.length ?? 0) > 0 && dcr.capabilities?.assess === true && !["Closed","Cancelled","Rejected"].includes(dcr.state)}`. ‚öÝ **The editor draft-state design took FIVE Codex P2/P1 rounds ‚Äî the landed answer is "KEY the editor, never reconcile server‚Üîdraft with a render-sync effect":** **(1)** the original spec gated on the SYSTEM-scoped `can("changeRequest.assess")` ‚Üí Codex steered it to **`dcr.capabilities?.assess`** (PROCESS-scoped ‚Äî the ui-2b `_dcr_capabilities` precedent; a PROCESS/DOC_CLASS grant-holder is no longer hidden); **(2)** a na√Øve re-seed on every `impact`-prop change **lost the user's unsaved edits on a background refetch** ‚Üí preserve unsaved edits across an identical refetch (+ a fixture trap: order the MSW impact handler before the detail one); **(3)** but then a genuine server change (another user annotated) wouldn't surface on a **pristine** draft ‚Üí adopt fresh server values when the draft is pristine; **(4)+(5)** the converging fix that subsumed (2)/(3) and killed a **cross-DCR leak** (a dirty draft for DCR-A surviving a switch to DCR-B ‚Üí Save would PUT to the wrong DCR) and a **post-save stale window**: the read-only `<DcrImpactTable>` delegates the editable path to a child **`EditableImpactTable` keyed on `` `${dcrId}::${annotationSignature(impact)}` ``** (signature = `id=requester_annotation` joined over the rows). The key **remounts** (re-seeds a plain `useState` draft) on ANY genuine server change ‚Äî a different DCR, a content refetch that changed a value, or **our own post-save `setQueryData` cache write** ‚Äî but NOT on an identical background refetch (same signature ‚Üí same key ‚Üí edits preserved). So the editor holds a plain local draft with **zero server‚Üîdraft reconciliation**; Save computes `draft[dim] !== seed[dim]` and sends only the changed subset, disabled when nothing changed; a calm inline error on failure. Paired with the cache-write `onSuccess` there is **no stale-refetch window** (the saved values are in cache before any refetch, and they change the signature ‚Üí the editor remounts to them). **Reviews:** diff-critic + web-test-trap-reviewer CLEAN; **5 Codex P2/P1 rounds all fixed + threads resolved** (gate-scope, MSW order, dirty-loss, pristine-clobber, cross-DCR leak, post-save stale). **Live smoke (Chrome MCP):** edited one Annotation cell ‚Üí Save ‚Üí confirmed the PUT carried exactly the one changed dimension and the value persisted on re-open. **Test delta: web 842‚Üí852 (+10).** PR [#132](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/132), squash `e6b8256`. Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-14-s-dcr-impact-annotation*`.

The `/tasks` CAPA approval context skipped the page h2 straight to h4 (missing h3) ‚Äî the **same** heading-order skip already fixed in `DcrApprovalContext` during ui-2b. Bumped `CapaApprovalContext`'s levels h4/h5 ‚Üí h3/h4 + added a page-context CAPA **jest-axe smoke** (failing-first on the old levels) so it can't regress. full routes drive cleanly in Chrome-MCP whereas the drawer is flaky; a deep-linkable diff URL is auditor-friendly). **F4 ‚Äî REVISE + Implemented/Closed** (`resulting_version_id` is set only at implement, only for REVISE/CREATE; `DcrDiffPage.tsx` (the route ‚Äî header + back-link to `/dcrs?dcr=:id`, the mode toggle, the pinned-pair viewers, calm states: not-eligible/403-no-access/no-predecessor/load-error); the `DcrDrawer` "View visual diff ‚Üí" link in the Resulting-version field (REVISE + `resulting_version_id` + `target_document_id`); the `App.tsx` `dcrs/:id/diff` route; `useDocumentVersions` widened with an optional `{retry?:boolean}` (the S-web-8 `useTask` conditional-spread precedent ‚Äî existing callers byte-untouched ‚Äî so the diff page skips retries on a deterministic `document.read_draft` 403). ‚öÝ **Folded-in fix (pre-existing, surfaced by the live smoke; the reused `useVisualDiff` hook ‚Äî reachable from the doc-detail Compare tab too, NOT introduced by this slice's feature):** the worker-async poll could **stall on first mount** (it seeded the cache from the POST's `onSuccess setQueryData`, then gated the poll's `enabled` on a NON-reactive `qc.getQueryData(key)?.status==="Pending"` ‚Äî when the POST seeded fresh data at the instant `enabled` flipped true, React Query v5's `shouldFetchOptionally‚ÜíisStaleByTime` [`staleTime:0`] read it as "fresh" and SKIPPED the initial GET; no `refetchInterval` fallback ‚Üí it hung on "Rendering‚Ä¶" with zero GET traffic until a manual "Re-request render"). Fix: **the poll owns its own fetch** ‚Äî drop the seed, enable off the reactive `request.isSuccess` so the first GET runs against an empty cache (`data===undefined` always fetches). Then a **Codex P2** caught that `request.isSuccess` isn't pair-scoped ‚Üí on a pair change while mounted (navigating between `/dcrs/:id/diff` pages, or the doc-detail picker) the new pair's poll could GET an unrequested row before its own POST ‚Üí 404; fix: **pair-scope the gate** (`request.isSuccess && request.variables === url`, the POST's url passed as the mutation variable) ‚Äî proven by a **genuine failing-first test** (confirmed it fails on the pre-fix code; models the backend's 404-until-POST). ‚öÝ **Traps carried:** the authed page-PNG is `apiGetBlob`‚ÜíobjectURL (the only API-proxied binary in the SPA); every MSW fixture `satisfies <Type>` (incl. the inline no-predecessor `DocumentVersion`, a web-test-trap-reviewer nit); +1 test. **Reviews:** diff-critic = CLEAN ("safe to PR"; verified the succession direction vs `lifecycle.py:505`, the hook widening's backward-compat, the casts); web-test-trap-reviewer = CLEAN on both the slice and the useVisualDiff fix (the GET overrides are required + faithful ‚Äî they return the same status, not a silent Ready upgrade); - **S-dcr-ui-2a** DCR intake & early-state writes ‚Äî **OPENS the DCR-UI WRITE track** (the first write slice atop the S-dcr-ui-1 read spine). **100% FRONT-END-ONLY** ‚Äî no migration, no permission key, no endpoint, no contract change; **gate = `/check-web` only** (head stays `0051`). **F3 ‚Äî deep-link-on-success only** (grep-verified there is **no `spawned_dcr_id` latch** ‚Äî only `Complaint`/`ReviewOutput` carry `spawned_capa_id` ‚Äî and the MR‚ÜíDCR/CAPA‚ÜíDCR spawns are **1:N idempotent** with the link living only on the *DCR* side ‚Üí a persistent "View DCR" would need a backend "spawned DCRs" enrichment, declined; spawn rows are **Raise-only** and a successful raise `navigate("/dcrs?dcr=<id>")`); **F5 ‚Äî wire the `/tasks` DCR-approval candidate-pool leg in ui-2b** (a signing `DecisionCard`, not a key). **The new `features/dcr/` write surface:** `mutations.ts` ‚Äî `useRaiseDcr` (POST `/dcrs`, 201, `onSuccess` invalidates `["dcrs"]`), `usePatchDcr`/`useCancelDcr` (**`onSettled`** invalidate `["dcrs"]`+`["dcr",id]`+`["dcr-impact",id]` ‚Äî a racing 409 `dcr_not_editable`/`dcr_not_cancellable` self-heals the drawer to the real state, the `useNcrDisposition` precedent), `useRaiseDcrFromCapa`/`useRaiseDcrFromMrOutput` (the two `Idempotency-Key` spawns; `SpawnDcrVars` shared) ‚Äî all **non-optimistic** (the server is the truth). `DcrRaiseFields` ‚Äî the shared controlled (value+onChange) form core: a `change_type` SegmentedControl, a **conditional target-document picker** (a searchable Select over `useDocuments({current_state:"Effective"},‚Ä¶)` ‚Äî the hook has no free-text filter so the Select filters client-side; **hidden for CREATE, required for REVISE/RETIRE**, and switching to CREATE clears the target ‚Üí the CREATE‚ü∫no-target biconditional is enforced client-side so `create_has_target`/`target_required` 422s are unreachable from the UI), a significance SegmentedControl, a required reason Textarea, and an optional native `<TextInput type="date">` (no `@mantine/dates` dep) ‚Üí `proposedEffectiveIso` (UTC-midnight ISO of the picked calendar date, R8). `RaiseDcrModal` (standalone create + a `reason_class` Select that **omits the MR-reserved `mgmt_review`** ‚Äî the `RaiseCapaModal` SOURCES precedent), `SpawnDcrModal` (**parameterized ‚Äî takes the bound mutation as a PROP** so ONE modal serves both the CAPA-drawer and the MR-output seams; a per-mount `crypto.randomUUID()` Idempotency-Key; on success `navigate("/dcrs?dcr=<id>")`; its submit is labelled **"Raise"** to match `RaiseDcrModal` and never share an accessible name with its caller's trigger), `EditDcrModal` (PATCH-while-Open, seeded; the **MR‚ÜíDCR** seam ‚Äî **this closes the long-deferred S-mr-1/-2/-3 "MR‚ÜíDCR front-end" deferral**). ‚öÝ **Patterns/traps confirmed:** **Mantine v7 `required` fields inject an aria-hidden ` *` into the label `textContent`** ‚Üí query required-field labels with a **regex** (`getByLabelText(/Reason for change/)`); ## v1.x CONTINUAL IMPROVEMENT family ‚Äî clause 10.3 (0052‚Äì0053, R46/R2) ‚Äî opens the last named-but-unbuilt doc-14 ¬ß9 entity; a NON-‚òÖ own-table mutable-state workflow object (the DCR/R22 doctrine), NOT a shared-PK kind=DOCUMENT subtype; S-improvement-2 wires the OFI-finding + MR-output spawn endpoints (zero-migration); S-improvement-4 (0053) adds the signed, engine-routed Top-Management authorization ‚Äî **family COMPLETE end-to-end**

- **S-improvement-4** the **engine-routed, signed Top-Management authorization** (clause 10.3, R46/R2) ‚Äî **CLOSES the Improvement family** (the last, opt-in slice): the initiative's management-authorization now routes through the multi-stage workflow engine to a signed leadership sign-off ‚Äî the **CAPA action-plan-approval template (`decide_capa_action_plan`) ported to an own-table subject.** **BACKEND (migration 0053) + thin FE.** A Completed initiative's manager opts in via **`POST /improvement-initiatives/{id}/request-authorization`**, opening an engine workflow routed to the seeded **"Top Management"** role; when a member signs (**`meaning=verify`**) via `POST /tasks/{id}/decision` (a new `IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE` dispatch leg), the sign-off **closes** the initiative, binding the `signature_event` to the new `Closed` `improvement_initiative_stage_event` via the **pre-generated-UUID seam** (two mutually-referencing INSERTs, never an UPDATE ‚Äî the table is REVOKE-immutable). **`GET /{id}/authorization`** surfaces the cycle (the `GET /documents/{id}/approval` analogue). **Migration `0053`** = three additive enum `ADD VALUE`s in an `autocommit_block` ‚Äî `workflow_subject_type.IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE` (the engine subject ‚Äî ‚öÝ **the FIRST migration to USE a just-added enum value in its OWN same-migration seed**, so the autocommit-commit-then-seed ordering is load-bearing), `signed_object_type.improvement_initiative_stage_event`, `event_type.INITIATIVE_AUTHORIZED` ‚Äî + a seeded `improvement_initiative_authorization` workflow_definition (single Top-Management **ANY** stage, `signature={meaning:verify}`; reuses the 0038 "Top Management" role + the 0052 `signed_event_id` hook; NOT-EXISTS-guarded downgrade). **NO new permission key** ‚Äî the SIGN is candidate-pool (Top-Management) membership (the self-scoped-task doctrine); the request gates the existing `improvement.manage` @ PROCESS, the read gates `improvement.read`. **Contract:** the two endpoints + `WorkflowInstance.subject_type`/`Decision.outcome`/`DecisionResult.outcome` `+= IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE`/`verify` + `DecisionResult.initiative_stage` + `ImprovementInitiativeStageEvent.signed_event_id` + the two new auth-cycle schemas. **Owner decisions (asked in-plan):** `meaning=verify` (leadership verifies the realized benefit; reuses the closed R2 set ‚Äî **no new meaning**); **additive/opt-in** (the existing unsigned `Completed‚ÜíClosed` `/transition` close is UNTOUCHED ‚Äî honors R46's "10.3 mandates no per-initiative sign-off"); a **single Top-Management ANY stage** (proportionate; fails closed to `NEEDS_ATTENTION` when no member is assigned); **backend + thin FE.** **Thin FE:** a `/tasks` `IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE` decision arm (`DecisionCard` verify/reject maps + `InitiativeApprovalContext` + the `isDocumentSubject` negation extended `&& !isImprovement`), a cockpit **"Request management authorization"** affordance (suppressed while a cycle is pending, "no Top-Management approver" on `NEEDS_ATTENTION`) + `RequestAuthorizationModal`, and an `InitiativeStageTimeline` "verified by leadership" marker. ‚öÝ **Codex found 9 real findings across 2 rounds that a CLEAN diff-critic + migration-reviewer + web-test-trap-reviewer ALL missed (the edge-finder lesson repeats HARD on a signed/engine-routed slice):** **round 1 (5√óP2 + 1√óP3):** (1) the generic engine ANY quorum treats EVERY positive `TaskOutcomeKind` (approve/complete/acknowledge/verify) as completing ‚Üí a Top-Management caller could POST `{outcome:"approve"}` and mint a **`verify` signature** + close the initiative without a real verify decision ‚Üí **a `{verify,reject}` allow-list** (the PERIODIC_REVIEW complete-only precedent); (2) the unsigned-close FE race (Close rendered during the auth-cycle load window) ‚Üí gate close/request on the cycle query having **resolved** (`!isLoading && !isError`); (3) the required request body 422'd a body-less POST ‚Üí `Model | None = None`; (4) `verify`/`initiative_stage` missing from the Decision contract; (5/P3) the IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE decision branch didn't invalidate `["my-tasks"]`; (6) **a single decline left the cycle pending** (ANY quorum fails only on all-reject) ‚Üí **a decline is now DECISIVE** ‚Äî force the instance `REJECTED` + skip sibling PENDING tasks (the **`decide_dcr_approval`** precedent), re-requestable. **round 2 (3√óP2):** (7) the **unsigned `/transition` Closed must be 409'd while a non-terminal authorization instance exists** (the FE suppressed it, but a direct call would close unsigned + orphan the pending sign-off) ‚Üí a backend guard in `transition_initiative`; (8) `WorkflowInstance.subject_type` enum in openapi missing `IMPROVEMENT_INITIATIVE`; (9) the verify/reject allow-list must run **AFTER** `_assert_initiative_authorizer` (else a non-pool caller gets a leaky 422 instead of the 404-collapse). ‚öÝ **The diff-critic DID catch its own P1 pre-PR:** the original reject test assumed a single-member pool (the shared CI DB always has ‚â•2 Top-Management members from `test_capa` + this file ‚Üí one decline = PENDING, not REJECTED, under ANY) ‚Äî made deterministic by the decisive-decline change (#6). ‚öÝ **the PostToolUse ruff hook strips a just-added unused import** bit THREE times (re-add AFTER the usage edit ‚Äî the recurring S-statusbadge-2 trap). **Deferred (named, not faked):** document-backed leadership routing (MR/OBJ/POL sign-off ‚Äî the named-enhancement deferral persists); a distinct unsigned "Verified" FSM node (folded into the authorized close); `improvement_initiative_action` milestone rows; objective-miss / 9.1.3 auto-seed; an effectiveness re-loop ("CAPA's 10.2 job"); - **S-improvement-3b** the Improvement Initiatives **cross-surface raise affordances + dashboard line** ‚Äî **CLOSES S-improvement-3** (the web track) and gives the family its **two ISO ways-in**: **Raise initiative** on OFI/OBSERVATION audit findings (`FindingPanel`/`FindingsCard`) + ACTION/IMPROVEMENT management-review outputs (`ReviewOutputsSection`), plus a neutral **"initiatives in progress" `StatLine`** on the Home **ACT** tile (`ActCard`). **FE-only: NO migration / endpoint / contract / permission key** (gate = `/check-web`; head stays `0052`) ‚Äî it consumes the **existing S-improvement-2 spawn endpoints** (`POST /findings/{id}/raise-initiative`, `POST /management-reviews/{id}/outputs/{oid}/raise-initiative`). reverted `allForbidden`/`loading` to the **actionable reads only** (the init line is purely additive ‚Äî when no-access wins the ternary shows TileNoAccess and the pushed line is never rendered). ‚öÝ **the GAP-2 coverage test I had added (a diff-critic-flagged uncovered branch) had itself CODIFIED the bug** (asserting the init line renders when the 3 actionable reads are forbidden) ‚Üí flipped into a **regression guard** (no-access wins even when the filter-not-403 read returns data). **Lesson: a coverage-gap test written without re-deriving the CORRECT behaviour can entrench a defect ‚Äî the adversarial reviewer that NAMES a gap is not the one that says what the gap's RIGHT answer is.** (2) **DEFERRED (pre-approved)** ‚Äî the MR Raise button gates on SYSTEM `improvement.manage`, hiding it from a PROCESS-only holder the endpoint would authorize via the selected `process_id`; **identical to the sibling Raise-CAPA/Raise-DCR SYSTEM-gating** on the same section ‚Äî the proper fix is an **any-process capability** covering all three MR raise buttons (`usePermissions` can't ask "at *any* process"); replied + resolved on-thread. **Deferred (named, not faked):** no persistent View link (no server `source_link_id` filter; reserved-null latch); un-reserving `review_output.spawned_initiative_id` (a `0053` owner call); - **S-improvement-2** the Improvement Initiative **SPAWN endpoints** (clause 9.2/9.3 ‚Üí 10.3) ‚Äî wires the two ways to **raise** an initiative from an origin: **POST `/findings/{finding_id}/raise-initiative`** (OBSERVATION/OFI finding ‚Üí `source=OFI`, `source_link_id=finding.id`; **422 `finding_not_improvable`** on an NC, **409 `finding_superseded`** on a corrected finding; inherits the audit's auditee process per R28 ‚Äî `_auto_capa_for_finding`'s `plan.auditee_process_id`, not the soft `process_ref`) + **POST `/management-reviews/{review_id}/outputs/{output_id}/raise-initiative`** (ACTION/IMPROVEMENT output ‚Üí `source=review`, `source_link_id=output.id`; **422 `output_not_improvable`** on a DECISION, **409 `review_not_tracking`** unless `close_state==ActionsTracked`; emits `MGMT_REVIEW_INITIATIVE_SPAWNED` on the MR doc). **ZERO-migration** ‚Äî every seam shipped in `0052`: the `source_link_id`/`spawn_idempotency_key` columns + the `uq_improvement_initiative_spawn` partial-UNIQUE, the `MGMT_REVIEW_INITIATIVE_SPAWNED` event type + `improvement_initiative` audit object type, the `create_initiative(_commit=False)` compose seam, the `improvement.read`/`improvement.manage` keys (head stays `0052`, next `0053`). Both are **1:N + optional `Idempotency-Key`** (201 new / 200 replay via the `(org, source_link_id, key)` partial-UNIQUE), compose `create_initiative(_commit=False)` in ONE txn, and mint **no signature** (R43); the idempotent replay runs **before** the mutable close-state gate so a retry after the review closes still replays (the `spawn_dcr_for_output` precedent), with the `IntegrityError` rollback+re-query backstop (the `allocate_seq` IMP-seq increment rolls back with the txn ‚Üí no counter leak). **Owner decisions (asked in-plan):** MR-output eligibility = **{ACTION, IMPROVEMENT}** (the reserved `IMPROVEMENT` output type is exactly this ‚Äî broader than the CAPA/DCR siblings' ACTION-only); the MR back-link **`review_output.spawned_initiative_id` stays reserved-null** (1:N one-way via `initiative.source_link_id`; un-reserving the reciprocal latch is a future owner-flipped `0053` per the 0051 `spawned_capa_id` recipe ‚Äî so the S-improvement-3 MR drawer finds initiatives by `source='review' AND source_link_id=output.id`, like DCRs). **Placement (parent-domain modules):** `services/mgmt_review/actions.py::spawn_initiative_for_output` (beside `spawn_capa`/`spawn_dcr`) + `services/audits/service.py::raise_initiative_from_finding` (beside `_auto_capa_for_finding`); both routes reuse `_initiative`/`_scope_for` imported from `api/improvement` (the `api/mgmt_review`‚Üí`api/dcr` cross-router precedent; `api/improvement` imports only services ‚Üí no cycle). ‚öÝ **diff-critic CLEAN but Codex found 3 real P2s (all valid; the lesson repeats HARD ‚Äî Codex, not the diff-critic, is the edge-finder):** (1) **replay scope authz** ‚Äî the idempotent replay returned an initiative by `(org, source_link, key)` without re-authorizing its STORED scope ‚Üí a process-B caller could read a process-A initiative via a known key; **fix:** both endpoints re-enforce `improvement.manage` against the returned `initiative.process_id` on a replay (gate-2; the finding endpoint keeps its `require()` gate-1 + adds an imperative gate-2). (2) **superseded findings** ‚Äî a corrected finding (the audit close gate already excludes it) could still seed an initiative (an OBS later corrected to NC); **fix:** load the `Record` and reject `superseded_by_correction` ‚Üí **409 `finding_superseded`**, checked AFTER the replay lookup so a prior valid raise still replays. (3) **tracking-window race** ‚Äî the unlocked `close_state` read; **documented benign**, matching the `spawn_capa`/`spawn_dcr` siblings (the close gate reads only the spawned MR_ACTION task state, never spawned objects, so a just-after-close spawn is coherent) ‚Äî a uniform lock across all three is a separate cross-cutting call (deferred). **Contract:** +2 paths in `openapi.yaml` (inline `additionalProperties:false` bodies, `Idempotency-Key` header, 201/200; the finding 409 added in the fix round) + a new **`docs/15 ¬ß8.12b` Improvement Initiatives** section (the family had no docs/15 entry). **Deferred (named, not faked):** **S-improvement-3** (the SPA register/InitiativeDrawer/`improvement_stage` StatusBadge/raise affordances/PDCA-ACT tile); **S-improvement-4** (opt-in Verified benefit stage / mgmt-authorization routing); the reciprocal `spawned_initiative_id` latch (a `0053` owner call); a uniform spawn-lock across capa/dcr/initiative. **Test delta: +15 integration (`test_improvement_spawn.py` ‚Äî both origins √ó {happy, 422 ineligible, 404 unknown, idempotent replay incl. replay-after-close, authz deny}, the superseded‚Üí409, the cross-process-replay‚Üí403, `source`/`source_link_id`/process-inheritance, the MR-side audit event, no-signature, `spawned_initiative_id`-stays-null); api unit + web unchanged (backend-only).** Verified locally (Windows): ruff + ruff format --check + mypy `src` clean; redocly lint valid; import smoke + unit collection clean ‚Äî integration is CI-authoritative (ProactorEventLoop/psycopg), all 4 shards green across both commits. + the unknown-UUID 500 above. **Migration `0052`:** two fresh native-PG enums from the ORM `*_VALUES` tuples (the 0010/0040 no-drift rule) ‚Äî `improvement_stage` (Open/InProgress/Completed/Closed/Cancelled, title-case like `dcr_state`) + `improvement_source` (`OFI` uppercase to match `FindingType.OFI`;
