## v1.x MANAGEMENT REVIEW family ‚Äî clause 9.3 (0050‚Äì0051) ‚Äî flips the 9.3 ‚òÖ COVERED ‚Üí the ISO 9001:2015 ‚òÖ spine is feature-complete; S-mr-2 makes it usable in the SPA; S-mr-3 wires its ACTION outputs to the CAPA/DCR action systems; S-mr-pack adds the filed-minutes PDF export

- **S-mr-pack** the Management Review minutes pack (PDF) (clause 9.3 ‚Üí doc 13 ¬ß7.3) ‚Äî **closes the named S-mr-1 deferral "the rendered Management-Review-Pack PDF (v1.1)" (R45).** A *released* MR now exposes a downloadable, table-styled PDF of its **filed minutes** at **`GET /management-reviews/{review_id}/pack`** (gate `mgmtReview.read`, **released-only** ‚Üí 409 `pack_unavailable`; 404 cross-org) + a "Download minutes pack (PDF)" button on the MR detail page (Effective-only). **ONE new endpoint + the OpenAPI entry + FE; NO migration, NO permission key, NO enum** (head stays `0051`, catalog 100); gates `/check-api` + `/check-contracts` + `/check-web`. **Owner-approved shape (the central fork ‚Äî 3 coherent end-to-end options surfaced):** the **lightweight "printable view"** ‚Äî a *synchronous, in-request* **reportlab Platypus** render streamed straight back as `application/pdf` (NOT the heavyweight evidence-pack: no Celery, no status row, no reaper, no cache, no blob, no new EVIDENCE record, no WORM re-seal ‚Äî the released MR version is *already* the canonical WORM record; the pack is a derived rendering of it, like a controlled-copy). ‚öÝ **Why sync is legal** (the "API can't render" rule is about `GotenbergRenderSink` HTML‚ÜíPDF via the external service): a reportlab table-PDF over a few-KB JSON dict is pure-Python ‚Äî and the MR's minutes blob is `application/json` (`no_controlled_rendition`, R26) so Gotenberg *can't* render it, which is exactly *why* a self-render is needed. **Sub-decisions (all owner-confirmed):** source = the **released version's FROZEN snapshot** (`metadata_snapshot["mgmt_review_minutes"]`), not the live `review_input`/`review_output` rows; delivery = a direct `Response(application/pdf)` stream (no blob/cache); include an **e-signature sign-off block**; **plain footer** (canonical version id + the JCS minutes source digest, no verify QR); **table-styled** (Platypus `Table`/`TableStyle` + `Paragraph` cells, not line-rendered). **Architecture (3 focused units):** the PURE render leaf `domain/mgmt_review/pack_render.py` (`render_minutes_pdf(...) -> bytes` ‚Äî no DB/IO/`ProblemException`; deterministic via an **invariant canvasmaker** [`Canvas(invariant=1)` fixes the PDF `/ID`+metadata, no `Date.now()`] so a given released MR renders byte-identical) ‚Üí the gather service `services/mgmt_review/pack.py` (`minutes_from_snapshot` [409 on a missing key], `_resolve_names` [org-scoped], `_signer_label`, `build_minutes_pdf`) ‚Üí `repository.list_signoffs_for_version` (the version's `approval`+`release` signatures, OUTER JOIN to `app_user`, **`voided_by IS NULL`** so a rescinded sig never appears in a compliance PDF) ‚Üí the thin endpoint. **FE:** the authed-binary `getBlob`‚ÜíobjectURL‚Üí`<a download>` pattern (the visual-diff PNG precedent ‚Äî the only API-proxied binary in the SPA); the button gates on `current_state==="Effective"`. ‚öÝ **Load-bearing traps ‚Äî the pack must render ONLY frozen/immutable facts (else byte-instability / a 500 / PII):** (1) **render the FROZEN snapshot title, NOT live `doc.title`** ‚Äî `PATCH /documents/{id}` can rename a released MR, changing the "filed" pack's bytes; (2) **DON'T render `close_state`** ‚Äî it mutates ActionsTracked‚ÜíClosed *after* filing, so before/after-close would differ; (3) **NO email PII** ‚Äî `_resolve_names`/`_signer_label` fall back display_name ‚Üí **id** (NEVER email) because the pack is only `mgmtReview.read`-gated and the directory exposes only `{id, display_name}` to ordinary members; (4) **signer identity** ‚Äî a human with a null `display_name` falls back to the id, NOT "system"; only a true null `signer_user_id` (a Beat system release) is "system" (select `signer_user_id` to distinguish); (5) **`Table(splitInRow=1, repeatRows=1)`** ‚Äî a max-length (4000-char) decision in one cell would otherwise exceed the page frame ‚Üí `LayoutError` ‚Üí a 500; (6) ‚öÝ **the CI web Blob.stream() trap (a genuine CI-vs-local divergence):** the FE download test's MSW handler returning a `Blob` body throws `object.stream is not a function` during MSW's interceptor lookup on CI's node (which lacks `Blob.stream`) ‚Üí the download path never runs ‚Üí the click-spy fails; **return a `Uint8Array` body** (streamable; the consumer's `resp.blob()` still works). ‚öÝ **THE review lesson repeats HARD ‚Äî diff-critic was CLEAN but Codex found 7 real P2s across 2 rounds, all valid, all fixed:** R1 [signer-as-system, the 4000-char LayoutError, mutable close_state, org-scoped names] + R2 [frozen title, email PII, the frozen `compiled_at` row]; the merge was held an extra round because R2 included a real PII leak. **Live smoke (Chrome MCP, full route ‚Äî no `/dcrs` drawer wall):** the button shows on the released MR-GEN-003 + is hidden on an InReview MR; click ‚Üí `GET ‚Ä¶/pack` ‚Üí 200, no console errors; the rendered PDF **eyeballed** (metadata table incl. the frozen `Inputs compiled` row, attendees, 9.3.2 RAG-summary inputs, 9.3.3 outputs with resolved owner names, the sign-off block [approval + release; null signer ‚Üí "system"], the verifiable footer). ‚öÝ Native-Windows: integration + the full unit suite are CI-only (ProactorEventLoop / native crash) ‚Äî verified locally via ruff + mypy + targeted unit tests, integration by reasoning + CI. **Deferred (named, not faked):** external share-links for the pack (the S-pack-2 token machinery); the heavyweight **embedded-source-artifacts** bundle (the maximal evidence-pack shape ‚Äî the owner chose printable-minutes); + the standing MR deferrals (MR-minutes revision, `improvement_initiative` **(model now built ‚Äî S-improvement-1 / R46; the MR-output spawn seam is slice 2)**, Top-Management approval routing, broader-than-ACTION output spawning). **+13 api unit (6 render + 7 service ‚Äî incl. `_signer_label` + a 4000-char-row split test) + 5 integration (CI-only: 200/409/404/403 + a frozen-snapshot-AND-close_state-invariance proof) / +5 web (861‚Üí866, incl. an Effective-state jest-axe smoke).** diff-critic CLEAN; CI 9/9 (one web flake from the Blob.stream trap, fixed); Codex 2 rounds, all 7 P2s fixed + threads resolved; subagent-driven TDD (6 tasks, per-task spec+quality review; the Task-5 integration test on opus for CI-fidelity). PR [#136](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/136), squash `1d8eb05`. Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-14-s-mr-pack-minutes-pdf*`.

- **S-mr-3** MR outputs ‚Üí action systems (clause 9.3 ‚Üí ¬ß10/¬ß7.5) ‚Äî **un-reserves the two deferred S-mr-1 seams + lands the S-mr-2 Codex-#1 chip**: a *released* Management Review's **ACTION output** now drives the action systems ‚Äî spawn a **CAPA** (full backend + FE) or a **DCR** (backend-only). ‚öÝ **Two ground-truth corrections to the brief's framing (the "verify everything against code" instruction earned its keep):** (1) `review_output.spawned_initiative_id` and the DCR link are **DIFFERENT seams** ‚Äî `spawned_initiative_id` points at an `improvement_initiative` table that **does not exist anywhere in the codebase** (docs/14 ¬ß9 "deferred/unbuilt in v1"), so it **stays reserved-null** this slice; the DCR link is the `DcrSourceLinkType.mgmt_review` enum member (one-way, on the DCR's `source_link`, no reciprocal column). (2) **The DCR domain has ZERO SPA surface** (no `features/dcr/`; grep `/dcrs`/`change_type`/`source_link` across `apps/web/src` is empty ‚Äî even the existing CAPA‚ÜíDCR loop is backend/CLI/test-only), so a Raise-DCR *button* would spawn a DCR into a black hole ‚Üí DCR is scoped **backend-only** (a tested endpoint + the contract; the FE waits for a future DCR-UI track). **Migration `0051` (breaks the migration-free streak, head 0050‚Üí0051):** the FK on the EXISTING `review_output.spawned_capa_id` column ‚Üí `capa.id` (`ondelete=RESTRICT` ‚Äî the `spawned_task_id` precedent on the same table; acyclic so no `use_alter`; **name-mirrored in the ORM `review_output.py` or `alembic check` phantom-DROPs it**) + additive `ALTER TYPE dcr_reason_class ADD VALUE 'mgmt_review'` + the `MGMT_REVIEW_CAPA_SPAWNED`/`MGMT_REVIEW_DCR_SPAWNED` event types (`IF NOT EXISTS` in an `autocommit_block` ‚Äî the 0048 pattern; a from-scratch `upgrade head` already has them via the `*_VALUES` tuples ‚Üí they no-op there). Round-trip up‚Üîdown‚Üî`alembic check` verified clean on a throwaway PG16. **The CAPA spawn (`services/mgmt_review/actions.py::spawn_capa_for_output`):** ‚öÝ **uses `build_capa(source=CapaSource.review_output, _commit=False)` NOT `raise_capa`** ‚Äî `raise_capa` still 422s `review_output` (the generic `POST /capas` stays closed to it); `build_capa` accepts it, mirroring `_auto_capa_for_finding`'s atomic flow (build uncommitted ‚Üí set `output.spawned_capa_id` ‚Üí `MGMT_REVIEW_CAPA_SPAWNED` audit ‚Üí ONE commit; **no signature**, R43). It is **forced on-demand** (a CAPA REQUIRES a severity the ACTION output doesn't carry ‚Üí an auto-at-release spawn would have to invent one), exposed as `POST /management-reviews/{id}/outputs/{oid}/raise-capa` (gate `capa.create` at SYSTEM ‚Äî the MR has no process), and a **one-shot latch**: the output row is locked `with_for_update().execution_options(populate_existing=True)` BEFORE the `spawned_capa_id is None` check and held across `build_capa`+commit, so two racers serialize ‚Üí the loser 409s `capa_already_spawned`. **The DCR spawn (`spawn_dcr_for_output`):** **1:N + idempotent**, mirroring `raise_dcr_from_capa` ‚Äî `raise_dcr(source_link_type=mgmt_review, source_link_id=output.id, reason_class=mgmt_review, spawn_idempotency_key=<Idempotency-Key>, _commit=False)`; idempotency pre-check ‚Üí try raise+`MGMT_REVIEW_DCR_SPAWNED` audit+commit ‚Üí except `IntegrityError` rollback+re-query (the audit lives inside the try so a rollback discards it; an early replay returns before the audit ‚Üí no dup; `refresh` only on success); `POST .../raise-dcr` gates `changeRequest.create` at the target-doc scope (`_dcr_doc_scope`; CREATE‚ÜíSYSTEM), returns 201 new / 200 replay. **F3 ‚Äî the close-gate DECOUPLE is the ABSENCE of a change:** a spawned CAPA must NEVER block MR close, so `close_review`/`output_blocks_close` are byte-untouched (they key solely off the spawned MR_ACTION task state via the fail-closed OUTERJOIN), pinned by `test_spawned_capa_does_not_block_close` (CAPA left open + task DONE ‚Üí close 200). **diff-critic confirmed the RESTRICT FK can't block a legal erasure** ‚Äî disposal/WORM-destroy keeps the `capa`/`record` row as a tombstone (no `session.delete(Capa)` anywhere) and `delete_output` is `_require_draft`-gated, so it can never row-delete an output carrying a `spawned_capa_id` (spawning requires the post-release `ActionsTracked` state). **Codex #1 (the S-mr-2 chip `task_ae567104`):** `_mr_capabilities` computes `{release}` at detail-read time via the SoD-2 overlay ‚Äî reuse the existing `_release_scope` (already `enrich_release_sod_scope`-enriched) + `gather_grants`+`authorize(sig_hook=True, sod=sod)`, mirroring `_objective_capabilities`'s release branch ‚Äî and `_mgmt_review` gains an optional `capabilities` kwarg included **detail-only** (only `get_review_endpoint` passes it; list/create/etc. don't); the FE Release button flips from `can("document.release")` to `mr.capabilities?.release === true && state==="Approved"` ‚Üí no show-then-403, and the FE Raise-CAPA gate `can("capa.create")` matches the backend SYSTEM `capa.create` (no FE/BE gate desync). **FE:** `RaiseMrCapaModal` (severity-only ‚Äî the backend derives the title + sets `source=review_output`), the `ReviewOutputsSection` Raise/View-CAPA affordances on ACTION rows (Raise when `tracking && capa.create`; a `/capa?capa=<id>` View deep-link ‚Äî the audit‚ÜíCAPA precedent ‚Äî when `spawned_capa_id` is set; the modal conditionally-mounted so close resets it), and `ManagementReviewDetailPage` passing `tracking={close_state==="ActionsTracked"}`. ‚öÝ Adding the non-optional `spawned_capa_id` to the `ReviewOutput` TS type breaks every fixture lacking it ‚Üí patched in the same task to keep `tsc` green (`capabilities?` is optional ‚Üí `MgmtReviewDetail` fixtures are safe). **diff-critic = CLEAN** (1 MINOR: the two new OpenAPI summaries said "Gated mgmtReview.record_outputs" but the handlers gate `capa.create`/`changeRequest.create` ‚Äî doc-only drift, fixed). **CI green (all 9 checks); Codex post-PR raised 3√óP2 the diff-critic missed ‚Äî all valid, all fixed:** (1) the FE View-CAPA deep-link was gated on `tracking` so a Closed review lost it (gate only Raise on tracking; show View whenever `spawned_capa_id` is set); (2) `spawn_dcr_for_output` ran the close-state gate BEFORE the idempotency replay ‚Üí a same-key retry after close 409'd instead of replaying (moved `_find_spawned_dcr_for_output` ahead of the tracking gate ‚Äî the `raise_dcr_from_capa` precedent); (3) the contract `DcrReasonClass` enum omitted `mgmt_review` though raise-dcr returns it. +2 tests (FE closed-review-View + the after-close idempotency-replay integration test). PR [#122](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/122), squash `1a2a7ba`. **Gates:** `/check-web` green (lint+tsc+build + the full **761-test** vitest suite), `/check-migrations` + `/check-contracts` green; backend ruff+mypy clean + targeted unit tests pass ‚Äî ‚öÝ the FULL unit suite + `-m integration` are CI-only on this native-Windows box (ProactorEventLoop / native crash), so the 6 new integration tests run in CI. Deferred (named, not faked): **MR-minutes revision** (the S-obj-4 analog ‚Äî DEFERRED: a 9.3.3 record is point-in-time, you convene a NEW review rather than revise a filed one), `improvement_initiative` + `spawned_initiative_id` (no target table **at S-mr-3 time ‚Äî the model now exists per S-improvement-1 / R46; the MR-output‚Üíinitiative spawn seam is slice 2**), the **MR‚ÜíDCR front-end** (awaits a dedicated DCR-UI track), broader-than-ACTION output spawning, the MR-Pack PDF (v1.1), Top-Management approval routing. +~13 api tests (7 unit + 6 integration) / +7 web (754‚Üí761); subagent-driven TDD (11 implementer tasks, per-task spec+quality review, opus on the service core, diff-critic pre-PR). both response shapes byte-preserved (the endpoint serializes from the returned `rows`, the two preservation tests stay green). **FE ‚Äî a new `features/management-review/` module** (greenfield; mirrors `features/objectives/`): the `/management-reviews` register (gated nav entry in the CHECK cluster + flat routes), the detail/lifecycle cockpit (header ‚Üí the **9.3.2 inputs as calm RAG tables** ‚Äî a generic `source_ref` renderer + the OBJECTIVES_STATUS RAG band, **N6 no-charts / N9 server-RAG-verbatim**, doc-13 ¬ß5.2's gauge/donut vocabulary restated ‚Üí the 9.3.3 outputs grouped DECISION/ACTION/IMPROVEMENT, an ACTION showing its owner/due + a best-effort spawned-task state ‚Üí a Lifecycle `Card` reusing the shared `ApprovalStepper` with Compile-inputs/Submit/Release/Close gated on `current_state` + `usePermissions().can(...)` since the MR serializer carries **no `capabilities` block**, + the as-built close-gate codes `review_close_blocked`/`review_not_open_to_close` mapped to calm copy), the Draft-only outputs editor (`AddOutputModal` ‚Äî an ACTION requires an owner, client-enforced), and the create modal. **FE ‚Äî the `/tasks` MGMT_REVIEW arm** in the shared `ReviewApprovePage`: `MR_INPUT` ‚Üí **nav-only** (no decide affordance ‚Äî non-decidability is a FE contract since `decide_mr_task` doesn't gate on `task.type`), `MR_ACTION` ‚Üí a complete-only **`MrActionCard`** (one-click `outcome:complete`, per-mount Idempotency-Key, **no signature/no DecisionCard** ‚Äî mirrors `AttestationCard`); - **S-mr-1** the Management Review backend (clause 9.3) ‚Äî **OPENS the Management Review family** (mig `0050`, **R45**) and is the last ‚òÖ-node slice: **one released Management Review flips the 9.3 ‚òÖ checklist node COVERED, so the ISO 9001:2015 ‚òÖ spine is now feature-complete** (proven in integration). **The DOCUMENT-head thesis:** a Management Review is a **kind=DOCUMENT shared-PK subtype** of `documented_information` (document_type `MR`, the S-obj-1/R44 precedent), auto-mapped to clause 9.3 at create ‚Äî a **deliberate, register-sanctioned deviation from doc-14 ¬ß9's RECORD prescription** (only a released *document* earns the `current_effective_version_id` the compliance checklist reads at `services/reports/checklist.py`, so DOCUMENT is the only shape that flips the ‚òÖ). **The freeze** (the S-obj-3/S-rec-3 recipe verbatim): at submit, the convened review's minutes ‚Äî the auto-compiled 9.3.2 inputs *as-of* + the 9.3.3 decisions/outputs ‚Äî `rfc8785`-canonicalize the JSON-safe dict (hashed **bare, no preamble**) ‚Üí `finalize_worm` an `application/json` source blob (lands `no_controlled_rendition`, R26) ‚Üí the SAME dict into `metadata_snapshot.mgmt_review_minutes` via a one-kwarg `_snapshot` fold; the document then rides the **unchanged** submit‚Üíapprove‚Üírelease machinery, and **release** files the minutes as the 9.3.3 retained record. The operational lifecycle (doc-10 ¬ß7 Scheduled‚Üí‚Ä¶‚ÜíClosed) maps onto the **authoring FSM + a mutable `close_state` tail** (`ActionsTracked ‚Üí Closed`) on the satellite, outside the version. **Sign-off** rides the standard signed `document.approve`/`document.release` (**no new `SignatureMeaning`**, R2; SoD-2 submitter‚âÝapprover‚âÝreleaser binds because the submitter authored the frozen version); `attendees` jsonb is the informational roster (a dedicated Top-Management approval routing is deferred). **Outputs** are append-only `review_output` rows; an `ACTION` output (owner + due) spawns one `MR_ACTION` task at release on a `MGMT_REVIEW` workflow_instance ‚Äî ‚öÝ **diff-critic MAJOR (fixed): a per-action `stage_key` `"action:<output_id>"`** so the engine's distinct-approver guard never spans two actions of one owner. The new `MGMT_REVIEW` `/tasks/{id}/decision` dispatch leg (`decide_mr_task`, the `decide_periodic_review` mirror; 404-collapse non-membership) flips the task DONE; the **review-close gate mirrors `_audit_close_gate`** (pure `output_blocks_close`, fail-closed: an ACTION whose task is None/not-DONE blocks; a DECISION never blocks; the loader OUTERJOINs the spawned task) ‚Üí 409 `review_close_blocked` until every action is DONE. **Input compilation** (`compile-inputs`, Draft-only) runs the **six live org-wide reads** (objectives scorecard, audits, CAPAs/NCRs/complaints, KPI readings, compliance-checklist+overdue, drift) gated on the review **owner's** grants (the deterministic-pack `gather_grants`+`authorize` direct PDP path), **fail-closed per source ‚Üí an `available=false` gap row, never a 403**; the four sourceless 9.3.2 inputs + risk/opportunity (e) + improvement (f) are honest gap rows. **Cadence** is a coded default (`system_config.mgmt_review_cadence_months`=12) driving a daily Beat sweep (`sweep_mgmt_reviews`, mirroring `sweep_reviews` ‚Äî advisory-lock single-flight, org-scoped `open_review_exists` idempotency, NULL-owner + mis-seed honest degrades) that mints the next Scheduled Draft MR + an `MR_INPUT` task. The family **rides the already-seeded `mgmtReview.read`/`create`/`record_outputs` keys** (seeded + granted to QMS Owner in `0004_seed_authz.py`) ‚Äî **no new permission key, catalog stays 100, no R38 change**; `record_outputs` is `sig_hook=False` (R43 ‚Äî recording outputs mints no signature). **Migration `0050`:** the `management_review` subtype + append-only-by-posture `review_input`/`review_output` child tables (the `spawned_capa_id`/`spawned_initiative_id` columns ship **reserved-null** ‚Äî the CAPA un-reserve + the DCR `mgmt_review` link are slice-2) + the `review_input_type` (12) / `review_output_type` / `management_review_close_state` enums + the four additive `MGMT_REVIEW_INPUTS_COMPILED`/`_OUTPUT_RECORDED`/`_ACTION_SPAWNED`/`_CLOSED` event types (`object_type='document'` + `scope_ref=<identifier>`, R39 reuse ‚Äî no new `audit_object_type`) + the `MR` document_type seed + the `management_review` workflow_definition seed + the `system_config` cadence/owner columns. The `/management-reviews` router (create/list/detail/compile-inputs/outputs-CRUD/submit-review/approval/release/close/meta-PATCH) is contracted in `packages/contracts/openapi.yaml`. Imported legacy minutes remain kind=RECORD type `MGMT_REVIEW` (evidence; do not flip the ‚òÖ) and coexist. Deferrals (named, not faked): the four sourceless 9.3.2 inputs + risk (e) + `improvement_initiative` (f) as gap rows; the CAPA `review_output` un-reserve + the DCR `mgmt_review` link ‚Üí slice-2; the rendered Management-Review-Pack PDF ‚Üí v1.1; a dedicated Top-Management approval routing; MR commitment **revision** (first-release-only in v1, the S-obj-3 posture); the trailing **S-mr-2** UI + the Home "next review in N days" widget. +41 api tests. Register **R45**. Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-12-s-mr-1-management-review*`.

## v1.x OBJECTIVE REVISION ‚Äî revise an Effective commitment through the full cycle ‚Äî closes the S-obj-3 residuals

- **S-obj-4** Objective commitment revision (clause 6.2) ‚Äî **MIGRATION-FREE** (head stays `0049` ‚Äî `alembic check` round-trip pinned as a no-op; catalog stays 100, no new audit type [V-5: working-copy edits are unaudited by system-wide precedent ‚Äî the documents metadata-PATCH emits nothing; the version chain is the audit trail], no new signature meaning) ‚Äî **closes every S-obj-3 deferral**: commitment-revision-edit, **F-2's read-back switch**, the FE submit-gate widening, AND the generic byte-path guard. An Effective objective now revises end-to-end: `POST /objectives/{id}/start-revision` (**`objective.manage`**, a thin wrapper over the SAME vault `start_revision` ‚Äî T7 FSM + Redis edit lock + WorkingDraft + REVISION_STARTED; namespaced because the QMS Owner holds no `document.edit` ‚Äî the F-1 asymmetry repeats) ‚Üí `PATCH /objectives/{id}` (**O-1**: the satellite IS "the editable working copy frozen at check-in" ‚Äî its own docstring; Draft|UnderRevision only, `model_fields_set` explicit-null semantics [null CLEARS the 3 nullables, 422s the 4 required], policy_id mirrors create's Effective-POL check) ‚Üí the **revision-aware submit** (T9; ‚öÝ **the S-obj-3 freeze guard INVERTS on a revision** ‚Äî the latest version is v1's *Effective* one whose snapshot HAS a commitment, so `is None` would SKIP the freeze and T9 would IllegalTransition; the new rule is the pure `commitment_needs_freeze`: freeze iff latest is None OR latest isn't a Draft OR the working commitment ‚âÝ the latest frozen one ‚Äî an unchanged re-submit still dedups; optional `change_reason` body lands on the frozen version, significance always MAJOR; the start-revision WD is deleted IN-txn + its lock released POST-commit, the generic-checkin pattern) ‚Üí re-approve ‚Üí re-release (the UNCHANGED `_cutover` supersedes v1 ‚Äî INV-1; **micro-call B**: a unit-changing re-release resets `current_value` to NULL ‚Äî rag honestly `unmeasured` until a new-unit reading; a same-unit revision PRESERVES it, test-pinned). **The read-back switch (O-3, F-2 closed): every grading read resolves the GOVERNING frozen commitment** ‚Äî `list_objectives`/`get_objective` outerjoin `metadata_snapshot['objective_commitment']` via `current_effective_version_id` (a per-row PK probe, the drift_report precedent ‚Äî the feared N+1 never existed; register/scorecard stay ONE query), the `_objective` serializer resolves through the pure `parse_commitment`/`resolve_commitment` (‚öÝ snapshot values are build_commitment STRINGS ‚Äî re-parse to Decimal/enum/date before `rules.py` or it TypeErrors; pre-first-release output is provably bit-identical), and **`record_measurement` validates unit + freezes `target_at_capture` against the governing commitment (O-2)** ‚Äî a mid-revision edit can never leak an unapproved target into WORM evidence; ‚öÝ its governing read is `populate_existing` but **NO doc-row lock** (it holds the qo FOR UPDATE ‚Äî a doc lock would invert `_load_objective_doc`'s doc‚Üísatellite order); ‚öÝ **the `current_value` rollup now unit-filters** (review catch: an old-unit backfilled reading would otherwise re-roll garbage against the new-unit target, resurrecting exactly what micro-call B reset). Detail gains **`pending_commitment`** (the diverging working commitment, null otherwise ‚Äî detail-only beside capabilities/effective_from) + capabilities `edit`/`start_revision` (micro-call C: identical to `submit` ‚Äî all `objective.manage`, state-blind, split so the contract self-describes). **The byte-path guard (O-5): `reject_objective_byte_path` 422s (`objective_managed_via_objectives`) at FOUR writers** ‚Äî `checkout`+`checkin` service-level (FIRST statement, before lock/WD ‚Äî deterministic), generic `start-revision`+`submit-review` ENDPOINT-level (‚öÝ the guard cannot live in the shared vault functions ‚Äî the objective endpoints call them); reads stay open (the approver card needs `/versions`); ‚öÝ the dangerous bypass was generic **submit** (it skips the content-aware freeze ‚Üí could advance a stale/commitment-less version toward an Effective-OBJ-with-no-commitment). **FE**: Start-revision (Effective+caps), the **calm revision panel** REPLACING the stepper while UnderRevision (O-6a ‚Äî the latest-instance read still returns v1's completed cycle, which would render "Not yet released" against a doc that IS released), `EditCommitmentModal` (seeds **`pending_commitment ?? main fields`** ‚Äî the main fields are GOVERNING, seeding from them would silently revert a prior edit; full-body PATCH, explicit-null clears; warn-not-block BandPreview), `ProposedRevisionCard` (was‚Üínow of changed fields only), register **state chips on non-Effective rows** (O-6c ‚Äî fixes the pre-existing Draft-invisibility; `ObjectiveState` is now a `DocumentCurrentState` alias so the shared StateBadge just works), and the `/tasks` approver card's **was‚Üínow delta** (O-6b) + the previously comment-only newest-first `.find` pin is now a **two-commitment-version regression test**. ‚öÝ Review catches worth carrying: (1) the approver's "was" must be **the newest commitment-bearing version that is `version_state=Effective`, NEVER `[1]` blindly** ‚Äî a changes_requested‚ÜíPATCH‚Üíre-submit cycle leaves a commitment-BEARING orphan Draft at [1], and on a first-release cycle there is no governing version at all (a phantom "revision" framing) ‚Äî version-state-filtered + orphan-regression-pinned; (2) the edit modal must **never let an errored/loading policy read DECIDE `policy_id`** ‚Äî preserve the seeded link (the S-home-1 lesson applied to WRITES, not just copy; the create modal was safe only because no link existed to lose); (3) MSW capabilities fixtures can never split submit/edit/start_revision (one server-side answer). Deferrals carried (named-not-faked): abandon-revision (T8 ‚Äî MVP-deferred for ALL documents; an UnderRevision objective only moves forward), approval-cycle history (latest-instance only ‚Äî v1's cycle leaves the stepper at re-submit; the audit trail holds it), the post-commit lock-release crash window (‚â§8h TTL, parity with generic checkin), mgmt-review routing, Process-Owner `objective.manage`, KPI charts (N6), org-tunable RAG (v1.x), title edits (document metadata, not commitment). +18 api tests (5 unit [incl. the freeze-matrix + strict-parse pins], 14-test `test_objective_revision.py` integration file ‚àí the deleted open-seam pin), +24 web (679‚Üí703); subagent-driven TDD (14 implementer/review dispatches; the two non-trivial review catches above were found by per-task quality reviews). **The Quality Objectives family is now revision-complete.** Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-12-s-obj-4-commitment-revision*`.

## v1.x OBJECTIVE LIFECYCLE ‚Äî release a Quality Objective to Effective ‚Äî flips the 6.2 ‚òÖ COVERED

- **S-obj-3** Objective lifecycle & release (clause 6.2) ‚Äî **MIGRATION-FREE backend-led slice** (head stays `0049`, catalog stays 100, R2 closed ‚Äî no new key/meaning/table) that **closes the S-obj-1/2/S-home-1 deferral**: objectives stop being permanently-Draft, and one released OBJ flips the **6.2 ‚òÖ checklist node COVERED** (proven live: PARTIAL‚ÜíCOVERED, `effective_count` 0‚Üí1). **The freeze** (the S-rec-3 `form_template` recipe): `domain/objectives/commitment.py::build_commitment` makes the canonical commitment dict (target/unit/direction/due/threshold/baseline/policy_id ‚Äî **decimals as STRINGS**, never float; `current_value` stays OUTSIDE the version) ‚Üí `rfc8785` ‚Üí `put_staging_bytes`/`finalize_worm` (`application/json` ‚Üí `no_controlled_rendition` R26, no garbage CONTROLLED COPY) ‚Üí a Draft `document_version` whose `metadata_snapshot.objective_commitment` is the **SAME dict** (bytes‚â°snapshot); the shared `_snapshot` extended by **ONE optional kwarg**, never branched (ordinary docs byte-identical, unit-pinned). ‚öÝ Unlike `checkin_form_schema`, `checkin_objective_commitment` **FLUSHES, never commits** ‚Äî it is a sub-step of `submit_objective_for_review` (409-unless-Draft ‚Üí freeze-**iff-no-version** [a request_changes‚Üíre-submit advances the SAME Draft version ‚Äî T3 reverts version_state, so T2's from-state check holds] ‚Üí T2 ‚Üí `instantiate_approval` ‚Üí audit, ONE txn); and it **flushes BEFORE `_emit`** (the `default=uuid.uuid4` id is a FLUSH-time default ‚Äî the legacy `checkin`/`checkin_form_schema` emit pre-flush and their CHECKIN audit rows carried no real version id ‚Äî FIXED in-PR: flush-before-emit in both + an object_id regression pin; historic NULL rows stay, the chain is append-only). **The lifecycle rides the proven machinery unchanged**: the approval is the DOCUMENT `/tasks` decide leg (`instantiate_approval` hardcodes subject_type=DOCUMENT; `document.approve` + SoD author‚âÝapprover ‚Äî the submitter IS the frozen version's `author_user_id`), release is the shared SERIALIZABLE `_cutover` via `POST /objectives/{id}/release` (imperative `enforce("document.release", sig_hook=True)` over the `enrich_release_sod_scope`-enriched scope ‚Äî SoD-2 author-can't-release proven by integration test; ‚öÝ `release()` commits in its OWN session ‚Üí **`session.expire_all()` before the re-read** or the serializer reads the pre-release identity map). Submit gates on **`objective.manage`** (ownership puts it up for review; the cryptographic sign-offs stay document.*) ‚Äî keeps the slice migration-free (no role-grant seed). Reads: `GET /objectives/{id}/approval` (**`objective.read`**-gated ‚Äî the QMS Owner may hold no `document.read`; local `_approval_instance`/`_task` serializers field-equivalent to workflow.py's), detail-only `capabilities {submit,release}` + `effective_from` (‚öÝ a DETAIL response **always carries `effective_from`, null until Effective** ‚Äî the `_document` precedent; list/scorecard rows omit both ‚Äî and the additions were **load-bearing in the contract**: `Objective` has `additionalProperties:false`, so an undocumented key would 422 schema validation), `GET /objectives/policy` (the Effective POL `{id,identifier,title}|null` ‚Äî **declared BEFORE `/{objective_id}`**, the scorecard/S-pack-2 route-order lesson, in FastAPI AND MSW). ‚öÝ The S-drift-1 trap bit TWICE: the submit handler's `for_update` load needs `populate_existing` on **BOTH** the doc AND the `quality_objective` satellite (the authz resolver identity-mapped both; a stale satellite would freeze yesterday's commitment once a commitment-edit path exists). **FE**: the detail page's Lifecycle card (Submit gated `caps.submit`+Draft ¬∑ the REUSED `ApprovalStepper` ‚Äî `ObjectiveState` is structurally `DocumentCurrentState` so no cast ¬∑ Release gated `caps.release`+Approved ¬∑ AuthorActions-style error Alert); the `/tasks` DOCUMENT leg renders **`ObjectiveCommitmentContext`** (the frozen commitment card) instead of the redline ‚Äî detection keys on **`metadata_snapshot.objective_commitment` presence, never the document type** (forms=`field_schema`, plain docs=neither; versions are newest-first by `version_seq DESC` so `.find(Boolean)` picks the InReview commitment in the revision era); the create modal's **policy checkbox** (`useEffectivePolicy`; sends `policy_id` only when checked). ‚öÝ **diff-critic MINOR (fixed, the S-home-1 green-on-error class):** the modal's policy fallback claimed the positive "No effective Quality Policy yet ‚Äî you can link one later" on a LOADING/ERRORED read, and "later" was a false promise (the commitment freezes `policy_id` at submit; no edit path) ‚Üí branch on `isError` ‚Üí neutral "Couldn't load the Quality Policy ‚Äî you can still create the objective" + the no-policy copy now says "the link is optional". Live smoke (worker heredoc, service-layer): create‚Üísubmit‚Üíapprove‚Üírelease = Effective + the exact frozen snapshot + 6.2 COVERED + `approval`+`release` signatures on the version. Deferrals (named-not-faked): **commitment-revision-edit** (first-release only in v1 ‚Äî no commitment-edit endpoint, so UnderRevision re-freeze is pointless; when it lands, ALSO switch Effective-objective reads to the frozen snapshot [F-2's deferred half] and widen the FE Submit gate); ‚öÝ **the generic `checkout`/`checkin` byte-path is an unguarded seam on an OBJ** (no v1 UI offers it, but a generic checkin on a Draft OBJ would suppress the freeze, and on an Effective OBJ a v2 byte-checkin would show a stale v1 commitment to the approver ‚Äî guard it when the revision slice lands); management-review approval routing (the OBJ rides the generic `document_approval` pool); Process-Owner `objective.manage`. +14 api tests (4 unit + 10 integration), +18 web tests (659‚Üí677); subagent-driven TDD (10 dispatches, per-dispatch spec+quality review; diff-critic = 1 MINOR, fixed). **The Quality Objectives family is now lifecycle-complete.** Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-11-s-obj-3-objective-lifecycle*`.

## v1.x PDCA DASHBOARD ‚Äî the QMS Health home wheel (front-end-only) ‚Äî CLOSES the v1 web track

- **S-home-1** the PDCA Home dashboard (QMS Health, doc 11 ¬ß5.1) ‚Äî **the v1 web-track FINALE; FRONT-END ONLY** (no migration/key/endpoint/contract; head stays `0049`, catalog stays 100). Replaces the `HomePage.tsx` placeholder with the calm four-quadrant **PLAN/DO/CHECK/ACT wheel** (the doc-11 "nav of four labeled regions" ‚Äî a 2√ó2 of `QuadrantCard`s, **NOT a donut**) composing **already-shipped reads** client-side, each tile degrading independently. Surfaces: a header **`HealthSummary`** band (‚òÖ mandatory coverage `{covered} / {total} mandatory items current` from `useComplianceChecklist().rollup`, a `coverageRag` badge, the **N9 microcopy** "status against configured thresholds ‚Äî not a compliance verdict" ‚Äî there is NO "Certified-ready" verdict; the whole band drills to `/compliance`); **PLAN** (objectives on-target `{on_target} / {total}` + `by_rag` from `useObjectiveScorecard` [server RAG **read verbatim, never recomputed** ‚Äî N9] + `rollup.overdue_review`; ‚Üí `/objectives`); **DO** (mirror & blob integrity from `useDriftStatus` [`driftRag` over `scans.{MIRROR,BLOB_REHASH}.status` + `blob_coverage.failing`] + superseded-copies count + `useAckCount`; ‚Üí `/drift`); **CHECK** (open audits `state!=="Closed"` from `useAudits` + `{covered} / {total}` coverage; ‚Üí `/audits`); **ACT** (open CAPAs `close_state‚àâ{Closed,Rejected}` + NCRs `disposition===null` + complaints `spawned_capa_id===null`; ‚Üí `/capa`); and a **`MyTasksRail`** (the self-scoped `useMyTasks` = `GET /tasks?assignee=me&state=PENDING`, count + top-3 by `due_at`, showing **type + action + due, NOT the doc name** ‚Äî the LIST omits `subject_*`, the `useAckCount` precedent; ‚Üí `/tasks`). Pure `rag.ts` rules (`planObjectivesRag`/`coverageRag`/`overdueRag`/`countRag`/`driftRag`/`worstRag` + the count filters), unit-tested; **tile RAG = `worstRag` of only the VISIBLE RAG-bearing signals** (a forbidden/errored read contributes no RAG, so it can never drag a tile red; the informational counts ‚Äî audits/superseded/acks ‚Äî never colour a tile). Per-signal & per-tile **calm-403 degrade** (each read's `forbidden` flag, `retry:false`): a forbidden signal omits its line, an all-forbidden tile shows `TileNoAccess`, the wheel never crashes. Under the **bare `demo` login only DO + My-Tasks light up** (`drift.read` + self-scoped tasks); the rest need SYSTEM overrides on the live `app_user` row (org **AHT**). ‚öÝ **diff-critic MINOR (fixed):** DoCard's empty-state fallback is reachable ONLY on a drift **non-403 error** with zero acks (a drift success always pushes the integrity line; forbidden+0-acks hits `TileNoAccess`) ‚Äî so it must render a **neutral "Couldn't load this section.", NOT a green "You're all caught up."** (which painted a green health state over an errored integrity read); fixed to match the three sibling cards + a regression test. Deferrals (named-not-faked): the precise **open-NC findings count** (no org-wide findings endpoint ‚Äî per-audit only; the findings payload can't see the linked CAPA's close-state ‚Äî owner-chosen defer); **"next management review in N days"** (no `ManagementReview` entity), **"high risks open"** (no surfaced `risk_opportunity` register), **"documents pending approval" org-wide** (no endpoint ‚Äî personal approvals live in the rail); the **6.2 ‚òÖ checklist node stays not-COVERED** (objective lifecycle/release is unwired, so CHECK coverage honestly reads e.g. 18/20 ‚Äî not papered over); **KPI charts/sparklines** (N6); **org-configurable RAG thresholds** (v1.x ‚Äî coded defaults ship now); the **density control + Process-Map header chrome** (no density system in v1). ‚öÝ Web traps re-confirmed: the `findByRole` on a card resolves on the immediately-rendered frame while the data line is still a skeleton ‚Üí the **first content assertion must `waitFor`**; the `MyTasksRail` heading + "See all my tasks" both match `/my tasks/i` ‚Üí assert with `getAllByText`; the decorative `‚Üí`/`See all` arrows are `aria-hidden` so they stay out of a link's accessible name. +32 web tests (627‚Üí659); subagent-driven TDD (per-phase spec + quality review; final **diff-critic = 1 MINOR, fixed**). **The v1 web track is now feature-complete.** Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-11-s-home-1-pdca-dashboard*`.

## v1.x OBJECTIVES family ‚Äî Quality Objectives backend (clause 6.2) (0049) ‚Üí the UI tail (front-end-only) ‚Üí S-obj-charts adds the KPI trend chart (closes the S-obj-2 "trend charts" deferral)

the ‚åòK-palette/redline house pattern); **detail-page only** (register sparklines = Fork B, deferred ‚Äî needs the per-objective series in the list response); **server-side RAG points** (additive serializer field, the rule stays server-side per N9). **The SVG:** reverses the newest-first series to oldest-left; `Number()`-parses the decimal strings; y-domain `[min,max]` over values‚à™targets padded ~8%, **never forced to 0**, degenerate-domain guarded; categorical x (thinned period labels); value polyline only at n‚â•2; a full-width horizontal target line at n=1; per-point circles filled via a LOCAL `RAG_FILL` of `var(--mantine-color-*-6)` (the `BandPreview` `ZONE_COLOR` idiom ‚Äî CSS vars, NOT the `labels.ts` `RAG_COLOR` name tokens); native `<title>` tooltips; `role="img"` + a meaningful `aria-label`. ‚öÝ **THE load-bearing correction (Codex ‚ë¢, against my own spec):** the "frozen verdict" is **PARTIAL** ‚Äî **only `target_at_capture` is frozen**; `direction`/`at_risk_threshold` come from the governing commitment, so a commitment revision that changes **DIRECTION or threshold re-grades historical readings** (a HIGHER‚ÜíLOWER flip rewrites green/red, not just the amber band ‚Äî my spec's "green/red stays exact" was WRONG). **Owner decision: keep migration-free; treat per-reading RAG as DESCRIPTIVE (N9), not an immutable stored verdict** ‚Äî documented honestly in the spec caveat + the `_measurement` comment; truly freezing the verdict needs `direction_at_capture`+`threshold_at_capture` columns (a migration that also **can't retroactively** freeze pre-existing readings) ‚Üí **named v1.x deferral**. ‚öÝ **Other traps a future session must carry:** **(1)** a chart that **filters its input** (same-unit ‚Äî a unit-changing revision leaves old-unit rows incomparable on one axis; the chart filters to the governing unit, **mirroring the backend same-unit rollup**, with the off-unit rows staying in the table) must still **EXPLAIN an empty result, never `return null` silently** (Codex ‚ë£ ‚Äî when ALL readings are off-unit, render "in a previous unit ‚Äî no comparable trend"); **(2)** **NEVER round a displayed reading value** (`toFixed` made `94.999`‚Üí"95"/looking on-target while graded amber, and `0.005`‚Üí"0") ‚Äî render the **raw decimal string** in tooltips + the aria-label summary; reserve rounding for **computed axis ticks** with **adaptive precision from the domain span** (Codex ‚ë§); **(3)** a one-coordinate `<polyline>` renders nothing ‚Äî a single-reading target needs a full-width 2-point segment (Codex ‚ë°). **Reviews:** diff-critic + web-test-trap-reviewer **CLEAN**; subagent-driven TDD (3 implementers [backend + chart parallel, integration after] + 3 per-task quality reviews, all clean); **Codex 5 real findings over 2 rounds (3√óP2 round 1: same-unit filter / single-reading target / the ‚ë¢ caveat-correction; P3+P2 round 2: ‚ë£ off-unit-explanation [introduced by my round-1 filter] / ‚ë§ raw-decimal labels), all fixed + threads resolved, round 3 clean** ("Didn't find any major issues") ‚Äî the Codex-finds-what-the-CLEAN-diff-critic-misses lesson REPEATS (incl. correcting a spec claim). **Live smoke (full PASS, OBJ-GEN-005):** the chart rendered an amber/amber/red/green spread with a stepping target line (98‚Üí99), the **frozen-verdict semantics showed live** (96-vs-frozen-98 = amber, not 96-vs-governing-99), and recording a measurement via the UI **live-updated** the chart 4‚Üí5 points; no console errors. **Test deltas: +13 api unit** (`test_objective_measurement_rag.py` ‚Äî rag across both directions √ó green/amber/red √ó None-threshold) **+ 5 api integration** (incl. the **frozen-verdict proof**: an old reading grades against its `target_at_capture`, not the revised governing target; CI-only on this Windows box, green on the 4 integration shards); **web 877‚Üí880** (the `ObjectiveTrendChart` has 9 tests ‚Äî oldest-left reverse, RAG fills, target+value lines, single-reading real-segment target, mixed-unit filter, all-off-unit explanation, raw-decimal precision, aria-label, jest-axe; `MeasurementsSection` + the `handlers.ts` fixture sweep updated). **CI 9/9 each round.** PR [#140](https://github.com/CoJoA13/EasySynQ/pull/140), squash `e2c6050`. - **S-obj-2** the Quality Objectives UI ‚Äî **CLOSES the Quality Objectives family; FRONT-END ONLY** (no migration/key/endpoint/contract ‚Äî it rides S-obj-1's `/api/v1/objectives*` surface). Mara's PLAN-phase surface. (1) the **`/objectives` register** ‚Äî a calm **scorecard band** (`total`/`on_target` "N / M on target" + green/amber/red/unmeasured count chips, read from `GET /objectives/scorecard` which returns BOTH the rollup AND the rows in one call) above a scannable Mantine **register table** (Ref ¬∑ Objective ¬∑ Current/target ¬∑ RAG `Status` badge ¬∑ Due), plus a minimal client-side **RAG filter** and the `objective.manage`-gated **New objective** button. (2) the **`/objectives/:id` detail** (a full page, the `/audits/:id` precedent) ‚Äî single-scroll: a **commitment hero** (`current_value` vs `target_value`+unit, a `Progress` bar whose value is `pct_toward_target` **clamped to [0,100]%** and rounded ‚Äî no bar when `pct` is null, RAG + attainment badges, a meta column) ‚Üí a **Plans** section (action/owner[`useUserDirectory`]/due rows; `objective.manage`-gated **Add plan** + per-row **Remove**) ‚Üí a **Measurement history** section (a **plain append-only table** ‚Äî Period ¬∑ Value ¬∑ **Target then** [`target_at_capture`, the honesty device for target drift] ¬∑ Source ¬∑ Recorded ‚Äî **NO chart**, N6; `kpi.read` 403s calmly section-locally; the `kpi.record`-gated **Record measurement**). (3) the **`NewObjectiveModal`** (single calm modal, no wizard) ‚Äî title/target/unit/**direction** (a `SegmentedControl`)/due required; an "amber at-risk band & baseline" **disclosure** with baseline + at-risk threshold + a live **`BandPreview`** strip (a pure `bandZones(target, threshold, direction)` drives the green/amber/red zone order + a **soft, non-blocking warn** when the threshold sits on the wrong side of target for the direction ‚Äî the backend silently collapses a backwards threshold to red, so we warn not block) + an optional process picker. (4) the **`RecordMeasurementModal`** ‚Äî the **unit is LOCKED** to the objective's `unit` (a non-editable `rightSection` adornment, sent verbatim) so a unit-mismatch 422 can't be raised from the UI; period required (defaults blank, editable to back-date a quarter); 422/404/409 ‚Üí a calm inline `Alert`. (5) the **`objective.read`-gated nav entry** (the `drift.read` precedent, PLAN region) + the two routes. **Every fixture is `satisfies`-pinned to the as-built `api/objectives.py` serializers** ‚Äî decimal **strings** everywhere EXCEPT `pct_toward_target` (a JSON `number|null`); lists wrap `{data:[‚Ä¶]}`; the scorecard is `{total,on_target,by_rag,objectives}`; the MSW handler order registers `/objectives/scorecard` before `/objectives/:id`. ‚öÝ **Build traps caught (green-vitest-blind ‚Äî tsc/lint/diff-critic caught them):** (1) **the jest-dom √ó vitest `expect` import trap** ‚Äî with `globals:true` a test's BARE global `expect` resolves to *jest's* matcher type (via `@types/jest` pulled by `jest-axe`), which lacks the jest-dom augmentation `setup.ts` applies to *vitest's* `expect`, so `tsc --noEmit` fails on `.toBeInTheDocument` even though the per-file `vitest run` is GREEN ‚Äî every component test MUST `import { expect, it } from "vitest"` (the existing repo tests' pattern); only the tsc gate / `/check-web` catches it. (2) A **persistently-mounted modal keeps its post-error/typed-field state across reopens** ‚Üí conditionally render the modal in its PARENT (`{open && <Modal .../>}`) so close unmounts+resets it (the S-web-7d lesson) + a reopen-resets regression test. (3) the register's RAG-filter state was **dead** until wired into a real control (don't `void` a setter ‚Äî implement the in-spec filter). (4) a raw `<label>` for a `SegmentedControl` fails `jsx-a11y/label-has-associated-control` ‚Üí Mantine **`Input.Wrapper`**. (5) `toBeEmptyDOMElement()` is false under `MantineProvider`'s injected `<style>` ‚Üí assert "no structural element" instead. Deferrals (named-not-faked): **objective lifecycle/release is omitted** ‚Äî S-obj-1 creates Draft objectives and the objectives router has no approve/release endpoint (an OBJ would ride the existing document review/approve/release flow), so the **6.2 ‚òÖ compliance-checklist node stays not-COVERED** (it needs an Effective objective; a later slice wires release); the create **policy field is omitted in v1** ‚Äî the backend requires `policy_id` to be the Effective POL singleton or null and **no API endpoint returns the Effective-POL id** (a small backend follow-up unblocks the "link to Quality Policy" checkbox); **KPI trend charts/sparklines** (v1.x, N6 ‚Äî history is a plain table); **per-process objective reads** (v1 SYSTEM-gates reads, the capa/audit precedent); the **commitment version-snapshot freeze** (v1.x). **The PDCA dashboard (Home) is now buildable ‚Äî acks ‚úÖ + objectives ‚úÖ both landed ‚Äî and is the natural next slice.** +36 web tests (591‚Üí627); subagent-driven TDD (5 sequential phases, per-task spec + quality review; the final **diff-critic verdict was CLEAN**). Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-11-s-obj-2-quality-objectives-ui*`.

- **S-obj-1** the Quality Objectives backend ‚Äî **OPENS the Quality Objectives family** (mig `0049`, **R44**). `quality_objective` as a kind=DOCUMENT shared-PK subtype of `documented_information` (document_type `OBJ`, the `form_template`/`capa` precedent) ‚Äî so the commitment (title, target, direction, due date) is the controlled-document layer (approvable through the existing vault lifecycle; the freeze of these satellite fields INTO the version snapshot is forward work ‚Äî see deferrals) while the operational `current_value` is a mutable rollup rolled OUTSIDE the version. `objective_plan` action rows (mutable). Append-only `kpi_measurement` projection of `KPI_READING` evidence records (REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE ‚Äî the house style; `target_at_capture` frozen at capture so a later target edit can never rewrite a past verdict; `latest-period-wins` rollup into `current_value`). **Direction-aware + amber-banded RAG** (`green`/`amber`/`red`/`unmeasured`) computed at read from the pure `domain/objectives/rules.py` ‚Äî never stored (N9/N6). `objective_direction` enum (`HIGHER_IS_BETTER`/`LOWER_IS_BETTER`). The Quality Policy is the already-seeded `POL` singleton (R25); `objective.policy_id` validates against the current Effective policy. Each objective auto-maps to clause `6.2`. **Rides the already-seeded `objective.*`/`kpi.*` keys** ‚Äî **no new permission key (catalog stays 100, no R38 change)**; `_objective_scope` PROCESS resolver + SYSTEM fallback. Three additive `OBJECTIVE_MEASUREMENT_RECORDED`/`OBJECTIVE_PLAN_ADDED`/`OBJECTIVE_PLAN_REMOVED` event types with `object_type='document'` + `scope_ref=<identifier>` (R39 reuse; no new `audit_object_type`). No new `SignatureMeaning` (R2). **Unblocks the PDCA dashboard** (separate later slice; acks + objectives both now landed). ‚öÝ **Traps caught in build:** (1) the migration's `op.create_index` calls MUST be mirrored in the ORM `__table_args__` or `alembic check` phantom-DROPs them (caught by the round-trip); (2) a KPI reading is an **ad-hoc** `KPI_READING` record (**no `source_document_id`**) ‚Äî pinning a non-FRM source triggers the R21 422 and a Draft objective has no version to pin (the `capture_complaint` precedent); (3) the rollup loads the objective `with_for_update().execution_options(populate_existing=True)` (the S-drift-1 stale-identity-map trap ‚Äî the authz resolver already `session.get`-loaded it); (4) `/objectives/scorecard` declared before `/objectives/{objective_id}` in the router (the S-pack-2 static-before-param rule). Deferrals (named-not-faked): the PDCA dashboard UI; KPI trend views (v1.x, N6); KPI readings pinned to an objective version (v1.x); Process-Owner `objective.manage` (QMS-Owner-only in v1); **per-process objective READS** (v1 SYSTEM-gates the list/scorecard reads + an org-scoped query, matching the shipped capa/audit precedent ‚Äî a PROCESS-scoped `objective.read` holder can't yet read via that grant; Codex P2); the **version-snapshot freeze of the commitment** (target/unit/direction/due) ‚Äî S-obj-1 creates Draft objectives + the live satellite and does not wire an objective check-in, so the commitment is NOT yet pinned into `document_version.metadata_snapshot` (the generic check-in snapshots base metadata only); the form_template-style freeze is forward work for when objectives are revised through the version lifecycle (Codex P5). Codex P1/P7 (multi-tenant cross-org lookups) do not apply under D1 single-org; P3 (orphan base doc on a bad `process_id` ‚Äî create_document commits first), P4 (mismatched measurement unit corrupts RAG), and P6 (direction-aware `pct_toward_target` ‚Äî no false 160% for a failing lower-is-better goal) were fixed in review. Register R44. Spec/plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-11-s-obj-*`. (The trailing **S-obj-2** front-end UI slice follows.)

## v1.x ACK family ‚Äî distribution + read-and-understood acknowledgements (0048) ‚Üí the UI tail (front-end-only)

- **S-ack-2** the Acknowledgements UI ‚Äî **CLOSES the S-ack family; FRONT-END ONLY** (no migration/key/endpoint/contract). Four surfaces over S-ack-1's endpoints: (1) the `/tasks` **DOC_ACK leg** ‚Äî a 4th `subject_type` branch in `ReviewApprovePage` rendering a *dedicated* `AttestationCard` ("I have read & understood", one click, **no signature, no radio** ‚Äî separate from `DecisionCard` so the DOCUMENT/CAPA/PERIODIC legs stay byte-untouched) + `DocAckContext` (best-effort doc, calm-403 never blocks the card); 409 `ack_obligation_lapsed`/`ack_superseded` mapped to calm copy. (2) the dedicated **bulk-ack inbox** at `/tasks?type=DOC_ACK` (`AckInbox`, multi-select looping the decision POST via `useBulkAcknowledge`/`allSettled` ‚Äî doc 10 ¬ß8.2; ‚öÝ the `GET /tasks` LIST omits `subject_type`/`subject_id` [detail-only], so each row fetches its task detail ‚Üí doc for the name). (3) the **doc page** refactored to real Mantine `Tabs` (Overview/History/Approvals/Where-used/**Acks**, `?tab=` deep-linkable) + the **Acknowledged tile** (restores the S-web-4 omission) + the **Acks tab** (`AckCoverageRing` + counts for any `document.read` reader; the named matrix + pending avatar stack + the `DistributionEditor` only with `document.distribute`). (4) the **TopBar ack bell** (open-DOC_ACK count via `useAckCount` in app/shell, links to the filtered inbox; the "Tasks" stub untouched, labels distinct). ‚öÝ **Remind stays OMITTED-NOT-FAKED** (the mockup shows it; R43 notifications-family deferral) ‚Äî and the **doc-level Audit tab is out of the initial release** (the admin audit-log sibling is parked). ‚öÝ QMS Owner holds `role.read` (`0004_seed_authz.py`) so the editor's `org_role` picker is viable for the distribute holder. Calm-403 reads pin a production-defaults QueryClient (the S-web-8 lesson). +38 web tests (551‚Üí589); subagent-driven TDD (per-task spec + quality review, sequential phases). Spec: `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-11-s-ack-2-acknowledgements-ui-design.md`.

- **S-ack-1** the Acknowledgements backend ‚Äî **opens the S-ack family** (mig `0048`; **R42** `document.distribute` [catalog 99‚Üí100, QMS Owner] + **R43** the family model). Sam's read-and-understood flow; the acks half of the PDCA-dashboard unblock. `distribution_entry` (editable issuance config, SELECT/INSERT/DELETE) + append-only `acknowledgement` (REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE ‚Äî the capa_stage house style; UNIQUE(user, version), XFF `client_ip` Text, `created_reason` enum) + `documented_information.acknowledgement_required` + the additive `DOC_ACK` task/subject enum + `DOCUMENT_ACKNOWLEDGED`/`DISTRIBUTION_UPDATED` events + the seeded single-stage `doc_acknowledgement` workflow (quorum ANY, **no signature** ‚Äî R2 untouched, `document.acknowledge` stays sig_hook=false). ‚öÝ **Re-ack is MAJOR-only with carry-forward** (`domain/ack/rules.py`): satisfied iff acked `version_seq ‚â• last-MAJOR-boundary`, walked over **ever-governed versions only** (a phantom never-Effective MAJOR draft cannot re-arm the audience ‚Äî the diff-critic MAJOR); MINOR carries coverage forward, no-MAJOR chains fall back to the lowest governed seq. ‚öÝ **In-force = `current_effective_version_id IS NOT NULL`, NOT `current_state == Effective`** (an UnderRevision doc still governs ‚Äî keying on state would mass-cancel the moment a revision opens). The sweep (`services/ack/sweep.py`, daily Beat `easysynq.ack.sweep` + post-commit enqueues via the `AckEnqueueSink` seam) is ONE universal mint covering release / R15 target entry / flag flips / entry changes; cancel-before-mint; **fail-closed on a missing definition** (no mass-cancel on broken config); `populate_existing` locked loads (the S-drift-1 trap). The DOC_ACK decide leg (the fourth `/tasks/{id}/decision` dispatch): membership 404-collapse ‚Üí `document.acknowledge` enforced at the doc scope (the key's first consumer) ‚Üí outcome whitelist `{acknowledge}` ‚Üí 409 `ack_obligation_lapsed`/`ack_superseded` ‚Üí the immutable ack row + audit in ONE txn; Idempotency-Key replay parity. Endpoints: GET/POST/DELETE `/documents/{id}/distribution` + the R42-gated named matrix `/documents/{id}/acknowledgements`; counts-only coverage under `document.read`. ‚öÝ Two pre-existing infra bugs surfaced + fixed on the first real integration run: a `pg_advisory_lock` stranded on pooled engines (now a dedicated held connection) and a ~19.5s Redis retry storm per `.delay()` in CI (the harness swaps both enqueue sinks to Logging doubles ‚Üí CI shards now ~2.5min). 11 unit + 13 integration tests. Deferred (R43): Remind + reminder history, the ¬ß6.3 report, process/folder targets, the org-wide PDCA rollup, bulk re-ack, the every-release config flag, the delegation carve-out, ack retention/GDPR. Spec: `docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-10-s-ack-acknowledgements-design.md`.

## v1.x DRIFT family ‚Äî D5 re-review (0045) ‚Üí D2+D3 mirror tamper/staleness scan (0046) ‚Üí D1+D4+admin surface (0047)

- **S-drift-3** D1 blob verify + D4 superseded-copies + the admin drift-status surface (`0047`) ‚Äî **COMPLETES the drift family's detection legs (D1‚ÄìD5 all shipped)**. Mig `0047`: `drift_scan_kind +=
BLOB_REHASH` (the S-drift-2 seam), `event_type += BLOB_INTEGRITY_FAILED`, and the **R41**
`drift.read` SYSTEM key (catalog 98‚Üí99; seeded + granted to System Administrator via the resilient
org lookup ‚Äî this install renamed the short_code). Owner forks: a NEW `drift.read` key over riding
`storage.read` (the D4 report isn't storage; riding widens storage-config readers); ONE
`BLOB_INTEGRITY_FAILED` event (classification HASH_MISMATCH/OBJECT_MISSING/READ_ERROR in the
payload ‚Äî no severity split exists, unlike MIRROR_STALE/TAMPER); daily rolling cadence where
**rotation IS the periodic full set** (FAILED-pinned first ‚Üí verified_at NULLS FIRST ‚Üí oldest,
default 500/day, CLI `--full` on demand). **The alarm latch is the slice's load-bearing call** ‚Äî
and the diff-critic MAJOR reshaped it: `blob.verified_at` stays the pure "last verified OK" cursor
(stamped on a pass only), while a finding sets **`blob.verify_failed_at`** (mig 0047), the explicit
pin that sorts FIRST in every rolling sample ‚Äî a finding re-alarms every run until restored (no
auto-correction exists for blobs; restore-from-backup per the new
`runbooks/blob-integrity-verify.md`). ‚öÝ The original stamp-on-OK-only-without-a-pin design had a
hole: a once-stamped-then-corrupted blob sorts BEHIND every never-verified row, so a NULL-cursor
influx > sample size (a bulk import) crowds a DETECTED corruption out of the daily sample and the
latest-per-kind status read goes CLEAN over it. The status surface exposes the pin directly
(`blob_coverage.failing`). Two sibling diff-critic folds: an `OBJECT_MISSING` finding whose ROW is
gone at persist time was a legal R27 disposal racing the scan ‚Üí pruned (info-log), never a
permanent false alarm; the stamp UPDATEs are chunked (10k) under psycopg's 65,535-bind-param cap
and the CLI surfaces a persist failure (warning + exit 1). Per-object errors are findings;
connection-class errors ABORT as FAILED salvaging findings (no noise-event storms when MinIO is
down). D4 is a LIVE
read ‚Äî `EXPORTED`/`PRINTED` events √ó now-Superseded/Obsolete versions is sound by construction
(`render_dynamic_copy` only ever serves the then-Effective version); no decrement leg (the `/verify`
token is the per-copy resolution). New surface: `GET /admin/drift/status` +
`GET /admin/drift/superseded-copies` (both `drift.read`; S-web-8 consumes them). Integration
technique: synthetic tamper via planted blob ROWS (a wrong-sha row over real bytes / a row with no
object) ‚Äî never fight WORM. Spec:
`docs/superpowers/specs/2026-06-10-s-drift-3-blob-verify-drift-surface-design.md`.

- **S-drift-2** D2+D3 mirror tamper/staleness scan (`0046`) ‚Äî **the drift family's THESIS slice**: D2 was *asserted* ("authority flows vault ‚Üí mirror"), now it is a *verified, audited, self-correcting invariant*. **Migration `0046`:** two operational tables (`mirror_build` = the **vault-side expected-state baseline** [one row per build, keyed by the `.builds/<hex>` dir; `manifest` jsonb with doc-owned entries carrying `document_id`/`version_id`; `manifest_sha256` over the on-disk `_meta/manifest.json`; `swapped_at` the pointer-integrity anchor], `drift_scan` = the per-scan summary [`kind` `MIRROR`; `status` `CLEAN`/`DIVERGENT`/`FAILED`; `counts` jsonb]) + two additive event types `MIRROR_STALE`/`MIRROR_TAMPER` (the 0011 ADD-VALUE pattern). ‚öÝ **The mirror is never trusted as truth** ‚Äî the expected state is the PG `mirror_build` manifest, and the on-disk manifest is byte-verified against the stored digest, never read as authority (its non-deterministic `generated_at` makes recompute impossible by design). **The scanner** (`services/vault/mirror_scan.py`, pure-core `compare_tree`/`classify_mismatch`/quarantine + DB orchestration `resolve_pointer`/`scan_mirror`/`persist_scan_results`/`scan_and_sync`): walks the served build tree (`os.walk(followlinks=False)`, NEVER `rglob`) against the baseline ‚Üí classifies (`STALE_REVISION` = a digest of an OTHER version of the **same** document [`_known_digests` EXCLUDES the expected version ‚Äî same-version bytes in the wrong role, e.g. raw source over the banded rendition, are TAMPER] ‚Üí `MIRROR_STALE`; `UNEXPECTED_CONTENT`/`EXTRA`/`MISSING`/`SYMLINK_DIVERGENT`/`POINTER_DIVERGENT` ‚Üí `MIRROR_TAMPER`) ‚Üí **QUARANTINES divergent bytes BEFORE any rebuild** (R11: the rebuild prunes the old tree, so scan-first is what preserves forensic evidence; in-tree files copied + re-hashed [`quarantined_sha256` chain of custody], foreign/rogue whole trees moved, into `<mirror>/.quarantine/<ts>__<scan-id>/` at `0o700`) ‚Üí audits each anomaly (`actor_type=system`; doc-attributable ‚Üí `object_type=document` + `scope_ref=identifier`, else `config` keyed on the resilient single-org lookup) ‚Üí writes the `drift_scan` summary ‚Üí **rebuilds (vault wins)**. ‚öÝ **Pointer integrity (the CRITICAL fold):** the `current` symlink is **verified against the registry, never trusted** ‚Äî `resolve_pointer` matches `current`'s target against the newest *swapped* `mirror_build` row; only the relative `.builds/<name>` shape `atomic_swap` writes is parsed (`_parse_current_target` ‚Äî an absolute/out-of-tree/nested/basename-colliding target classifies **foreign ‚Üí MIRROR_TAMPER**, raw string as evidence, NEVER resolved against the filesystem); a missing `current` ‚Üí `missing`, a real-dir `current` ‚Üí `rogue_dir` (moved aside to unblock the swap), an older swapped build ‚Üí `rollback`, the swap-then-crash window ‚Üí `selfheal` (persist stamps `swapped_at`); only an **empty registry** is the benign no-baseline (fresh install / pre-0046 upgrade ‚Äî zero false alarms). ‚öÝ A **destroyed or symlink-swapped served `.builds/<name>` tree** is `MIRROR_TAMPER` (`POINTER_DIVERGENT`) + `is_current` stays False so the hourly path rebuilds ‚Äî NOT a silent CLEAN (a bare `is_dir()` guard that follows symlinks was the C1 quality-review catch). **Composition (owner fork ¬ß0.1):** one scan-first pipeline ‚Äî **every** `sync_mirror` scans the outgoing tree first (R11's per-sync leg; the `mirror_build` insert + the current-target-protected keep-last-20 prune + the post-swap `swapped_at` stamp all moved inside the session scope), and a **NEW hourly Beat `easysynq.mirror.scan`** (`MIRROR_SCAN_INTERVAL_SECONDS`, default 3600 = the accepted drift window) runs the same pipeline, rebuilding only on DIVERGENT/behind-vault/no-baseline and NEVER on `FAILED` (a scan failure is not evidence the mirror is wrong; the sync path still rebuilds ‚Äî the correction must never be blocked). Both serialize under `LOCK_MIRROR_SYNC`. ‚öÝ **Lock/persist hardening:** `scan_mirror` is DB-READ-ONLY and **never raises** (an infra failure ‚Üí an honest `FAILED` report that SALVAGES already-classified findings so persist still audits them); `persist_scan_results` returns success and a persist failure WITH findings **defers the rebuild** (it would erase the on-disk evidence the next scan needs); after a FAILED scan or failed persist the pipeline **re-verifies advisory-lock ownership** (`holds_advisory_lock`, `objsubid=1`) before rebuilding ‚Äî a mid-scan connection loss silently frees the session-level lock and a lockless rebuild could race a concurrent sync's prune. CLI `easysynq mirror scan` (scan-only) / `sync` / `rebuild` (the force-clear scoped `WHERE version_state == Effective`, committed BEFORE the pipeline). **No new permission key, no endpoint, no contract change** (the admin drift-status read surface is S-drift-3). **Tests:** 19 unit (the classification matrix ¬∑ the pointer matrix ¬∑ `_parse_current_target` ¬∑ quarantine copy/move/rehash ¬∑ counts math ¬∑ the FAILED family ¬∑ gate-order persist-before-rebuild) + 12 integration (Linux CI: tamper‚Üíquarantine‚Üíaudit‚Üícorrect, stale [source + older-rendition], behind-vault-not-tamper, foreign/rollback/destroyed-tree pointer cases, foreign-tree quarantine-by-move, the protected keep-N prune, the FAILED row, the real task-path lock skip-tick). **4-lens pass folded** (1 CRITICAL pointer-integrity + 8 MAJOR before code) + per-task spec+quality subagent review (C1 destroyed-tree, the out-of-tree basename-collision bypass, salvage-into-FAILED among the catches). **Deferred residuals:** the admin drift-status surface + the trailing UI (S-drift-3 / S-web-8); D1 blob re-hash + D4 superseded-copies report (S-drift-3, which reuses `drift_scan` with `kind=BLOB_REHASH` additively); the by-move √ó persist-failure window (best-effort, documented); the `built_at`-tiebreak determinism note (practically distinct microsecond timestamps under `LOCK_MIRROR_SYNC`); **the advisory-lock connection-pinning P1 (Codex round 5) ‚Äî assessed NOT reachable** (per-task `create_async_engine` = isolated pools + the global `pg_try_advisory_lock` at task entry serialize workers; two backends can't both be the lock holder), owner-accepted deferral with a re-evaluation trigger (if these tasks ever share a process-wide engine/pool) recorded in the spec ¬ß11a. ‚öÝ **Codex did 6 review rounds on #108** (5 P1/P2 clusters all in the adversarial-filesystem surface ‚Äî symlink/special/raw-collision at `current`/`.builds`/`.quarantine`, STALE-class precision, salvage ordering, lock recheck); all fixed except the round-5 pin (pushed back + documented). Owner steer (2026-06-10): disregard further nitpicks/unreachable items, document them, squash-merge on green.

- **S-drift-1** D5 scheduled re-review currency sweep (`0045`) ‚Äî **opened the v1.x drift family**. **Migration `0045`:** three nullable columns on `documented_information` (`review_period_months` INTEGER ‚Äî **NOT interval**: psycopg3 cannot load month-bearing PG intervals into `timedelta`, so the column is plain int months; `next_review_due` DATE STORED, reset from the review date on confirm and recomputed on release/PATCH; `last_reviewed_at` timestamptz) + a **partial index `ix_documented_information_next_review_due` on (next_review_due) WHERE NOT NULL** (the Beat sweep's scan path) + additive event types `REVIEW_CONFIRMED`/`REVIEW_OVERDUE` + the seeded single-stage `periodic_review` workflow definition. ‚öÝ **Org-lookup trap:** the seed uses a `scalar_one_or_none` on `short_code='DEFAULT'` with a `SELECT the only org` fallback ‚Äî `0038`/`0043`'s verbatim `scalar_one` on `'DEFAULT'` would ABORT an OPERATIONAL install's upgrade because setup G-E renames the short_code (this install = `AHT`); those earlier migrations only "ran clean" because they pre-dated setup. The engine gained an additive `context_users` assignee-spec key in `_resolve_pool` (role path byte-identical) + `instantiate` widened to `actor: AppUser | None` (system sweeps). **Write paths:** create default = 24 months; T2 **AUTO-DEFAULT at submit** (not a 422 ‚Äî a legacy doc must not strand at submit while the SPA lacks the field, pre-S-web-8); `next_review_due` recomputed on release (`_cutover`, both T6 + scheduled), on confirm, and on PATCH. **ONE rule:** anchor = the LATER of (`last_reviewed_at`, `effective_from`), org-tz dated, + months (`add_months` day-clamped). `PATCH /documents/{id}` accepts `review_period_months` (ge=1 le=120; `null` = opt-out; `model_fields_set` distinguishes omitted vs explicit-null); loads the doc lock-aware. `review_period_months` joins the version `metadata_snapshot` + the `SNAPSHOT_FIELDS` metadata-diff. **Daily Beat sweep `easysynq.documents.review_sweep`** (Beat key `documents-review-sweep`): advisory-lock single-flight (`LOCK_REVIEW_SWEEP`) ‚Äî `acks_late` re-delivery makes concurrent runs real, and no schema constraint stops two open instances per subject; 30-day lead window; instantiates the seeded `periodic_review` definition per due Effective doc (idempotent open-instance check; subject `PERIODIC_REVIEW`; owner-assigned via `context_users`); task `due_at` = org-tz midnight of `next_review_due`; escalation = once-per-CYCLE `REVIEW_OVERDUE` audit (dedup anchored on `after.instance_id`). ‚öÝ **Task state is NEVER flipped on escalation**: `engine.decide()` accepts ONLY `PENDING` (engine.py:390) ‚Äî an `ESCALATED` task would be undecidable. **Decision dispatch** `POST /tasks/{id}/decision` `PERIODIC_REVIEW` ‚Üí `decide_periodic_review`: 404-COLLAPSE non-membership (never 403) + **live-owner re-check** (`doc.owner_user_id` NOW, with the doc row `FOR UPDATE` ‚Äî the `context_users` analogue of the siblings' live role re-check); outcomes `complete` ("no change needed" ‚Üí `signature_event(meaning=review_confirmed)` bound to the Effective version id + its `source_blob_sha256` digest + `REVIEW_CONFIRMED` audit `[scope_ref=identifier]` + `last_reviewed_at=now` + clock reset) | `changes_requested` (‚Üí instance `REJECTED`, NO clock reset ‚Äî the sweep re-nags while the doc stays Effective and due); a doc obsoleted mid-review ‚Üí 409 with full txn rollback (task stays `PENDING`). **Read surface:** 4 fields on the `_document` serializer (`review_period_months`, `next_review_due`, `last_reviewed_at`, `review_state` derived `current|due_soon|overdue` ‚Äî never stored) on detail + list; the compliance checklist's previously-deferred doc 13 "overdue review" leg (`overdue_review` bool per ‚òÖ row + rollup count). Contract: `Document`/`MetadataUpdate`/`ChecklistRow`/`ChecklistRollup` additions + `Decision`/`DecisionResult` gain outcome `complete` + 3 nullable result keys. **Unblocks:** `next_review_due` / the "Days to review" tile (deferred since S-web-1), the checklist overdue UI leg (S-web-6 ¬ß3.1), currency reporting toward metric M3 (<5% overdue). **Tests:** 24 targeted unit + 17 new/extended integration (Linux CI); 9 implementation commits. **Deferred residuals:** the grace‚ÜíFinding optional policy (doc 04 ¬ß9.1 row 3); org-config default period/lead window (constants 24mo/30d in v1); the dedicated currency/overdue report endpoint (v1.x reporting family); ALL UI (trailing S-web-8 after the family); D1‚ÄìD4 (S-drift-2 ‚úÖ mirror tamper/staleness scan; S-drift-3 blob integrity verify + the D4 superseded-copies report).

## MVP (S0‚ÄìS11) ‚Äî COMPLETE ‚úÖ

All 11 ordered slices shipped to `main` via PR, all CI green, validated on the real Docker stack (exit slice S11 = PR #41).
All six MVP acceptance proofs in; mirror epic + both IA backends complete; doc-18 ¬ß12 exit checklist closed. Spec-before-code.

- **S0** walking skeleton ¬∑ **S1** AuthN (Keycloak OIDC/PKCE, JWT‚ÜîJWKS, `app_user` JIT, `GET /me`) ¬∑ **S2** AuthZ (deny-wins PDP/PEP, the closed doc-07 96-key catalog + 8 seeded roles, the R35 two-tier grant guard).
- **S3** Vault (check-out ‚Üí presigned CAS upload ‚Üí immutable check-in; MinIO WORM + Redis lock; atomic `{TYPE}-{AREA}-{SEQ}` numbering) ¬∑ **S4** Lifecycle **[AC#1]** (the doc FSM + the atomic SERIALIZABLE single-Effective cutover + the INV-1 partial-unique index) ¬∑ **S5** Approval + SoD (`POST /tasks/{id}/decision` one-txn + append-only `signature_event` + the deny-wins SoD-1/2/3 gate).
- **S6** Audit **[AC#6]** (append-only, monthly-partitioned, hash-chained `audit_event` behind DB **role separation** [non-owner `easysynq_app`] + the decoupled chain-linker + frozen `canonical_serialize` + the off-host checkpoint anchor) ¬∑ **S7** Mirror **[AC#2]** (RO Effective-only filesystem mirror, atomic symlink-repoint swap, mounted `:ro`) + **S7b/c/d** (watermarked-PDF rendering via Gotenberg + a deterministic reportlab/pypdf ¬ß11.3 band ¬∑ Ed25519 verify-token + QR + public `GET /verify` ¬∑ the per-request export/print stamp).
- **S8a‚ÄìS8d** first-run setup + admin (PRs #16/#18/#20/#22/#24) ‚Äî the **423 setup-latch** + **bootstrap-of-trust** (`easysynq setup mint-bootstrap` ‚Üí the first System Administrator) + the extensible **gate registry** (G-A admin ¬∑ G-B WORM-probe ¬∑ G-C backup‚Üírestore-drill [AC#5] ¬∑ G-D auth-proof ¬∑ G-E org-profile) ‚Üí the one-way `UNINITIALIZED‚ÜíIN_SETUP‚ÜíOPERATIONAL` finalize; then Users & Roles admin + invite/enable-disable (R35 two-tier guard; last-admin guard). A Mantine `<Stepper>` wizard.
- **S9/S9b/S9c/S9d** the two IA backends + the mirror tree (PRs #27/#31/#32/#33) ‚Äî the read-only ISO 9001 **clause spine** (83-clause/20‚òÖ catalog, `db/seeds/iso9001_clauses.py`) + M:N `clause_mapping` + the submit-needs-‚â•1-mapping gate (`0017`/`0018`); the **process graph** (`process`/`process_edge`/`process_link`, `0019`); the ¬ß10.3 mirror **clause tree** (`{PLAN|DO|CHECK|ACT}/{NN-Name}/`) + a `by-process/` index (pure `mirror.py`, no migration). Authoring rides SYSTEM overrides until owner-assignment.
- **OpenAPI catch-up** (PR #35) ‚Äî `packages/contracts/openapi.yaml` is redocly-lint ONLY (no codegen); **document new endpoints in-PR going forward**.
- **S10** search/reporting backend (PR #38, backend only) ‚Äî the org-wide **Compliance Checklist** `GET /reports/compliance-checklist` (the 20‚òÖ clauses ‚Üí COVERED/PARTIAL/GAP + rollup) + Postgres-FTS `GET /search(/suggest)` behind the `Indexer` seam (OpenSearch the v1 drop-in, R34; Effective-only + filter-not-403) + `clause_refs` + the doc-15 bracketed `filter[field][op]` grammar on `GET /documents` (`0020`).
- **S11** the MVP EXIT slice (PR #41) ‚Äî operator-grade `easysynq restore` (WORM-aware restore-to-VERIFIED-TARGET) + `easysynq upgrade` (pre-backup ‚Üí migrate ‚Üí health-gate) + backup archive v2 (AES-256-GCM, only-if-encrypted) + a strict static Caddy CSP + 9 operator runbooks (`docs/runbooks/`) (`0022`).

**Deferred (S8e / v1 / Part-11):** the doc-14 `storage_config.mirror_layout` toggle (with its config UI); **owner-assignment** (`org_role_assignment` + concrete PROCESS-scope grants ‚Üí real Process-Owner authoring) + `/org-roles`/`/suppliers` authoring (v1); the **web** Compliance-Checklist + Admin Audit-Log screens + clause-spine nav + mapping UI + process-map UI; the rest of doc-13 search/reporting (faceted facet-rail, saved searches, dashboards, canonical reports, evidence packs, find-where-used, content-plane/body-text FTS, the `{data,page,_links}` cursor envelope, subtree clause rollup, the checklist's "overdue review"/"linked evidence" legs [need `next_review_due`/records], R31 scope-conditional coverage); wizard Step 8 (scope/process-map seed ‚Üí SEED nodes) + Step 9 (import ‚Üí the v1 ingestion epic); custom-role create/update/delete + bulk-CSV invite + the effective-permissions explorer (v1); in-app Keycloak admin-API provisioning (v1); MFA *enforcement* + `acr`/step-up (Part-11, D3); the ¬ß10.4 self-grant friction + `ADMIN_SELF_GRANTED_QMS_CAP` event (v1).

**Deferred (v1.x, D-6 / R37):** continuous **PITR/WAL**, retention **pruning**, **S3/cloud backup destination**, **automated in-place live cutover** (restore-to-verified-target + a documented manual cutover ships; automation is the hardening TODO in `restore.py`/`upgrade.py`), **per-request nonce-CSP** (strict static CSP ships; nonce needs SPA HTML-nonce injection ‚Äî web track), **COMPLIANCE object-lock mode** (GOVERNANCE ships, D-7). S6/S7 seams still open (Keycloak auth-event SPI, `/audit-events/export` async-export job). Pre-existing hardening: `area_code` is unconstrained `Text` at the S3 create boundary.
