## v1 AUDITS/FINDINGS/CAPA family (doc 02 Cl 9.2/10.2, doc 10 ¬ß5-6, UJ-5/UJ-6) ‚Äî COMPLETE ‚úÖ

Locked posture: **R39** (declarative-routing ¬∑ severity-aware SoD-4 ¬∑ block-until-corrected audit close ¬∑ `audit_program` own-table ¬∑ the S-capa-3 addendum: Verify‚ÜíRootCause loop ¬∑ M4 = real evidence_for_link gate ¬∑ the S-aud-capa-pack addendum: subject-not-a-pack_item ¬∑ sealed v2 dossier ¬∑ PII-projected signers ¬∑ gap N/A).

- **S-aud-1** audit programmes/plans/audits + lifecycle FSM (`0034`) ‚Äî `audit_program`+`audit_plan` own-table scheduling containers + `audit` as a `kind=RECORD` shared-PK subtype (captured via `capture_record(_commit=False)`, REC-shared identifier, mutable `state`); the linear FSM Scheduled‚Üí‚Ä¶‚ÜíClosing‚ÜíClosed (FOR-UPDATE + audited-then-commit; the Closing‚ÜíClosed close-gate is the real live-NC-findings check as of S-aud-2); `/audit-programs`+`/audit-plans`+`/audits`+6 flat-action transitions (gates `audit.{plan,create,conduct,close,read}`, PROCESS conduct/close via an `_audit_scope` resolver w/ SYSTEM fallback).
- **S-wf-engine** the doc-10 declarative workflow engine (`0035`) ‚Äî NEW `services/workflow/engine.py` (generic `instantiate`+multi-stage `decide`) on the existing `workflow_*` tables, the S5 DOCUMENT `decide()` left **byte-identical**; SEQUENTIAL/PARALLEL stages + `domain/workflow` pure helpers: tri-state quorum (ANY/ALL/N_OF_M/PERCENT, distinct approvers, early-fail), `conditional` quorum/ROUTER routing over an `ast`-sandboxed predicate grammar on `workflow_instance.context`, candidate-pool via the permission-role `users_with_roles` seam, due-date SLA. **Instance-row `FOR UPDATE` is the quorum serialization point**; cross-role conjunction (Critical CAPA) is composed as sequential stages. Fail-closed totality ‚Üí `NEEDS_ATTENTION`. Service-level only.
- **S-capa-1** the CAPA core + intake (`0036`) ‚Äî `capa` (`kind=RECORD` shared-PK subtype, mutable `close_state` FSM Raised‚Üí‚Ä¶‚ÜíClosed/Rejected; only **Raised‚ÜíContainment** service-wired) + append-only `capa_stage` (`REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE`; doc-14 `attachments` realized as `evidence_for_link(CAPA_STAGE)` edges; `signed_event_id`/`cycle_marker` forward seams) + `ncr` (own-table, R20 disposition + `NCR-{SEQ}` id) + `complaint` (R16 shared-PK subtype) + the **idempotent complaint‚ÜíCAPA spawn** (`complaint.spawned_capa_id` latch under `FOR UPDATE`; 201 fresh / 200 replay). PROCESS-scoped write keys gate via in-handler `enforce` from `body.process_id`; reads at SYSTEM. Slice-0 grant-backfill: `capa.update`‚ÜíProcess Owner; `ncr.create`‚ÜíQMS Owner + Internal Auditor; `ncr.record_correction`‚ÜíQMS Owner. `system_config.allow_capa_self_verify` (default OFF) is the S-capa-3 SoD-4 seam.
- **S-aud-2** audit findings + the NC‚ÜíCAPA auto-link + the REAL close gate (`0037`) ‚Äî `audit_finding` (`kind=RECORD` shared-PK subtype; `finding_type` NC/OBSERVATION/OFI, `severity` reuses `nc_severity` + a DB CHECK `ck_audit_finding_nc_has_severity`, soft `clause_ref`/`process_ref`, `auto_capa_id`); `create_finding` ‚Äî an **NC mandatorily auto-creates** its CAPA in ONE txn via `build_capa(_commit=False)` (SYSTEM-side under the auditor's `finding.create`, NOT gated on `capa.create` ‚Äî auditor independence). The **deferred cross-FK lands**: `capa.origin_finding_id`‚Üí`audit_finding` (use_alter back-edge) + `audit_finding.auto_capa_id`‚Üí`capa`. **General retype** path `POST /findings/{id}/correction` (any direction; to-NC auto-creates a CAPA). The **real `_audit_close_gate`** blocks Closing‚ÜíClosed (409 `audit_close_blocked`) while any LIVE NC lacks a linked `capa.close_state=Closed`. Findings open-until-Closed. `evidence_for_link` FINDING/CAPA_STAGE validation enabled.
- **S-capa-2** RootCause + ActionPlan + the severity-routed engine approval + the REAL signature (`0038`, seed-only) ‚Äî `POST /capas/{id}/root-cause` (gate `capa.record_rca`, Containment‚ÜíRootCause, unsigned) + `POST /capas/{id}/action-plan` (gate `capa.plan_action`) which **instantiates** the seeded `capa_action_plan_approval` `workflow_definition` (ROUTER on `severity`: **Critical** ‚Üí `crit_qm`[QMS-Owner,ANY]‚Üí`crit_topmgmt`[Top-Management,ANY] SEQUENTIAL; **Major/Minor** ‚Üí `qm_approval`[QMS-Owner,ANY]; uniform ‚â§5-day SLA). `close_state` stays RootCause during approval; proposed plan rides `workflow_instance.context`. HTTP wiring = a **`POST /tasks/{id}/decision` subject-type dispatch** (DOCUMENT byte-identical; CAPA ‚Üí `decide_capa_action_plan`): on the COMPLETING approval writes ONE `signature_event(meaning=approval, signed_object_type=capa_stage)` + appends the SIGNED ActionPlan stage (`signed_event_id` set at INSERT via a pre-gen stage UUID ‚Äî no UPDATE on the append-only table) + flips `close_state`‚ÜíActionPlan, all in ONE txn. Authz = candidate-pool membership + live-role re-check + cross-STAGE distinct-approver guard. NEW additive reserved **Top Management** role (`capa.read` only).
- **S-capa-3** Implement + Verify + Close ‚Äî the M4 closure gate + severity-aware SoD-4 (zero-migration; head stays `0038`; PR #70) ‚Äî `POST /capas/{id}/implement` (gate `capa.capture_effectiveness`, ActionPlan‚ÜíImplement, unsigned) + `POST /capas/{id}/verify` (gate `capa.verify`; Implement‚ÜíVerify; the REAL `signature_event(meaning=verify)`; decision sealed into the Verify block) + `POST /capas/{id}/close` (gate `capa.close`). **Severity-aware SoD-4** (`domain/capa/sod.py::capa_self_verify_blocked` ‚Äî Critical/Major HARD-409 verifier‚âÝimplementer; Minor respects `allow_capa_self_verify`) runs UNCONDITIONALLY before any grant short-circuit; the **implementer set** = Implement-stage `created_by` ‚à™ ActionPlan `action_items[].owner`-UUIDs over the WHOLE trail (excludes the ActionPlan stage `created_by` = the approver). The **M4 gate** (`domain/capa/closure.py`, under the capa FOR UPDATE): `effective` ‚àß root_cause ‚àß ‚â•1 implemented-action-with-`evidence_for_link(CAPA_STAGE)` ‚àß effectiveness-evidence ‚Üí **Closed**; `not_effective` ‚Üí loop **Verify‚ÜíRootCause** + `cycle_marker++`; `effective` but evidence-incomplete ‚Üí 409 `capa_close_incomplete`. **Freeze:** `records.unlink_evidence` 409s `evidence_frozen` for a CAPA_STAGE Verify-stage or Closed-CAPA target. Proof: an audit with a live NC closes once its auto-CAPA is driven to Closed (`test_audits.py`).
- **S-aud-capa-pack** the family close-out ‚Äî Evidence-Pack **Finding/CAPA scope** + a content-hash-sealed dossier (`0039` = `ALTER TYPE pack_scope_kind ADD VALUE FINDING/CAPA`) ‚Äî `POST /evidence-packs {scope_kind:"FINDING"|"CAPA", finding_ids|capa_ids}` resolves the records linked AS EVIDENCE to the finding/CAPA stages (the finding/CAPA SUBJECT is NEVER a pack_item ‚Äî no `evidence_blob`) and bundles per-subject `findings/<id>.json`/`capas/<id>.json` dossiers (the finding fields / the CAPA stage trail RootCause‚ÜíActionPlan‚ÜíVerify + e-signature metadata, projected to `{user_id, display_name}` ONLY). Dossier folds into `pack_content_hash` as **v2** (`easysynq.evidencepack.v2`; CLAUSE/PROCESS byte-identical v1) via a `dossier_digest` over the manifest per-file shas. Gap report N/A for finding/CAPA; no new keys/enum/task.

## v1 REVISION & CHANGE DEPTH family (doc 05, the DCR family) ‚Äî COMPLETE ‚úÖ

Owner decisions **R40**: DCR is an own-table mutable-state workflow object [R22, NOT a record] ¬∑ the InApproval changes-requested loop targets **Open** [doc 15 ¬ß8.7, superseding doc 05 ¬ß5.5's Routed] ¬∑ keys = the seeded `changeRequest.*` family [R5] ¬∑ scope-forks: **full** diff [meta+text+visual] + a **doc‚Üîdoc link table** for where-used ¬∑ scheduled re-review D5 + drift D1‚ÄìD4 stay in the v1.x drift family.

- **S-dcr-1** the DCR core + intake (`0040`) ‚Äî `dcr` own-table (mutable `state` FSM Open‚Üí‚Ä¶‚ÜíClosed/Cancelled/Rejected; `DCR-{YYYY}-{SEQ}` 4-digit id; `target_document_id` NULL‚ü∫CREATE via the `ck_dcr_create_iff_no_target` CHECK; `source_link_id` polymorphic no-FK; `resulting_version_id` nullable seam) + append-only `dcr_stage_event` (`REVOKE UPDATE,DELETE`; `signed_event_id` FK present, populated S-dcr-4) + 4 enums + pure `domain/dcr/fsm.py` (InApproval changes-requested loop ‚Üí Open; cancel from {Open,Assessed,Routed} only) + `audit_object_type=dcr` + `DCR_RAISED`/`DCR_UPDATED`/`DCR_TRANSITIONED`. Endpoints `POST/GET /dcrs`, `GET/PATCH /dcrs/{id}` (assess-gated edit-while-Open), `POST /dcrs/{id}/cancel`. Grant-backfill: orphaned `changeRequest.assess` + `changeRequest.close` ‚Üí Process Owner + QMS Owner. NO new permission keys.
- **S-dcr-2** where-used / impact + assess (`0041`) ‚Äî the NEW `document_link` doc‚Üîdoc graph (`parent_of`/`child_of`/`references`/`supersedes`; editable metadata `GRANT SELECT,INSERT,DELETE`, the `clause_mapping` precedent; CRUD `POST/GET/DELETE /documents/{id}/links` on `document.manage_metadata`) + `impact_assessment` (one row per the 7 doc-05-¬ß5.3 dimensions, `UNIQUE(dcr_id,dimension)`) + `GET /documents/{id}/where-used` (`document.read` ‚Äî the ¬ß7.2 categories over `process_link`/`document_link`/`clause_mapping`/records/`dcr.source_link`) + the pure ¬ß7.3 `obsoletion_blocked` predicate SURFACED as a `where-used.obsoletion_safety` advisory (governs-active-process / referenced-by-Effective / sole-‚òÖ-coverage) ‚Äî **enforcement deferred to S-dcr-5** per the R40 addendum (the shipped `document.obsolete` untouched) + `POST /dcrs/{id}/assess` (Open‚ÜíAssessed; mirrors `cancel_dcr` + UPSERTs the impact rows from where-used in one txn; a CREATE DCR ‚Üí all-N/A) + `GET/PUT /dcrs/{id}/impact`. NO new keys, NO Celery task. The S-dcr-1 `_dcr_doc_scope` (R28 process_ids) gates assess.
- **S-dcr-3a** redline/diff core (**ZERO-migration**, head stays `0041`) ‚Äî `GET /documents/{id}/versions/{vid}/diff?from={vid2}` (gate **`document.read_draft`** ‚Äî the diff exposes non-released version content, so `document.read` alone would leak Draft text to an Employee/Guest). The two doc-05-¬ß8.1 core dimensions: **metadata diff** (pure `domain/diff/metadata.py` over the frozen `metadata_snapshot` SNAPSHOT_FIELDS) + **text redline** (pure `domain/diff/text.py` `difflib` line-LCS over on-demand Tika text via a `TextExtractor` seam; fail-closed ‚Üí `text_diff: unavailable`) + the **provenance header** (`signature_event[]` projected to `{signer_user_id}` only). `document.diff` NOT seeded ‚Äî the diff rides `document.read_draft` (R5). Owner chose **full diff incl. visual** ‚Üí delivered as 3a + 3b.
- **S-dcr-3b** the visual page-image diff (`0042`) ‚Äî **worker-async** (owner chose full coverage over in-request-PDF-only, since the **API can't render**: `LoggingRenderSink` no-op; rendering is worker-only). Deps **pypdfium2** (Apache/BSD prebuilt wheels ‚Äî NOT PyMuPDF/fitz, passes `test_no_pymupdf_or_fitz_in_lockfile`; no system dep / air-gap impact) + Pillow `ImageChops`. NEW `visual_diff` cache table (`UNIQUE(from,to)` idempotency latch + cache key; `VisualDiffStatus` Pending/Ready/Failed/Unavailable; GRANT SELECT,INSERT,UPDATE ‚Äî regenerable cache, not append-only) + `easysynq.visual_diff` Celery task (FOR-UPDATE + early-return-on-terminal idempotent; `acks_late` redelivery + re-POST self-heal ‚Äî **no Beat reaper**) + pure `domain/diff/visual.py` (pypdfium2 rasterize @ scale 2.0 / cap 100 pages + Pillow per-page `ImageChops` overlay) + `services/diff/visual.py`. The task obtains each version's PDF (cache-hit on the mirror `rendition_blob_sha256`; else render via the worker's `GotenbergRenderSink` **TRANSIENTLY ‚Äî NEVER writes `rendition_blob_sha256`**, else a Draft's diff-rendition [copy_status=state, no verify QR] would POISON the mirror's controlled-copy cache when it goes Effective ‚Äî the diff-critic-preempted catch), rasterizes both, diffs page-by-page, caches each page's from/to/diff PNG as a content-addressed non-WORM `Blob` (no purge wiring ‚Äî verified no path deletes a `document_version`'s blobs). Contract = **POST-compute (202) + pure-GET-poll (404-before-request) + `GET .../visual-diff/page/{n}?layer=from|to|diff` PNG stream** (the design-critic-mandated shape; the packs/imports async precedent), all gated `document.read_draft`. Watermark band-noise (footer band differs by rev ‚Üí a changed footer region) accepted + documented for v1 (raw-render = v1.x). NO new permission key / event type. **The doc 05 ¬ß8 full diff (metadata + text + visual) is COMPLETE.**

- **S-dcr-4** routing + approval (`0043`) ‚Äî DCR approval via the declarative engine (subject_type=DCR, the S-capa-2 pattern). Migration 0043 = ONE `signed_object_type ADD VALUE 'dcr'` (workflow_subject_type.DCR already existed from 0008) + the seeded `dcr_approval` `workflow_definition` (**ROUTER on `change_significance`**: MAJOR ‚Üí `major_proc` [Process Owner, ANY] ‚Üí `major_qms` [QMS Owner, ANY] SEQUENTIAL; MINOR ‚Üí `minor_qms` [QMS Owner, ANY]; reuses the existing roles, no new role) + the `changeRequest.route` grant-backfill (Process Owner + QMS Owner, PROCESS-scoped). `route_dcr` (gate `changeRequest.route`): Assessed‚ÜíRouted‚ÜíInApproval atomically ‚Äî instantiates the workflow w/ `context={change_significance}`; NEEDS_ATTENTION (empty pool) ‚Üí fail-fast 409 `dcr_no_approvers` (rolls back, DCR stays Assessed). `POST /tasks/{id}/decision` extended with a **DCR dispatch** (DOCUMENT/CAPA byte-identical) ‚Üí `decide_dcr_approval`: **per-approver signatures** (doc 05 ¬ß5.4 ‚Äî EACH approve writes `signature_event(meaning=approval, signed_object_type='dcr', signed_object_id=<DCR id>)`; a MAJOR DCR ‚Üí TWO; the `dcr_stage_event(InApproval‚ÜíApproved).signed_event_id` links the sealing one); on the COMPLETING approve it flips ‚ÜíApproved + sets `decision/decided_by/decided_at`. **reject (‚ÜíRejected) / changes_requested (‚ÜíOpen, R40 loop) is DECISIVE** ‚Äî one approver force-terminates the instance (`current_state=REJECTED` + skip sibling PENDING tasks under the instance lock), since the engine's ANY quorum won't fail on a single negative with other live candidates; a re-route opens a FRESH instance. Authz = `_assert_dcr_approver` (candidate-pool + live-role 404-collapse + cross-stage distinct-approver 409; NO key ‚Äî `changeRequest.approve` stays ungranted, the CAPA precedent). NO new permission key / event type / Celery task.

- **S-dcr-5** implement/close + the shared-path obsoletion gate + the CAPA‚ÜíDCR loop (`0044`) ‚Äî **CLOSES the DCR family.** **DCR-as-orchestrator** (owner, reconciling doc 05/15's "DCR drives the release" over doc 10's "spawn-a-revision"): `POST /dcrs/{id}/implement` (gate `changeRequest.implement`, already-seeded) drives the vault action **atomically by construction** ‚Äî REVISE releases the target's Approved revision / CREATE releases the authored `resulting_version_id` / RETIRE obsoletes ‚Äî by setting the version's `effective_from` (`proposed_effective_from` or now) + the cross-FK link + flip‚ÜíImplemented in ONE commit, then the EXISTING `release_due` Beat sweep performs the SERIALIZABLE single-Effective cutover (DCR-driven release = system-attributed; **no `_cutover` change, no new reaper**); RETIRE folds the flip into `lifecycle.obsolete`'s own commit. **No DCR side-door past document control**: the implement endpoint ALSO `enforce`s `document.release` (REVISE/CREATE, full SoD-2 overlay ‚Äî the PDP keys SoD on `document.release`, so a hand-rolled check would skip the approver-side leg) / `document.obsolete` (RETIRE) IN ADDITION to `changeRequest.implement` ‚Äî so a revision's author cannot self-implement (403 `sod_violation`). Shared `enrich_release_sod_scope` (extracted from `documents.py::_release_scope`) is reused by both the direct release endpoint + the implement path. `POST /dcrs/{id}/close` (gate `changeRequest.close`): Implemented‚ÜíClosed requires the change actually-effective (¬ß5.5; 409 `dcr_effectivity_pending`). **The ¬ß7.3 obsoletion gate moves to the SHARED `lifecycle.obsolete()`** ‚Äî BOTH the direct `POST /documents/{id}/obsolete` AND the DCR RETIRE-implement now 409 `obsoletion_blocked` on a coverage gap unless `force_retire` + `override_justification` (recorded on the signature intent + audit), **superseding the S-dcr-2 addendum** (no bypass; T11-only). The ¬ß7.3 reads + `evaluate_obsoletion` centralized in NEW `services/vault/obsoletion.py` (the where-used advisory consumes the same fn ‚Äî gate + advisory can't diverge; dcr‚Üívault, no cycle; `sole_star_coverage` moved out of `dcr_repo`). **CAPA‚ÜíDCR loop = dedicated `POST /capas/{id}/raise-dcr`** (gate `changeRequest.create`; `raise_dcr_from_capa` ‚Üí `raise_dcr(_commit=False, source_link_type=capa)`): **1:N** (a CAPA may spawn child DCRs ‚Äî NO latch), an `Idempotency-Key` (NEW `dcr.spawn_idempotency_key` partial-UNIQUE) makes a retry return the same DCR (201 new / 200 replay); a terminal CAPA ‚Üí 409 `capa_terminal`. **The deferred cross-FK** `document_version.dcr_id` ‚Üî `dcr.resulting_version_id` lands (`use_alter` 2-table cycle, both named FKs via `op.create_foreign_key`, the `capa.origin_finding_id`‚Üî`audit_finding` precedent). Mig `0044` = the cross-FK pair + `spawn_idempotency_key` + its partial-UNIQUE (excluded in `env.py`) + the `changeRequest.implement` grant-backfill (Process Owner + QMS Owner). NO new permission key (R5) / event type (reuse `DCR_TRANSITIONED`) / enum value (`Implemented`/`Closed` exist since 0040) / Celery task.

**The DCR family (doc 05, the Revision & Change Depth family) is now COMPLETE ‚úÖ.** Deferred to the v1.x drift family: scheduled re-review (D5) + drift detection (D1‚ÄìD4).

## v1 WEB UI track (apps/web ‚Äî React 18 + Mantine 7 SPA) ‚Äî STARTED

The SPA was MVP-deferred to just the setup wizard + admin stubs while the API matured. This track ports the owner-approved mockup (`mockup/easysynq-mockup.html`, 8 screens; `styles.css` = 722 design tokens) into the live app as a **vertical operational journey** (UJ-3 review‚Üíapprove) in 3 slices. Stack: React 18 + Mantine 7 + TanStack Query 5 + react-router 7 + Tailwind 3; tests are **stack-free** via vitest + @testing-library/react + **MSW** + **jest-axe** (the web CI job now also runs `npm test`). WCAG 2.2 AA is a release gate (jest-axe + eslint-jsx-a11y). Spec + plan: `docs/superpowers/{specs,plans}/2026-06-06-*`.

- **S-web-1** app shell + design-system foundation (**front-end only ‚Äî NO migration**) ‚Äî the single-source **token port** (`mockup/styles.css` `--es-*` ‚Üí `src/theme/tokens.css`, consumed by BOTH the Mantine theme [system fonts, indigo primary] AND Tailwind; the mockup's `[data-theme="dark"]` re-keyed to `:root[data-mantine-color-scheme="dark"]`); the **app shell** on Mantine `AppShell` (TopBar [disabled ‚åòK slot, task/ack bells, user-menu logout] ¬∑ LeftRail [PLAN/DO/CHECK/ACT clause spine from `GET /clauses` + Home/Library] ¬∑ Breadcrumb ¬∑ a deep-linkable `?detail=` resizable focus-trapped **DetailDrawer** ¬∑ skip-link [zIndex above the header ‚Äî WCAG 2.2 Focus-Not-Obscured] + ARIA landmarks); an **AuthProvider** context + a token-aware **`useApi()`** client + React Query hooks (`useDocuments`, `useClauses`); **routing** = `AppShell` at `/` (Home index + `/library` live; `/documents/:id` + `/tasks/:id` reserved; `/setup` + `/admin` unchanged); a **thin Library list** from `GET /documents` (Identifier ¬∑ Title ¬∑ State badge ¬∑ Clause chips ‚Äî friendly type/owner deferred [the list endpoint returns only IDs] + no next-review column [`next_review_due` doesn't exist until the drift family]); a calm **Home placeholder** (full PDCA dashboard = a later slice). 12 vitest tests incl. axe; lint/typecheck/build/test all green. Method: brainstorm (visual companion) ‚Üí owner forks (vertical journey ¬∑ 3-slice plan) ‚Üí spec+plan ‚Üí subagent-driven TDD with per-logic-task spec+quality review (caught & fixed pre-merge: a `render.tsx` task-ordering bug, the Task-5/6 `StateBadge`‚Üî`DocumentDrawer` import cycle, an `api.ts` import-placement nit, the LibraryPage deep-link empty-shell flash, and a skip-link z-index a11y bug) ‚Üí whole-branch review **READY TO MERGE**.

`require("document.read")` resolves at SYSTEM scope ‚Üí would exclude ordinary readers), the directory returns **`{id, display_name}` ONLY** (minimal disclosure, ACTIVE non-guest); `GET /documents` gains a **`{data, page}` pagination envelope** with `offset` (**authz-correct**: scan a bounded candidate window ‚Üí per-row `document.read` filter ‚Üí in-memory slice + derived `has_more`, NOT a pre-authz SQL OFFSET; - **S-web-4b** the worker-async **visual page-image diff viewer** ‚Äî the doc 11 ¬ß4.7 Side-by-side / page-image mode S-web-4 deferred (**front-end only; NO migration [head stays `0044`], NO new permission key, NO `openapi.yaml` change** ‚Äî the worker-async backend trio was already built + contracted in **S-dcr-3b**). Owner forks (3): **D-A** layer UX = a **single image pane + a Before/After/Diff toggle** (default Diff = the server-composed overlay), rendered via the **authed `fetch ‚Üí blob ‚Üí objectURL ‚Üí <img>`** path ‚Äî the page-PNG endpoint is **authenticated, NOT presigned**, so a bare `<img src>` would 403 (NOT side-by-side synced-scroll ‚Äî PDF.js is out of the track per S-web-4 D-C; NOT onion-skin/canvas); **D-B** the **Text | Visual `SegmentedControl` lives in `VersionCompare`**, swapping the **byte-identical** S-web-4 `RedlineViewer` (Text) and a new `VisualDiffViewer` (Visual) as siblings ‚Äî URL-driven `?mode=visual`, reusing the same `?from=&to=` pair; **D-C** the **full** viewer (the ¬ß4.7/¬ß6.2 bar), not a minimal single-layer image. **The worker-async contract** (`useVisualDiff`, the S-dcr-3b "POST-compute / pure-GET-poll / stream a page sub-resource" shape): a **POST trigger** (idempotent ‚Äî UPSERTs the cache row + enqueues only while Pending) seeds the poll cache so the **GET poll** never races the 404-before-request, and `refetchInterval` runs **only while `status==="Pending"`** and halts at any terminal status (the `SetupWizard` precedent); a terminal POST never fires a redundant GET. **`VisualDiffViewer`** (`features/document/`): the single image pane (a new **`apiGetBlob`/`useApi().getBlob`** authed-binary helper ‚Äî the **only** API-proxied binary in the SPA, every other download is a presigned URL ‚Äî fetches each page+layer PNG ‚Üí `objectURL`, **revoked** on every page/layer change + unmount, no leak) + a **changed-page rail** (the ¬ß4.7 minimap AND the ¬ß6.2 screen-reader change index, driven by `pages[].changed` with a **non-color** glyph + textual "changed") + the Before/After/Diff toggle + **`n`/`p`** next/previous-changed-page nav + a phased **¬ß4.9 long-op** poll (skeletons matching final layout, an `aria-live` region, a manual "Re-request render" for the dev renderer-off "Pending forever" case ‚Äî never a frozen UI). **Calm terminal states** (not errors): `Unavailable` (a non-renderable R26 version) ‚Üí a source-download fallback; a page-endpoint **404** ("No image for this page/layer" ‚Äî an added page's Before / a removed page's After) ‚Üí a per-side note; `Failed` ‚Üí a calm terminal with the same source-download fallback (**NOT re-drivable** ‚Äî `get_or_create_visual_diff` re-enqueues only a `Pending` row, so the viewer offers **no dead Retry** on a terminal Failed; the re-request affordance lives on `Pending` only, for the dev renderer-off case); **403 ‚Üí quiet** (DP-6). **The hook is keyed by the pair** ‚Äî `status` is read from the pair-keyed poll cache (seeded by the POST), so changing versions never flashes the prior pair's pages or fires page requests for a not-yet-requested diff; the viewer resets the selected page on a pair change. **0-based** `pages[].page`, labelled 1-based in the UI. **Honest v1 caveat surfaced in-copy:** the watermarked rendition's footer band differs by revision ‚Üí a near-universal "changed" footer region (raw render = v1.x). **Tests:** **+26 web** across `useVisualDiff` (POST-then-poll‚ÜíReady, terminal-without-redundant-GET, Failed/Unavailable/403, `retry()` re-POST), `VisualDiffViewer` (authed page fetch + alt + objectURL, the layer toggle re-fetching `?layer=`, the 404 no-image + non-404 error branches, `n`/`p`, the objectURL **revoke-on-change**, Pending/Failed/Unavailable/403), and `VersionCompare` (the Text|Visual switch + `?mode=` deep-link, RedlineViewer unchanged) ‚Äî **jest-axe `toHaveNoViolations` release gate** on `VisualDiffViewer` (each state) + `VersionCompare` (both modes); the full web suite stays green (`RedlineViewer.test.tsx` byte-identical). Method: spec+plan (`docs/superpowers/.../2026-06-08-*s-web-4b*`) ‚Üí TDD ‚Üí **diff-critic = CLEAN** (2 minor coverage gaps folded: the objectURL revoke + the non-404 image-error branch). Live: the 3 visual-diff routes confirmed **mounted on the running api** (401 vs a 404 control); the full visual click-through needs a 2-version Effective doc (the dev vault has none) + a real render (renderer/worker up). **Next:** S-web-5 (Review & Approve ‚Äî closes UJ-3).

- **S-web-5** Review & Approve ‚Äî **CLOSES UJ-3** (author ‚Üí review ‚Üí approve ‚Üí release) (**full-stack but thin: ONE migration-free read endpoint, NO migration [head stays `0044`], NO new permission key**; every write [`submit-review`, `POST /tasks/{id}/decision`, `release`] + most reads [`GET /tasks`, `/tasks/{id}`, `/workflow-instances/{id}`, the per-doc `capabilities`, the redline] were already contracted + implemented). New repo helper `latest_instance_for_subject` = **latest, ANY state** (NOT `find_nonterminal_instance`): `lifecycle.release` never closes the instance (it lingers `APPROVED` for an Effective doc ‚Äî which the stepper *wants* to show) and a `NEEDS_ATTENTION` empty-pool instance must still surface. Gate + serializer reuse `get_instance_endpoint` verbatim (the closed catalog has **no `task.*`/`workflow.*` key** ‚Äî `document.read` on the subject is the real-world gate). 5 integration tests (instance+tasks / null-never-submitted / 404-unknown / 403-no-read / latest-returns-the-decided-APPROVED-instance; the empty-pool NEEDS_ATTENTION case isn't isolable in the shared-DB integration suite ‚Äî other tests' org-wide Approver grants populate the pool ‚Äî so it rides code review). **Front-end** (new `features/review/` + doc-side additions in `features/document/`, dep direction `review ‚Üí document ‚Üí lib`, acyclic): a `/tasks` **TasksInbox** (self-scoped `GET /tasks`; task/stage/state/due + link ‚Äî the per-row Document column deferred, it'd N+1 instance‚Üídoc; shown on the review page instead), a per-task **ReviewApprovePage** (task ‚Üí instance ‚Üí subject doc ‚Üí the **reused `VersionCompare`/redline** + the **`DecisionCard`** for a PENDING task; a DONE task shows a read-only "Decided"), the **`DecisionCard`** (Approve / Request-changes / Reject radiogroup; comment **conditional-required** for changes/reject [`aria-describedby` rule]; a DP-10 **signature slot** [a "meaning = approval" confirm checkbox + the honest "v1 ‚Äî single-factor logged confirmation"]; 403 `sod_violation`/409-already-decided/`step_up_required` all rendered **calmly**; a per-mount `crypto.randomUUID()` **Idempotency-Key** so a retry replays not 409s), an **`ApprovalStepper`** (`features/document/`; the doc-11 ¬ß4.4 vertical stepper, **derives nodes from the instance + tasks + the doc's own state** ‚Äî submit / quality-approval [current/done/rejected per task+instance] / release-to-effective [from the doc `Effective`/`effective_from`, authoritative] ‚Äî **non-color** glyph+label DP-7, `aria-current="step"`; renders the *actual* single stage, NOT the mockup's aspirational multi-stage spine), the **`ApprovalsTab`** card on `DocumentDetailPage` (stepper + a `capabilities.release`+`Approved`-gated **Release** button + a candidate-only "Review & approve ‚Üí" deep-link), a **`TaskStateBadge`** (DP-7), and the hooks (`useDocumentApproval`, `useTasks`/`useTask`/`useWorkflowInstance`/`useDecideTask`, `useReleaseDocument`, `useMe`). `lib/api.ts` gains an optional `headers` arg on `send` (the Idempotency-Key path, backward-compatible); `App.tsx` swaps the `tasks/:id` `Reserved` stub for the real `/tasks` + `/tasks/:id` routes; `LeftRail` adds the "Review & Approve" nav. **Tests:** 5 api integration (CI/Linux gate ‚Äî see the Windows note below) + **+28 web** (vitest+MSW+jest-axe across the hooks, stepper node-derivation per state, DecisionCard conditional-comment/SoD-403/a11y, inbox, review page, the doc-page card; the full suite = **132 web tests** green). Method: 7-agent exploration ‚Üí owner forks (4 decisions) ‚Üí spec+plan (`docs/superpowers/.../2026-06-08-*s-web-5*`) ‚Üí TDD ‚Üí **diff-critic = 1 CRITICAL, fixed + regression-tested**: `ApprovalsTab` gated the approve CTA on `user.profile.sub` (the OIDC **Keycloak subject**) vs `candidate_pool`/`assignee_user_id`, which are **`app_user.id` UUIDs** ‚Äî a *different* identifier in production, so the "Review & approve" link would never render for the real approver; **the fixtures had collapsed `sub == /me.id == candidate_pool[0]` (a textbook false-PASS).** Fix = a new `useMe()` (`GET /me` ‚Üí `app_user.id`), gate on `me.id`, + a regression test with `sub ‚âÝ me.id`. **‚öÝ The full create‚Üíapprove‚Üírelease loop needs 3 DISTINCT users** (SoD-1/2 non-overridable): the `priya`/`ken`/`mara` `just seed-personas` fixture. **Live smoke (DONE ‚Äî full 3-persona loop in the browser):** priya authored SOP-PUR-002 (Rev A, clause 8.4) ‚Üí submit-review; **ken** saw it in the new `/tasks` inbox ‚Üí Review & Approve page ‚Üí Approve (+ the DP-10 signature confirm) ‚Üí Approved; **mara** opened the doc page ‚Üí the Approvals stepper (Submitted ‚úì / Approved by Ken ‚úì / Released ‚óâ) ‚Üí **Release** ‚Üí **Effective**. The `/me.id` fix was genuinely exercised (ken's app_user id was in the candidate pool; his Keycloak `sub` was not). Two **fixture** gaps surfaced + fixed for the demo: the seeded author lacked **`clauseMap.read`** (added to `seed_personas._AUTHOR_KEYS`, the UI clause picker needs it) and the seeded Keycloak users lacked an email/name profile (set via `kcadm` to clear the VERIFY_PROFILE required action ‚Äî a one-time dev step, not code). Browser-automation note for next time: in-memory tokens mean **full navigations re-auth to `/`** (move via client-side nav). **Browser presigned upload/download fix (post-smoke, now verified live ‚Äî real browser PUT ‚Üí 200):** two parts were needed ‚Äî (1) `S3_PUBLIC_ENDPOINT=http://localhost:9000` so the presign targets a browser-reachable host (the #90 setting; it was empty), AND (2) the SPA CSP **`connect-src`** must include that object-store origin ‚Äî `connect-src 'self'` alone blocked the direct browser‚ÜíMinIO call (a gap #90 missed). Fixed generally: the Caddyfile CSP is now `connect-src 'self' {$S3_PUBLIC_ENDPOINT}` (templated; the `proxy` service gets `S3_PUBLIC_ENDPOINT` from `.env`), so browser presigned upload/download works in dev (localhost:9000) and prod alike (set the public object-store host; empty when it's same-origin behind Caddy). `S3_PUBLIC_ENDPOINT` now **defaults to `http://localhost:9000` in `.env.example`** (and `install.sh` `cp`s that, so a fresh clone gets in-app upload/download working out of the box); the live value lives in the gitignored `.env`. Both browser paths verified live: presigned PUT ‚Üí 200 + check-in 201; controlled-copy download ‚Üí a 15.9 KB watermarked PDF (application/pdf) ‚Üí 200 through the CSP.

The **`/search?q=` results page** (`SearchResultsPage`, URL-driven via `useSearchParams`) = `useSearch` ranked rows (`SearchResultRow`: identifier ¬∑ title‚Üí`/documents/:id` ¬∑ reused `StateBadge` ¬∑ clause chips‚Üí`/library?clause=N` ¬∑ the **XSS-safe `Snippet`** ‚Äî splits PostgreSQL `ts_headline`'s literal `<b>‚Ä¶</b>` into `<Mark>`, renders every other segment as a React **text node**, **NO `dangerouslySetInnerHTML`** [a `<script>` in a title renders as literal text]) + the **`hidden_by_scope` footer** ("N hidden by your access scope") + an **honesty hint** ("title/identifier/clause refs ‚Äî Effective documents only") + **calm** empty/no-results/**error** states (search **filters, never 403s**). **Compliance surface** (`features/compliance/`): a dedicated **`/compliance`** route + a **`LeftRail` entry gated on `usePermissions().can("report.compliance_checklist.read")`** (hidden unless held ‚Äî the SYSTEM key sits with QMS Owner + Internal Auditor, **not** the demo admin; `useComplianceChecklist` surfaces a **`forbidden`** flag from `ApiError.status===403`+`retry:false` ‚Üí a **calm no-access panel**, not a crash); the page = a **RAG rollup** (a **non-color** glyph+label+count legend ‚Äî `‚úì Covered / ‚óî Partial / ‚úï Gap`, *not* badges, to avoid a duplicate-`aria-label` clash with the table) + the **20‚òÖ clause `Table`** (`CoverageBadge` COVERED/PARTIAL/GAP, **DP-7** glyph+label) with each clause row ‚Üí `/library?clause=N` (the doc-13 ¬ß3.1 drill-through; reuses the existing Library clause filter). **Tests:** **+30 web** (vitest + MSW + jest-axe) across the hooks (`useSearch`/`useSuggest` enabled-guards ¬∑ `useComplianceChecklist` success+403), the **XSS-safe `Snippet`** (incl. a `<script>`-as-text guard), the `CommandPalette` (suggest‚Üídoc nav ¬∑ footer‚Üí`/search` ¬∑ Enter ¬∑ **axe**), the `SearchResultsPage` (URL-driven ¬∑ `hidden_by_scope` ¬∑ no-results ¬∑ **error** ¬∑ axe), `CoverageBadge`, the `CompliancePage` (rollup ¬∑ drill-through href ¬∑ **403-calm** ¬∑ axe rows+403), the **gated nav** (shown/hidden by `/me/permissions`), the shell wiring (‚åòK + click open the palette), and the `/search`+`/compliance` routes ‚Äî the full suite = **162 web tests** green (lint + tsc-strict + build all clean; tsc caught a `noUncheckedIndexedAccess` nit the per-task vitest runs missed).
